358    /**
359     * acceptTrade(TradeReportStruct externalTradeStruct) Gets the BT/EFP information from the param
360     * Calls the createTrade() method which creates and persists the trade, and publishes for CTM
361     * and SIAC?? returns the TradeReportStruct, with the tradeId populated.
362     * 
363     * @param externalTradeStruct Information about the Block Trade, or EFP Trade entered by the
364     * Help Desk
365 * @exception   SystemException -       Thrown by createTrade()
366 * @exception   CommunicationException - May be thrown by isValid()
367 * @exception   AuthorizationException - -same-
368     * @exception DataValidationException - if the product being traded Product not found for given
369     * productKey
370     * @exception NotAcceptedException - if the trade being accepted is a REGULAR_TRADE, or if the
371     * product being traded is a strategy
372     * @exception TransactionFailedException - if the attempt to persist fails for any reason ?? the
373     * method used by Manual stock trade report was overwritten in TradeServiceStockImpl
374     */
375 
376    public TradeReportStruct acceptTrade(TradeReportStruct externalTradeStruct)
377            throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException,
378            DataValidationException, NotAcceptedException, TransactionFailedException
379{
380    TradeReportStructV2 theTrade = doPreProcess(externalTradeStruct);
381    TradeReportStructV2 acceptedTrade = acceptTradeV2(theTrade);
382    return acceptedTrade.tradeReport;
383}
384 
385private TradeReportStructV2 doPreProcess(TradeReportStruct externalTradeStruct)
386{
387        if (Log.isDebugOn())
388        {
389            Log.debug(this, "In " + getClass().getName() + ".acceptTrade");
390    }
391    TradeReportStructV2 theTrade = new TradeReportStructV2();
392        // set the default current trade setllement date as today, and set transaction time with
393        // current time
394        theTrade.settlementTradeReport = com.cboe.domain.util.StructBuilder
395                .buildDefaultTradeReportSettlement();
396    theTrade.tradeReport = externalTradeStruct;
397    return theTrade;
398}
399 
400    public TradeReportStruct acceptTradeWithClearingType(TradeReportStruct externalTrade,
401            boolean isParTrade, char tradedSide, AtomicCmtaAllocationStruct[] atomicCmtaAllocations)
402            throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException,
403            DataValidationException, NotAcceptedException, TransactionFailedException
404    {
405        testARException(externalTrade, tradedSide);
406        TradeReportStructV2 theTrade = doPreProcess(externalTrade);
407        short handlingInstructions = TradeReportHandlingInstructions.REGULAR;
408        
409        TradeReportStructV2 acceptedTrade = acceptTradeV2(theTrade, handlingInstructions,
410                isParTrade, tradedSide, atomicCmtaAllocations);
411 
412        if (isParTrade)
413        { /* The par trade has to be TradeSources.PAR */
414            // this is for manual trade only.
415            acceptedTrade.tradeReport.tradeSource = TradeSources.PAR;
416        }
417        
418        return acceptedTrade.tradeReport;
419    }

421    public TradeReportStruct acceptTradeWithClearingType(TradeReportStruct externalTrade,
422            boolean isParTrade, char tradedSide,
423            AtomicCmtaAllocationStruct[] atomicCmtaAllocations, char[] clearingTypes,
424            boolean sweepTrade) throws SystemException, CommunicationException,
425            AuthorizationException, DataValidationException, NotAcceptedException,
426            TransactionFailedException
427    {
428        testARException(externalTrade, tradedSide);
429        TradeReportStructV2 theTrade = doPreProcess(externalTrade);
430        short handlingInstructions = TradeReportHandlingInstructions.REGULAR;
431 
432        TradeReportStructV2 acceptedTrade = acceptTradeV2(theTrade, handlingInstructions,
433                isParTrade, tradedSide, atomicCmtaAllocations, clearingTypes, sweepTrade);
434 
435        if (isParTrade)
436        { /* The par trade has to be TradeSources.PAR */
437            // this is for manual trade only.
438            acceptedTrade.tradeReport.tradeSource = TradeSources.PAR;
439        }
440 
441        return acceptedTrade.tradeReport;
442    }

444    private TradeReport acceptManualTradeWithClearingType(TradeReportStruct externalTrade,
445            boolean isParTrade, char tradedSide, AtomicCmtaAllocationStruct[] atomicCmtaAllocations, char [] clearingTypes, boolean sweepTrade, boolean turnOffPersistent)
446            throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException,
447            DataValidationException, NotAcceptedException, TransactionFailedException
448    {
449        testARException(externalTrade, tradedSide);
450        TradeReportStructV2 theTrade = doPreProcess(externalTrade);
451        short handlingInstructions = TradeReportHandlingInstructions.REGULAR;
452 
453        TradeReport acceptedTrade = acceptManualTradeV2(theTrade, handlingInstructions,
454                isParTrade, tradedSide, atomicCmtaAllocations, clearingTypes, sweepTrade, turnOffPersistent);
455 
456        if (isParTrade)
457        { /* The par trade has to be TradeSources.PAR */
458            // this is for manual trade only.
459            ((TradeReportImpl)acceptedTrade).setTradeSource(TradeSources.PAR);
460        }
461 
462        return acceptedTrade;
463    }
464    
465    private boolean isParentProduct(int productKey)
466    {
467        boolean isParentProduct = false;
468        ProductData prodData;
469        try
470        {
471            prodData = getProductDataCacheHome().find().getProductData(productKey);
472            isParentProduct = prodData.isStrategy();
473        }
474        catch (Exception e)
475        {
476            // This shouldn't really happen. So for now, let's just swallow the 
477            // exception and move on.
478            Log.information("Encountered exception while attempting to confirm whetherOther product is strategy-product/");
479        }        
480        return isParentProduct;
481    }
482    
483    public TradeReportStruct[] acceptManualTrade(ManualTradeReportStruct p_externalTrade,
484            boolean sweepTrade) throws SystemException, CommunicationException,
485            AuthorizationException, DataValidationException, NotAcceptedException,
486            TransactionFailedException
487    {
488        ClearingTradeReportStruct [] trades = p_externalTrade.tradeReports;
489        List<TradeReport> tradeReports = new ArrayList<TradeReport>(trades.length);
490        TradeReport parentTradeReport = null;
491        boolean isStrategyTraded = false;
492        for (int i = 0; i < trades.length; i++)
493        {
494            TradeReport theReport = acceptManualTradeWithClearingType(trades[i].tradeReport, trades[i].isParTrade, trades[i].tradedSide, trades[i].atomicCmtaAllocations, 
495                    trades[i].manualReportTypes, sweepTrade, true);
496            tradeReports.add(theReport);
497            if (isParentProduct(trades[i].tradeReport.productKey)) {
498                parentTradeReport = theReport;
499                isStrategyTraded = true;
500            }
501        }
502        if (isStrategyTraded && parentTradeReport != null)
503        {
504            assignParentReport(tradeReports, parentTradeReport);
505        }
506        TradeReportStruct[] theReturnedStruct = new TradeReportStruct[tradeReports.size()];
507        int j = 0;
508        for (TradeReport theReport : tradeReports) {
509            theReturnedStruct[j++] = theReport.toStruct(true);
510        }
511        return theReturnedStruct;
512    }
513 
514    private void assignParentReport(List<TradeReport> acceptedTrades, TradeReport parentTradeReport)
515    {
516        if (parentTradeReport == null) {
517            Log.debug(this, "Unable to assign the Parent trade report - " + parentTradeReport.getTradeId());
518        }
519        Transaction.startTransaction();
520        for (TradeReport theReport : acceptedTrades) {
521            long theTradeId = theReport.getTradeId();
522            if (theTradeId != parentTradeReport.getTradeId()) {
523               ((TradeReportImpl)theReport).setParentReport(parentTradeReport);
524            }
525        }
526        Transaction.commit();
527    }
528    /**
529     * Create a trade for the linkage order filled for underlying order as result of Auto Link to
530     * away exchange.
531     */
532    public long createTradeForLinkageFill(OrderStruct underlyingOrder,
533            FilledReportStruct fillReport, OrderStruct linkageOrderStruct,
534            DateTimeStruct transactionTime, String p_executingBroker)
535                                            throws  DataValidationException, SystemException
536    {
537            long tradeDbId = 0;
538            
539        if(Log.isDebugOn())
540        {
541            Log.debug(this, "In " + getClass().getName()+ ".createTradeForLinkageFill");
542        }
543        boolean sweepNReturnTrade = false;
544        if(p_executingBroker != null && p_executingBroker.trim().length() > 0)
545            sweepNReturnTrade = true;
546        TradeReportStruct tradeReportStruct = getTradeReport(fillReport, underlyingOrder,
547                linkageOrderStruct, transactionTime, p_executingBroker);
548        AtomicCmtaAllocationStruct[] atomicCmtaAllocations = getAtomicCmtaAllocations(
549                tradeReportStruct, underlyingOrder, linkageOrderStruct, fillReport);
550 
551        String outboundVendor = getOutbounVendorsForAutoLinkTrades(linkageOrderStruct);
552        
553        TradeReportStructV2 theTrade = doPreProcess(tradeReportStruct);
554        Price price = PriceFactory.create(theTrade.tradeReport.price);
555        TradingProduct product;
556        try
557        {
558            product = getTradingProductHome().findByKey(theTrade.tradeReport.productKey);
559        }
560        catch (NotFoundException e)
561        {
562            // this was already validated in isValidTrade
563            String message = "Unable to access trading prodcut for product key "
564                    + theTrade.tradeReport.productKey;
565            Log.exception(this, message, e);
566            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(message,
567                    DataValidationCodes.INVALID_PRODUCT);
568        }
569 
570        if (Log.isDebugOn())
571        {
572            Log.debug(this, "TradeServiceImpl.createTrade creating a manual trade...");
573        }
574 
575        TradeReportImpl tradeReport = (TradeReportImpl) getTradeReportHome().create(product,
576                theTrade.tradeReport.quantity, price, theTrade, getMyIdService(),
577                                                              atomicCmtaAllocations, outboundVendor, sweepNReturnTrade);
578 
579        tradeDbId = tradeReport.getObjectIdentifierAsLong();
580        
581        logAfterTradeReportCreation(product, theTrade.tradeReport.quantity, price,
582                TradeReportHandlingInstructions.REGULAR, theTrade, tradeReport);
583        
584        return tradeDbId;
585    }

587        // NOL use for generating Trade Report
588    private TradeReportStruct getTradeReport(FilledReportStruct fillReport,
589            OrderStruct underlyingOrderStruct, OrderStruct linkageOrderStruct,
590            DateTimeStruct transactionTime, String executingBroker)
591    {
592        TradeReportStruct tradeReport = TradeReportStructBuilder.buildTradeReportStruct();
593        // populate tradereport from fillreportstruct.
594        
595        tradeReport.tradeSource = TradeSources.SYSTEM;
596        tradeReport.tradeType = TradeTypes.NO_PRINT_LINKAGE_TRADE;
597        tradeReport.sessionName = underlyingOrderStruct.activeSession;
598        tradeReport.productKey = underlyingOrderStruct.productKey;
599        tradeReport.quantity = fillReport.tradedQuantity;
600        tradeReport.price = fillReport.price;
601        tradeReport.businessDate = new DateWrapper(TradingSessionNameHelper
602                .getSession(fillReport.sessionName).businessDay).toDateStruct();
603        long transTimeInMillis = DateWrapper.convertToMillis(transactionTime);
604        tradeReport.timeTraded.date = DateWrapper.convertToDate(transTimeInMillis);
605        tradeReport.timeTraded.time = DateWrapper.convertToTime(transTimeInMillis);
606 
607        ArrayList<AtomicTradeStruct> atomicTradeStructList = new ArrayList<AtomicTradeStruct>();
608        atomicTradeStructList = populateAtomicTrade(fillReport, underlyingOrderStruct,
609                linkageOrderStruct, executingBroker);
610 
611        if(atomicTradeStructList.size() > 0)
612        {
613            tradeReport.parties = new AtomicTradeStruct[atomicTradeStructList.size()];
614            tradeReport.parties = atomicTradeStructList
615                    .toArray(new AtomicTradeStruct[atomicTradeStructList.size()]);
616        }
617 
618        return tradeReport;
619    }

621    private String getOutbounVendorsForAutoLinkTrades(OrderStruct linkageOrderStruct)
622    {
623        String extensions = linkageOrderStruct.extensions;
624        String outboundVendor = "";
625 
626        if (extensions !=null) 
627        {
628            try 
629            {
630                ExtensionsHelper extensionHelper = new ExtensionsHelper(extensions);
631                outboundVendor = extensionHelper.getValue(ExtensionFields.BROKER_ROUTING_ID);
632            } 
633            catch(ParseException pe) 
634            {
635                Log.alarm("Cannot parse the Extensions - Outbound Vendor field for linkage order "
636                        + pe.getMessage());
637            }
638            
639        }
640        return outboundVendor;
641    }
642    
643    /**
644     * These are the new fields passed to Trade Report for the CMTA Allocation for manual trades per
645     * contra.
646     * 
647     * @param tradeReports
648     * @return
649     */
650    private AtomicCmtaAllocationStruct[] getAtomicCmtaAllocations(TradeReportStruct tradeReport,
651            OrderStruct anOrderStruct, OrderStruct linkageOrderStruct, FilledReportStruct fillReport)
652    {
653     
654        String awayExchange = "";
655        try
656        {
657            ExtensionsHelper extensionsHelper =  new ExtensionsHelper(fillReport.extensions);
658            awayExchange = extensionsHelper.getValue(ExtensionFields.EXCHANGE_DESTINATION);
659        }
660        catch(ParseException pe)
661        {
662        }
663 
664        AtomicCmtaAllocationStruct[] atomicCmtaAllocations = null;
665        AtomicTradeStruct[] atomicTrades = tradeReport.parties;
666        atomicCmtaAllocations = new AtomicCmtaAllocationStruct[atomicTrades.length];
667        
668        for(int i = 0; i < atomicTrades.length; i++)
669        {
670            AtomicCmtaAllocationStruct atomicCmtaAllocationStruct = AtomicCmtaAllocationStructBuilder
671                    .buildAtomicCmtaAllocationStructBuilder();
672            
673            atomicCmtaAllocationStruct.atomicTradeId = atomicTrades[i].atomicTradeId;
674            if(anOrderStruct.side == Sides.BUY)
675            {
676                atomicCmtaAllocationStruct.buyerAwayExchangeAcronym = new ExchangeAcronymStruct(
677                        awayExchange, "");
678                atomicCmtaAllocationStruct.buyerOrderDate = anOrderStruct.orderId.orderDate;
679                atomicCmtaAllocationStruct.buyerOrsid = anOrderStruct.orsId;
680                atomicCmtaAllocationStruct.buyerSupressionReason = 0;
681                
682                atomicCmtaAllocationStruct.sellerAwayExchangeAcronym = new ExchangeAcronymStruct(
683                        "", "");
684                atomicCmtaAllocationStruct.sellerOrderDate = linkageOrderStruct.orderId.orderDate;
685                atomicCmtaAllocationStruct.sellerOrsid = linkageOrderStruct.orsId;
686                atomicCmtaAllocationStruct.sellerSupressionReason = 0;
687 
688            }
689            else
690            {
691                atomicCmtaAllocationStruct.sellerAwayExchangeAcronym = new ExchangeAcronymStruct(
692                        awayExchange, "");
693                atomicCmtaAllocationStruct.sellerOrderDate = anOrderStruct.orderId.orderDate;
694                atomicCmtaAllocationStruct.sellerOrsid = anOrderStruct.orsId;
695                atomicCmtaAllocationStruct.sellerSupressionReason = 0;
696                
697                atomicCmtaAllocationStruct.buyerAwayExchangeAcronym = new ExchangeAcronymStruct("",
698                        "");
699                atomicCmtaAllocationStruct.buyerOrderDate = linkageOrderStruct.orderId.orderDate;
700                atomicCmtaAllocationStruct.buyerOrsid = linkageOrderStruct.orsId;
701                atomicCmtaAllocationStruct.buyerSupressionReason = 0;
702 
703            }
704            atomicCmtaAllocations[i] = atomicCmtaAllocationStruct;
705        }
706        return atomicCmtaAllocations;
707    }
708 
709    private ArrayList<AtomicTradeStruct> populateAtomicTrade(FilledReportStruct fillReport,
710            OrderStruct underlyingOrderStruct, OrderStruct linkageOrderStruct,
711            String executingBroker)
712    {
713        ArrayList<AtomicTradeStruct> atomicTradeStructList = new ArrayList<AtomicTradeStruct>();
714//        ContraPartyStruct[] contraBrokers = fillReport.contraParties;
715        
716        ContraPartyStruct[] contraBrokers = new ContraPartyStruct[1];
717        ContraPartyStruct contra = new ContraPartyStruct();
718        contra.firm = new ExchangeFirmStruct();
719        contra.firm.exchange = fillReport.executingOrGiveUpFirm.exchange;
720        contra.firm.firmNumber = fillReport.executingOrGiveUpFirm.firmNumber;
721        contra.user = new ExchangeAcronymStruct();
722        contra.user.acronym = defaultLinkageContraUser.acronym;
723        contra.user.exchange = this.anonymousBrokerExchange;
724        contra.quantity = fillReport.tradedQuantity;
725        contraBrokers[0] = contra;
726        
727        String fillReportAccount = (fillReport.account.length() > 16
728                ? fillReport.account.substring(0, 15)
729                : fillReport.account);
730        String fillReportSubAccount = (fillReport.subaccount.length() > 10
731                ? fillReport.subaccount.substring(0, 9)
732                : fillReport.subaccount);
733        fillReport.account = fillReportAccount;
734        fillReport.subaccount = fillReportSubAccount;
735        
736        for(int i = 0; i < contraBrokers.length; i++)
737        {
738            int quantity = contraBrokers[i].quantity;
739            
740            if(quantity <= 0)
741            {
742                continue;
743            }
744            
745            //This checks to see if the contra for the same product exists then add the quantity
746            AtomicTradeStruct atomicTradeForcontra = checkIfContraExistsInList(contraBrokers[i],
747                                          atomicTradeStructList, underlyingOrderStruct.side);
748            
749            if(atomicTradeForcontra != null)
750            {
751                atomicTradeForcontra.quantity = atomicTradeForcontra.quantity + quantity;
752                continue;
753            }
754            
755            AtomicTradeStruct atomicTrade = TradeReportStructBuilder.buildAtomicTradeStruct();
756            atomicTrade.active = true;
757            atomicTrade.sessionName = fillReport.sessionName;
758            long time = System.currentTimeMillis();
759            atomicTrade.entryTime.date = DateWrapper.convertToDate(time);
760            atomicTrade.entryTime.time = DateWrapper.convertToTime(time);
761            atomicTrade.entryType = TradeReportEntryTypes.ADD;
762            atomicTrade.lastEntryType = TradeReportEntryTypes.ADD;
763            atomicTrade.quantity = quantity;
764            
765            if( underlyingOrderStruct.side == Sides.BUY)
766            {
767                //Underlying Order Side
768                atomicTrade.buyerAccount = underlyingOrderStruct.account;
769                if(executingBroker != null && executingBroker.trim().length() > 0)
770                {
771                    atomicTrade.buyerBroker.acronym = executingBroker;
772                }
773                else
774                {
775                    atomicTrade.buyerBroker.acronym = defaultLinkageUser.acronym;
776                }
777                atomicTrade.buyerBroker.exchange = underlyingOrderStruct.userAcronym.exchange;
778                atomicTrade.buyerCmta = underlyingOrderStruct.cmta;
779                atomicTrade.buyerCorrespondentId = underlyingOrderStruct.orderId.correspondentFirm;
780                atomicTrade.buyerFirm = underlyingOrderStruct.orderId.executingOrGiveUpFirm;
781                atomicTrade.buyerFirmBranch = underlyingOrderStruct.orderId.branch;
782                atomicTrade.buyerFirmBranchSequenceNumber = underlyingOrderStruct.orderId.branchSequenceNumber;
783                atomicTrade.buyerOptionalData = underlyingOrderStruct.optionalData;
784                atomicTrade.buyerOrderOrQuote = true;
785                atomicTrade.buyerOrderOrQuoteKey = new CboeIdStruct(
786                        underlyingOrderStruct.orderId.highCboeId,
787                        underlyingOrderStruct.orderId.lowCboeId);
788                atomicTrade.buyerOriginator = underlyingOrderStruct.originator;
789                atomicTrade.buyerPositionEffect = underlyingOrderStruct.positionEffect;
790                atomicTrade.buyerOriginType = underlyingOrderStruct.orderOriginType;
791                atomicTrade.buyerSubaccount = underlyingOrderStruct.subaccount;
792                
793                //Linkage fill Report Side
794                atomicTrade.sellerAccount = fillReport.account;
795                atomicTrade.sellerBroker.acronym = contraBrokers[i].user.acronym;
796                atomicTrade.sellerBroker.exchange = contraBrokers[i].user.exchange;
797                atomicTrade.sellerCmta = fillReport.cmta;
798                atomicTrade.sellerCorrespondentId = linkageOrderStruct.orderId.correspondentFirm;
799                atomicTrade.sellerFirm.firmNumber = contraBrokers[i].firm.firmNumber;
800                atomicTrade.sellerFirm.exchange = contraBrokers[i].firm.exchange;
801                atomicTrade.sellerFirmBranch = linkageOrderStruct.orderId.branch;
802                atomicTrade.sellerFirmBranchSequenceNumber = linkageOrderStruct.orderId.branchSequenceNumber;
803                atomicTrade.sellerOptionalData = fillReport.optionalData;
804                atomicTrade.sellerOrderOrQuote = true;
805                atomicTrade.sellerOrderOrQuoteKey = new CboeIdStruct(
806                        linkageOrderStruct.orderId.highCboeId, linkageOrderStruct.orderId.lowCboeId);
807                atomicTrade.sellerOriginator = fillReport.originator;
808                atomicTrade.sellerPositionEffect = linkageOrderStruct.positionEffect;
809                atomicTrade.sellerOriginType = linkageOrderStruct.orderOriginType;
810                atomicTrade.sellerSubaccount = fillReport.subaccount;
811            }
812            else
813            {
814                //Underlying Order
815                atomicTrade.sellerAccount = underlyingOrderStruct.account;
816                if(executingBroker != null && executingBroker.trim().length() > 0)
817                {
818                    atomicTrade.sellerBroker.acronym = executingBroker;
819                }
820                else
821                {
822                    atomicTrade.sellerBroker.acronym = defaultLinkageUser.acronym;
823                }
824                atomicTrade.sellerBroker.exchange = underlyingOrderStruct.userAcronym.exchange;
825                atomicTrade.sellerCmta = underlyingOrderStruct.cmta;
826                atomicTrade.sellerCorrespondentId = underlyingOrderStruct.orderId.correspondentFirm;
827                atomicTrade.sellerFirm = underlyingOrderStruct.orderId.executingOrGiveUpFirm;
828                atomicTrade.sellerFirmBranch = underlyingOrderStruct.orderId.branch;
829                atomicTrade.sellerFirmBranchSequenceNumber = underlyingOrderStruct.orderId.branchSequenceNumber;
830                atomicTrade.sellerOptionalData = underlyingOrderStruct.optionalData;
831                atomicTrade.sellerOrderOrQuote = true;
832                atomicTrade.sellerOrderOrQuoteKey = new CboeIdStruct(
833                        underlyingOrderStruct.orderId.highCboeId,
834                        underlyingOrderStruct.orderId.lowCboeId);
835                atomicTrade.sellerOriginator = underlyingOrderStruct.originator;
836                atomicTrade.sellerPositionEffect = underlyingOrderStruct.positionEffect;
837                atomicTrade.sellerOriginType = underlyingOrderStruct.orderOriginType;
838                atomicTrade.sellerSubaccount = underlyingOrderStruct.subaccount;
839                
840                //Linkage side 
841                atomicTrade.buyerAccount = fillReport.account;
842                atomicTrade.buyerBroker.exchange = contraBrokers[i].user.exchange;
843                atomicTrade.buyerBroker.acronym = contraBrokers[i].user.acronym;
844                atomicTrade.buyerCmta = fillReport.cmta;
845                atomicTrade.buyerCorrespondentId = linkageOrderStruct.orderId.correspondentFirm;
846                atomicTrade.buyerFirm.exchange = contraBrokers[i].firm.exchange;
847                atomicTrade.buyerFirm.firmNumber = contraBrokers[i].firm.firmNumber;
848                atomicTrade.buyerFirmBranch = linkageOrderStruct.orderId.branch;
849                atomicTrade.buyerFirmBranchSequenceNumber = linkageOrderStruct.orderId.branchSequenceNumber;
850                atomicTrade.buyerOptionalData = fillReport.optionalData;
851                atomicTrade.buyerOrderOrQuote = true;
852                atomicTrade.buyerOrderOrQuoteKey = new CboeIdStruct(
853                        linkageOrderStruct.orderId.highCboeId, linkageOrderStruct.orderId.lowCboeId);
854                atomicTrade.buyerOriginator = fillReport.originator;
855                atomicTrade.buyerPositionEffect = linkageOrderStruct.positionEffect;
856                atomicTrade.buyerOriginType = linkageOrderStruct.orderOriginType;
857                atomicTrade.buyerSubaccount = fillReport.subaccount;
858            }
859            
860            atomicTradeStructList.add(atomicTrade);
861        }
862     
863        return atomicTradeStructList;
864    }
865    
866    /**
867     * This return the Atomic trade for the contra if it exists in the list.
868     * 
869     * @param contraBroker
870     * @param atomicTradeStructList
871     * @param side
872     * @return
873     */
874    private AtomicTradeStruct checkIfContraExistsInList(ContraPartyStruct contraBroker,
875            ArrayList<AtomicTradeStruct> atomicTradeStructList, char side)
876    {
877        AtomicTradeStruct atomicTradeForContra = null;
878 
879        for(int contraIndex = 0; contraIndex < atomicTradeStructList.size(); contraIndex++)
880        {
881            AtomicTradeStruct atomicTrade = atomicTradeStructList.get(contraIndex);
882            if(side == Sides.BUY)
883            {
884                if ((atomicTrade.sellerBroker.acronym.equals(contraBroker.user.acronym))
885                        && (atomicTrade.sellerFirm.firmNumber.equals(contraBroker.firm.firmNumber)))
886                {
887                    atomicTradeForContra = atomicTrade;
888                }
889            }
890            else
891            {
892                if ((atomicTrade.buyerBroker.acronym.equals(contraBroker.user.acronym))
893                        && (atomicTrade.buyerFirm.firmNumber.equals(contraBroker.firm.firmNumber)))
894                   {
895                       atomicTradeForContra = atomicTrade;
896                   }
897            }
898        }
899 
900        return atomicTradeForContra;
901 
902    }
903    
904/**
905     * acceptTrade(TradeReportStruct externalTradeStruct) /** Crystal Chen
906     *
907     * @param trade - TradeReportStructV2
908     * @exception   com.cboe.exceptions.CommunicationException - May be thrown by isValid()
909     * @exception   AuthorizationException - -same-
910     * @exception DataValidationException - if the product being traded Product not found for given
911     * productKey
912     * @exception NotAcceptedException - if the trade being accepted is a REGULAR_TRADE, or if the
913     * product being traded is a strategy
914     * @exception TransactionFailedException - if the attempt to persist fails for any reason ?? Mei
915     * Wu 08/18/2003
916     */
917    public TradeReportStructV2 acceptTradeV2(TradeReportStructV2 trade) throws SystemException,
918            CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException,
919            NotAcceptedException, TransactionFailedException
920    {
921        if (Log.isDebugOn())
922        {
923            Log.debug(this, "In " + getClass().getName() + ".acceptTradeV2");
924        }
925        short handlingInstructions = TradeReportHandlingInstructions.REGULAR;
926        return acceptTradeV2(trade, handlingInstructions);
927    }
928 
929    public TradeReportStructV2 acceptTradeV2(TradeReportStructV2 trade, short handlingInstruction)
930            throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException,
931            DataValidationException, NotAcceptedException, TransactionFailedException
932    {
933    //  overrides passed in PC time on manual trades from SA Gui
934        for (int i = 0; i < trade.tradeReport.parties.length; i++)
935        {
936           trade.tradeReport.parties[i].entryTime.time = TimeServiceWrapper.toDateTimeStruct().time;
937        }
938        TradingProduct product = performPreTradeCreateValidation(trade, handlingInstruction, false);
939        TradeReport tradeReport = null;
940        Price price = null;
941        try
942        {
943            price = PriceFactory.create(trade.tradeReport.price);
944            if (price.isCabinetPrice())
945            {
946                                    Log.information("Cabinet Price Converted to Penny Price for the Fill Report: ");
947                // A constant for the penny would be better.
948                                    price = PriceFactory.create(0.01);
949            }
950            tradeReport = createTrade(product, trade.tradeReport.quantity, price, null,
951                    handlingInstruction, trade, null);
952        }
953        catch (SystemException e)
954        {
955            Log.exception(this, "Exception creating manual Trade Report. " + e.details.message, e);
956            throw e;
957        }
958        try
959        {
960            // execute within product lock, else delegate to class lock:
961            product.acceptCommand(new AcceptTradeCommand(trade.tradeReport.productKey, price
962                    .toStruct()), false);
963        }
964        catch (NotAcceptedException e2)
965        {
966            Log.exception(this, "AcceptTradeCommand not acccpeted for manual TradeReport : "
967                    + e2.toString(), e2);
968            throw e2;
969        }
970 
971        product.setLastTradeTradeId(tradeReport.getTradeId());
972        return tradeReport.toStructV2(true); // true - include only Active trades
973    }
974    
975    public TradeReportStructV2 acceptTradeV2(TradeReportStructV2 trade, short handlingInstruction,
976            boolean isParTrade, char tradedSide, AtomicCmtaAllocationStruct[] atomicCmtaAllocations)
977            throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException,
978            DataValidationException, NotAcceptedException, TransactionFailedException
979    {
980        if (Log.isDebugOn())
981        {
982            Log.debug(this, "In " + getClass().getName()
983                    + ".acceptTradeV2 with handling instruction");
984        }
985        TradingProduct product = performPreTradeCreateValidation(trade, handlingInstruction,
986                isParTrade);
987        TradeReport tradeReport = null;
988        Price price = null;
989        try
990        {
991            price = PriceFactory.create(trade.tradeReport.price);
992 
993            tradeReport = createTrade(product, trade.tradeReport.quantity, price,
994                    handlingInstruction, trade, isParTrade, tradedSide, atomicCmtaAllocations);
995        }
996        catch (SystemException e)
997        {
998            Log.exception(this, "Exception creating manual Trade Report. " + e.details.message, e);
999            throw e;
1000        }
1001        try
1002        {
1003            // execute within product lock, else delegate to class lock:
1004            product.acceptCommand(new AcceptTradeCommand(trade.tradeReport.productKey, price
1005                    .toStruct()), false);
1006        }
1007        catch (NotAcceptedException e2)
1008        {
1009            Log.exception(this, "AcceptTradeCommand not acccpeted for manual TradeReport : "
1010                    + e2.toString(), e2);
1011            throw e2;
1012        }
1013        product.setLastTradeTradeId(tradeReport.getTradeId());
1014        return tradeReport.toStructV2(true); // true - include only Active trades

1070    private void performPreTradeCreateValidation(TradingProduct product, TradeReportStructV2 trade,
1071            short handlingInstruction) throws NotAcceptedException, DataValidationException,
1072            AuthorizationException, CommunicationException, SystemException
1073    {
1074        if (Log.isDebugOn())
1075        {
1076            Log.debug(this, "In " + getClass().getName() + ".performPreTradeCreateValidation()");
1077        }
1078        
1079        String openSessionName = TradingSessionNameHelper.getOpenConfiguredSessionName();
1080 
1081        if (trade.tradeReport.sessionName == null || openSessionName == null
1082                || !openSessionName.equals(trade.tradeReport.sessionName))
1083        {
1084            String message = "Invalid trading session name: " + trade.tradeReport.sessionName
1085                    + ", current Open Session: " + openSessionName + " at " + getClass().getName()
1086                    + ".performPreTradeCreateValidation().";
1087            Log.alarm(this, message);
1088            throw ExceptionBuilder.notAcceptedException(message, NotAcceptedCodes.INVALID_STATE);
1089        }
1090 
1091        if (product == null)
1092        {
1093            String message = "Invalid product: "+ product + ". Product cannot be null";
1094            Log.alarm(this, message);
1095            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(message,
1096                    DataValidationCodes.INVALID_PRODUCT);
1097        }        
1098        
1099        if (handlingInstruction != TradeReportHandlingInstructions.NO_TRADEREPORT_NO_TICKER
1100                && handlingInstruction != TradeReportHandlingInstructions.NO_TICKER
1101                && handlingInstruction != TradeReportHandlingInstructions.REGULAR
1102                && handlingInstruction != TradeReportHandlingInstructions.NO_TRADEREPORT)
1103        {
1104            String message = "Invalid Handling Instruction code passed: " + handlingInstruction
1105                    + " at " + getClass().getName() + ".performPreTradeCreateValidation().";
1106            Log.information(message);
1107            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(message,
1108                    DataValidationCodes.INVALID_TRADE_REPORT_HANDLING_INSTRUCTION);
1109        }
1110 
1111        // validate the trade
1112        isValidTrade(trade, product.getProductKeys().productType);
1113    }

1115    /**
1116     * Creates the billing information for a handheld trade report. It can be extended to support
1117     * other type of trades if needed.
1118     * 
1119     * @param trade: actual trade.
1120     * @param product: product being traded.
1121     * @return array of AtomicTradeBillingStruct containing billing information.
1122     * @throws NotAcceptedException
1123     * 
1124     * @autor Francisco Ojeda
1125     */
1126    private AtomicTradeBillingStruct[] createBillingInfo(TradeReportStructV2 trade,
1127            char tradedSide, TradingProduct product) throws NotAcceptedException
1128    {
1129        if(Log.isDebugOn())
1130    {
1131        Log.debug(this, "In " + getClass().getName() + ".createBillingInfo()");
1132        }
1133 
1134        String DEFAULT_EXCHANGE_ID = " ";
1135        AtomicTradeBillingStruct[] billings = new AtomicTradeBillingStruct[trade.tradeReport.parties.length];
1136 
1137        // add to this check if method is to support other trade types in the future.
1138        if (trade.tradeReport.tradeType == TradeTypes.HANDHELD_TRADE)
1139        {
1140            for (int i = 0; i < billings.length; i++)
1141            {
1142                billings[i] = new AtomicTradeBillingStruct();
1143                billings[i].atomicTradeId = trade.tradeReport.parties[i].atomicTradeId;
1144                billings[i].buyBillingType = BillingTypeIndicators.CROSS;
1145                billings[i].sellBillingType = BillingTypeIndicators.CROSS;
1146                if (tradedSide == Sides.BUY)
1147                {
1148                    billings[i].buyerClearingType = ClearingTypes.CLEAR;
1149                    billings[i].sellerClearingType = ClearingTypes.IGNORE;
1150                }
1151                else if (tradedSide == Sides.SELL)
1152                {
1153                    billings[i].buyerClearingType = ClearingTypes.IGNORE;
1154                    billings[i].sellerClearingType = ClearingTypes.CLEAR;
1155                }
1156                else
1157                {
1158                    String message = "Cannot create billing information for trade side "
1159                            + tradedSide;
1160                    throw ExceptionBuilder.notAcceptedException(message, 0);
1161                }
1162                billings[i].buyAwayExchanges = DEFAULT_EXCHANGE_ID;
1163                billings[i].sellAwayExchanges = DEFAULT_EXCHANGE_ID;
1164            }
1165        }
1166        else
1167        {
1168            String message = "Cannot create billing information for trade type "
1169                    + trade.tradeReport.tradeType;
1170            throw ExceptionBuilder.notAcceptedException(message, 0);
1171        }
1172        return billings;
1173    }

1219    private TradingProduct performPreTradeCreateValidation(TradeReportStructV2 trade,
1220            short handlingInstruction, boolean isParTrade) throws NotAcceptedException,
1221            DataValidationException, AuthorizationException, CommunicationException,
1222            SystemException
1223    {
1224        if (Log.isDebugOn())
1225        {
1226            Log.debug(this, "in " + getClass().getName() + ".acceptTradeV2FromStruct");
1227        }
1228        String openSessionName = TradingSessionNameHelper.getOpenConfiguredSessionName();
1229 
1230        if (!isParTrade)
1231        {
1232            // this is for manual trade only.
1233            trade.tradeReport.tradeSource = TradeSources.MANUAL;
1234        }
1235        if (trade.tradeReport.sessionName == null || openSessionName == null
1236                || !openSessionName.equals(trade.tradeReport.sessionName))
1237        {
1238            String message = "Invalid trading session name: " + trade.tradeReport.sessionName
1239                    + ", current Open Session: " + openSessionName + " at " + getClass().getName()
1240                    + ".acceptTradeV2().";
1241            Log.alarm(this, message);
1242            throw ExceptionBuilder.notAcceptedException(message, NotAcceptedCodes.INVALID_STATE);
1243        }
1244 
1245        if (handlingInstruction != TradeReportHandlingInstructions.NO_TRADEREPORT_NO_TICKER
1246                && handlingInstruction != TradeReportHandlingInstructions.NO_TICKER
1247                && handlingInstruction != TradeReportHandlingInstructions.REGULAR
1248                && handlingInstruction != TradeReportHandlingInstructions.NO_TRADEREPORT)
1249        {
1250            String message = "DataValidationException thrown. Invalid Handling Instruction code in acceptTrade Code value passed="
1251                    + handlingInstruction;
1252            Log.information(message);
1253            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(message,
1254                    DataValidationCodes.INVALID_TRADE_REPORT_HANDLING_INSTRUCTION);
1255        }
1256 
1257        TradingProduct product;
1258        try
1259        {
1260            product = getTradingProductHome().findByKey(trade.tradeReport.productKey);
1261        }
1262        catch (NotFoundException e)
1263        {
1264            // this was already validated in isValidTrade
1265            String message = "Unable to access trading prodcut for product key "
1266                    + trade.tradeReport.productKey;
1267            Log.exception(this, message, e);
1268            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(message,
1269                    DataValidationCodes.INVALID_PRODUCT);
1270        }
1271 
1272        if (product == null)
1273        {
1274            String message = "Unable to access trading prodcut for product key "
1275                    + trade.tradeReport.productKey;
1276            Log.alarm(this, message);
1277            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(message,
1278                    DataValidationCodes.INVALID_PRODUCT);
1279        }
1280 
1281        if (isParTrade == false)
1282        {
1283            // validation product state condition
1284            if (!product.inTradingState())
1285            {
1286                // TODO does this rule apply to BLOCK_TRADE only or all types of manual trades?
1287                if ((TradeTypes.BLOCK_TRADE == trade.tradeReport.tradeType)
1288                        && (ProductStates.CLOSED == product.getCurrentStateCode())
1289                        && (isBlockTradeAllowedForClosedProduct(trade.tradeReport.sessionName)))
1290                {
1291                    if (Log.isDebugOn())
1292                    {
1293                        Log.debug("TradeServiceImpl: Block Trade for "
1294                                + trade.tradeReport.sessionName
1295                                + " allowed even though the Product state is Closed.");
1296                    }
1297                }
1298                else if ((TradeTypes.GWAP_TRADE == trade.tradeReport.tradeType)
1299                        && (ProductStates.CLOSED == product.getCurrentStateCode()))
1300                {
1301                    if (Log.isDebugOn())
1302                    {
1303                        Log.debug("TradeServiceImpl: GWAP Trade for "
1304                                + trade.tradeReport.sessionName
1305                                + " allowed even though the Product state is Closed.");
1306                    }    
1307                }
1308                else if ((TradeTypes.EXCHANGE_FOR_PHYSICAL == trade.tradeReport.tradeType)
1309                        && (ProductStates.CLOSED == product.getCurrentStateCode())
1310                        && (isBlockTradeAllowedForClosedProduct(trade.tradeReport.sessionName)))
1311                {
1312                    if (Log.isDebugOn())
1313                    {
1314                        Log.debug("TradeServiceImpl: EXCHANGE_FOR_PHYSICAL Trade for "
1315                                + trade.tradeReport.sessionName
1316                                + " allowed even though the Product state is Closed.");
1317                    }
1318                }
1319                else
1320                {
1321                    String message = "Unable to trade for product key "
1322                        + trade.tradeReport.productKey + ", when the product state is :("
1323                        + product.getCurrentStateCode() + ")";
1324                    Log.alarm(this, message);
1325                    throw ExceptionBuilder.notAcceptedException(message, 0);
1326                }
1327            }
1328        }
1329 
1330        // validate the trade
1331        if (!isParTrade)
1332        {
1333            isValidTrade(trade, product.getProductKeys().productType);
1334        }
1335        return product;
1336}

1414        /**
1415     * Verifies whether a given session allowes block trades for product in CLOSED state.
1416     * 
1417     * @param sessionName Session name
1418     * @return <code>true</code> if trades is allowed for given session, <code>false</code>
1419     * otherwise.
1420     * @author thakkar
1421     */
1422    protected boolean isBlockTradeAllowedForClosedProduct(String sessionName)
1423    {
1424        boolean allowedSession = false;
1425        for (int index = 0; index < acceptableSessionsWhenProductClosed.size(); index++)
1426        {
1427            if (sessionName.equalsIgnoreCase((String) acceptableSessionsWhenProductClosed
1428                    .get(index)))
1429            {
1430                allowedSession = true;
1431                break;
1432            }
1433        }
1434        return allowedSession;
1435    }
1436 
1437        /**
1438     * Once a AcceptTrade is dequeued from the TradingClass, this method is invoked to finish
1439     * processing the request in sequence. If this is the first trade in the session, set the flag
1440     * and the price even though it may be an out of sequence trade.
1441     * 
1442         * @param productKey TradingProduct which has traded
1443     * @param priceStruct Price at which it traded Sudhir Malhotra
1444     */
1445 
1446    public void setProductTradeInfo(int productKey, PriceStruct priceStruct)
1447            throws SystemException, NotFoundException
1448        {
1449                try
1450                {
1451                    TradingProduct product = getTradingProductHome().findByKey(productKey);
1452            if (!product.hasTradedInSession())
1453                    {
1454                        Price price = PriceFactory.create(priceStruct);
1455                product.setHasTradedInSession(true);
1456                        product.setLastTradePrice(price);
1457                    }
1458                }
1459                catch (NotFoundException ex)
1460                {
1461            // SM throwing NotFoundException here instead of DataValidationException
1462                    String message = "Unable to find ClassKey for given productKey";
1463                    if (Log.isDebugOn())
1464                    {
1465                        Log.debug(this, message);
1466                    }
1467                    throw ex;
1468                }
1469          }

1471    /**
1472     * Crystal Chen
1473     */
1474    protected void isValidTrade(TradeReportStructV2 trade, short productType)
1475            throws DataValidationException, AuthorizationException, CommunicationException,
1476            SystemException, NotAcceptedException
1477    {
1478        TradeValidationStrategy strategy = getTradeValidationStrategy(
1479                trade.tradeReport.sessionName, productType);
1480        strategy.validateTrade(trade);
1481    }
1482 
1483    protected TradeValidationStrategy getTradeValidationStrategy(String sessionName, int productType)
1484            throws DataValidationException
1485{
1486    if (theTradeValidationStrategyHome == null)
1487    {
1488        try
1489                {
1490                        HomeFactory theHomeFactory = HomeFactory.getInstance();
1491                theTradeValidationStrategyHome = (TradeValidationStrategyHome) theHomeFactory
1492                        .findHome(TradeValidationStrategyHome.HOME_NAME);
1493                if (theTradeValidationStrategyHome != null)
1494                {
1495                    if (Log.isDebugOn())
1496                    {
1497                        Log.debug(this, "got the TradeValidationStrategyHome "
1498                                + theTradeValidationStrategyHome);
1499                }
1500            }
1501            else
1502            {
1503                return null;
1504            }
1505        }
1506                    catch (Exception e)
1507                {
1508                        Log.alarm("Couldn't get TradeValidationStrategy");
1509                Log.exception(this, e.getMessage()
1510                        + ", !!! PLEASE CHECK the configuration in XML !!! will NOT use DEFAULT Bust Strategy to continue",
1511                              e);
1512                throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(
1513                        "TradeValidationStrategy not found for given productKey", DataValidationCodes.INVALID_PRODUCT);
1514                }
1515    }
1516    return theTradeValidationStrategyHome.find(sessionName, productType);
1517}

1519    private TradingProduct findTradingProduct(int productKey) throws DataValidationException
1520    {
1521        try
1522        {
1523            return getTradingProductHome().findByKey(productKey);
1524        }
1525        catch (NotFoundException e)
1526        {
1527            Log.exception(this, "Unable to find TradingProduct for given productKey = "
1528                        + productKey, e);
1529                throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(
1530                        "Product not found for given productKey", DataValidationCodes.INVALID_PRODUCT);
1531        }
1532    }
1533 
1534    /**
1535     * Accepts a trade bust request and queues a command on the TradingClass
1536     *
1537     * The busting process largely delegate the tasks to BustManager. The BustManager coordinates
1538     * any necessary steps/parties for a bust
1539     * 
1540     * @param tradingSessionName The trading session name
1541     * @param productKey traded product
1542     * @param tradeId the trade id of the trade being busted
1543     * @param tradesToBust A sequence of BustTradeStructs representing the trades atomic trades to
1544     * bust
1545     * @param reasonDescription A text description of the reason the bust was performed
1546     * @param isMarketMakerRequestedBust tells if the bust request comes from a market maker. This
1547     * is relevant only for PAR trade busts initiated on ctmi. For all other trade types this value
1548     * can be set to false.
1549     * @param marketMakerSide if isMarketMakerRequestedBust = true, this parameter tells the side (B
1550     * or S) the market maker is on. This is relevant only for PAR trade busts initiated on ctmi.
1551     * For all other trade types (and when a market maker does not exist) this value can be set to
1552     * Sides.UNSPECIFIED.
1553     */
1554    private void acceptTradeBustV2(String tradingSessionName, int productKey, CboeIdStruct tradeId,
1555            BustTradeStruct[] tradesToBust, String reasonDescription,
1556            boolean isMarketMakerRequestedBust, char marketMakerSide) throws SystemException,
1557            CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException,
1558            NotAcceptedException, TransactionFailedException
1559    {
1560       TradeReport tradeReportToBust = validateTradeBustParameters(tradingSessionName, tradeId);
1561        bustLocalTrades(tradingSessionName, tradeReportToBust, tradesToBust, reasonDescription, isMarketMakerRequestedBust, marketMakerSide );
1562    }

1567    public void acceptTradeBust(String tradingSessionName, int productKey, CboeIdStruct tradeId,
1568            BustTradeStruct[] atomicTrades, String reasonDescription) throws SystemException,
1569            CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException,
1570            NotAcceptedException, TransactionFailedException
1571    {
1572        TradeReport tradeReportToBust = validateTradeBustParameters(tradingSessionName, tradeId);
1573        bustLocalTrades(tradingSessionName, tradeReportToBust, atomicTrades, reasonDescription, false, Sides.UNSPECIFIED );
1574    }

1576private TradeReport validateTradeBustParameters(String tradingSessionName, CboeIdStruct tradeId)
1577throws SystemException, DataValidationException, NotAcceptedException
1578{
1579    String openSessionName = TradingSessionNameHelper.getOpenConfiguredSessionName();
1580    if (tradingSessionName == null || openSessionName == null
1581            || !openSessionName.equals(tradingSessionName))
1582    {
1583        String message = "Invalid trading session name: " + tradingSessionName
1584        + "Open Session: " + openSessionName + " at TradeService.acceptTradeBust().";
1585        Log.alarm(this, message);
1586        throw ExceptionBuilder.notAcceptedException(message, NotAcceptedCodes.INVALID_STATE);
1587    }
1588 
1589    //  verify that trade id is valid and that trade can be busted
1590    TradeReport tradeReport;
1591    try
1592    {
1593        tradeReport = getTradeReport(CboeId.longValue(tradeId));
1594        ((TradeReportImpl) tradeReport).turnOffPersistentBObjectInterceptor(true);
1595    }
1596    catch (NotFoundException nfe)
1597    {
1598        throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(
1599                "Unable to find trade report for tradeId - " + tradeId, 0);
1600    }
1601    return tradeReport;        
1602}
1603 
1604    
1605    private TradeReport validateTradeBustParameters(MultipleTradeBustStruct tradeBustRequest) 
1606        throws SystemException, DataValidationException, NotAcceptedException
1607    {
1608        String tradingSessionName = tradeBustRequest.tradingSessionName;
1609        String openSessionName = TradingSessionNameHelper.getOpenConfiguredSessionName();
1610        if (tradingSessionName == null || openSessionName == null
1611                || !openSessionName.equals(tradingSessionName))
1612        {
1613            String message = "Invalid trading session name: " + tradingSessionName
1614            + "Open Session: " + openSessionName + " at TradeService.acceptTradeBust().";
1615            Log.alarm(this, message);
1616            throw ExceptionBuilder.notAcceptedException(message, NotAcceptedCodes.INVALID_STATE);
1617        }
1618 
1619        //  verify that trade id is valid and that trade can be busted
1620        TradeReport tradeReport;
1621        try
1622        {
1623            tradeReport = getTradeReport(CboeId.longValue(tradeBustRequest.tradeId));
1624            ((TradeReportImpl) tradeReport).turnOffPersistentBObjectInterceptor(true);
1625        }
1626        catch (NotFoundException nfe)
1627        {
1628            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(
1629                    "Unable to find trade report for tradeId - " + tradeBustRequest.tradeId, 0);
1630        }
1631        
1632        // Trade bust request for cross-product strategy trade at package level
1633        // can not be busted partially.
1634        int totalTradeBustQty = 0;
1635        for (BustTradeStruct atomicTradeBust : tradeBustRequest.tradeBustDetail)
1636        {
1637            totalTradeBustQty += atomicTradeBust.bustedQuantity;
1638        }
1639        if ((tradeReport.getTradeType() == TradeTypes.CROSS_PRODUCT_CROSS_TRADE) ||
1640            (tradeReport.getTradeType() == TradeTypes.CROSS_PRODUCT_LEG_TRADE) ||
1641            (tradeReport.getTradeType() == TradeTypes.CROSS_PRODUCT_AIM_CROSS_TRADE))            
1642        {                        
1643            if ((tradeReport.isParentReport()) && (tradeReport.getQuantity()!= totalTradeBustQty)) 
1644            {
1645                throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("Cannot partially bust cross-product strategy trade at package level.", DataValidationCodes.INVALID_UPDATE_ATTEMPT);
1646            } 
1647        }
1648        if (tradeReport.getTradeType() == TradeTypes.HANDHELD_TRADE)
1649        {
1650            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("Cannot bust floor or carded trade.", DataValidationCodes.INVALID_UPDATE_ATTEMPT);
1651        }
1652        return tradeReport;
1653    }
1654    
1655    private List<TradeBustResponseStruct> bustRemoteTrades(TradeReport tradeReport,
1656            BustTradeStruct[] tradesToBust, String requestingUserId, String transactionId, DateTimeStruct timeStamp, 
1657            KeyValueStruct[] auditLogProperties) throws SystemException,
1658            CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException,
1659            NotAcceptedException, TransactionFailedException
1660    {
1661        ArrayList<BustManager> bustManagerList = new ArrayList<BustManager>();  
1662        TradingProduct product = findTradingProduct(tradeReport.getProduct());
1663        String tradingSessionName = product.getTradingClass().getSessionName();
1664        TradeValidationStrategy tradeValidationStrategy = getTradeValidationStrategy(tradingSessionName, product.getProductKeys().productType);
1665 
1666        BustManager bustManager = new CrossProductLegReportBust(tradeReport, tradesToBust, requestingUserId, 
1667                transactionId, timeStamp,  auditLogProperties);
1668        if (bustManager.isElgibleForClassLock())
1669        {
1670            processTradeBustWithLock(product, bustManager);
1671        }
1672        else
1673        {
1674            processTradeBustWithoutLock(bustManager);
1675        }
1676        bustManagerList.add(bustManager);        
1677        return collectTradeBustResults(bustManagerList);
1678    }
1679    
1680    private IntHashMap<List<TradeReport>> groupTradeReportsByProductKey(Vector reports)
1681    {
1682        IntHashMap<List<TradeReport>> reportsByProductKey = new IntHashMap<List<TradeReport>>();
1683        for (int index = 0; index < reports.size(); index++)  {
1684            int productKey = ((TradeReport) reports.get(index)).getProduct();
1685            List<TradeReport> reportListForProduct = reportsByProductKey.get(productKey);
1686            if (reportListForProduct == null) {
1687                reportListForProduct = new ArrayList<TradeReport>();
1688                reportsByProductKey.put(productKey, reportListForProduct);
1689            }
1690            reportListForProduct.add((TradeReport) reports.get(index));
1691        }
1692        return reportsByProductKey;        
1693    }
1694    private Map<Long, BustTradeStruct> allocateChildBustQuantityToAtomicTrades(List<TradeReport> childReports, 
1695            TradeReport strategyReport, int bustQuantity) 
1696    {
1697        Map<Long, BustTradeStruct> atomicTradeBustAllocation = new HashMap<Long, BustTradeStruct>();
1698        int bustQuantityCounter = 0;
1699        int bustQuantityAdded = 0;
1700        int bustQuantityRequired = bustQuantity * calculateLegRatio(strategyReport.getProduct(), childReports.get(0).getProduct());
1701        int iterationCount = bustQuantityRequired;
1702        
1703        while (bustQuantityCounter < bustQuantityRequired)
1704        {
1705            bustQuantityAdded = 0;
1706            for (TradeReport childReport : childReports)
1707            {
1708                TradeReportEntry[] atomicTrades = childReport.getEntries(true);
1709                for (TradeReportEntry anAtomicTrade : atomicTrades)
1710                {
1711                    if (anAtomicTrade.getQuantity() > 0)  
1712                    {
1713                        long lAtomicTradeId = anAtomicTrade.getAtomicTradeId();
1714                        BustTradeStruct bustRequest = atomicTradeBustAllocation.get(lAtomicTradeId);
1715                        if (bustRequest == null)
1716                        {
1717                            bustRequest = new BustTradeStruct();
1718                            bustRequest.atomicTradeId = CboeId.toStruct(lAtomicTradeId);
1719                            bustRequest.bustedQuantity = 1;
1720                            bustRequest.buyerReinstateRequested = false;  // Reinstate not allowed for strategies
1721                            bustRequest.sellerReinstateRequested = false; // Reinstate not allowed for strategies
1722                            atomicTradeBustAllocation.put(lAtomicTradeId, bustRequest);       
1723                            bustQuantityAdded++;
1724                        }
1725                        else
1726                        {
1727                            if (bustRequest.bustedQuantity < anAtomicTrade.getQuantity())
1728                            {
1729                                bustRequest.bustedQuantity += 1;
1730                                bustQuantityAdded++;
1731                            }
1732                        }
1733                    }
1734                } 
1735            }
1736            if (bustQuantityAdded == 0)
1737            {
1738                // We have gone through all trade reports and their atomic trades
1739                // and there is no more quantity remaining to bust in these trades.
1740                // Yet the strategy bust quantity is still not satisfied. Something is
1741                // wrong here. 
1742                //mismatchQtyWarning = "WARNING: Insufficient qty to bust in equity leg to match with requested bust qty, but busted whatever qty was present";
1743                break;
1744            }
1745            // Increment the strategy level quantity count
1746            bustQuantityCounter += bustQuantityAdded;
1747        }   
1748        return atomicTradeBustAllocation;
1749    }
1750 
1751    private Map<Long, List<BustTradeStruct>> organizeChildTradeBustRequests(List<TradeReport> childReports,
1752            Map<Long, BustTradeStruct> childTradeBustAllocationByAtomicTrade)
1753    {    
1754        Map<Long, List<BustTradeStruct>> bustRequestsForAllChildReports = new HashMap<Long, List<BustTradeStruct>>();
1755        for (TradeReport childReport : childReports)  
1756        {
1757            List<BustTradeStruct> bustRequestsForSingleChildReport = new ArrayList<BustTradeStruct>();
1758            TradeReportEntry[] atomicTrades = childReport.getEntries();
1759            for (TradeReportEntry anAtomicTrade : atomicTrades)
1760            {
1761                long lAtomicTradeId = anAtomicTrade.getAtomicTradeId();
1762                BustTradeStruct atomicTradeBust = childTradeBustAllocationByAtomicTrade.get(lAtomicTradeId);
1763                if (atomicTradeBust != null)
1764                {
1765                    bustRequestsForSingleChildReport.add(atomicTradeBust);
1766                }                 
1767            }
1768            bustRequestsForAllChildReports.put(childReport.getTradeId(), bustRequestsForSingleChildReport);
1769        }
1770        return bustRequestsForAllChildReports;
1771    }
1772 
1773    private List<TradeBustResponseStruct>  bustLocalTrades(String tradingSessionName, TradeReport tradeReport,
1774            BustTradeStruct[] tradesToBust,  String reasonDescription, boolean isMarketMakerRequestedBust, char marketMakerSide) 
1775            throws SystemException,
1776            CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException,
1777            NotAcceptedException, TransactionFailedException
1778    {
1779        ArrayList<BustManager> bustManagerList = new ArrayList<BustManager>();
1780        if (tradeReport.getQuantity() == 0) {
1781            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(
1782                    "Trade Report doesn't have enough quantity to bust for given TradeId " + tradeReport.getTradeId(), DataValidationCodes.INVALID_ID);                            
1783        }
1784        
1785        int productKey = tradeReport.getProduct();        
1786        if (tradeReport.isStrategyReport())
1787        {
1788            TradeReport parentTradeReport = tradeReport.getParentReport();
1789            // The trade report is for the strategy package level
1790            if (parentTradeReport == null )
1791            {      
1792                Vector childReports = tradeReport.getChildReports();
1793                if (childReports != null && childReports.size() > 0)
1794                {
1795                    // Determine the total bust quantity for the
1796                    // entire strategy to determine the bust quantity distribution
1797                    // across multiple trade reports and atomic trades at the leg level.
1798                    int strategyPkgBustQty = 0;
1799                    for (BustTradeStruct theBustStruct : tradesToBust)
1800                    {
1801                        strategyPkgBustQty += theBustStruct.bustedQuantity;
1802                    }                              
1803                    IntHashMap<List<TradeReport>> childReportGroupedByLeg = groupTradeReportsByProductKey(childReports);
1804                    Collection<List<TradeReport>> allGroupedChildReports = childReportGroupedByLeg.values();
1805                    for (List<TradeReport> childReportsForSingleLeg : allGroupedChildReports)
1806                    {
1807                        Map<Long, BustTradeStruct> bustQtyByAtomicTrade = allocateChildBustQuantityToAtomicTrades(childReportsForSingleLeg, 
1808                                tradeReport, strategyPkgBustQty);
1809                        Map<Long, List<BustTradeStruct>> bustRequestsByChildReport = organizeChildTradeBustRequests(childReportsForSingleLeg,
1810                                bustQtyByAtomicTrade);
1811                        for (TradeReport aChildReport : childReportsForSingleLeg)
1812                        {
1813                            String sessionName = aChildReport.getTradingProduct().getTradingClass().getSessionName();
1814                            long childReportId = aChildReport.getTradeId();
1815                            List<BustTradeStruct> bustRequestsForSingleReportForLeg = bustRequestsByChildReport.get(childReportId);
1816                            if (bustRequestsForSingleReportForLeg != null)  
1817                            {
1818                                for (BustTradeStruct atomicTradeBust : bustRequestsForSingleReportForLeg) 
1819                                {
1820                                    BustManager bustMgr = doExecute(aChildReport.getProduct(), aChildReport, 
1821                                            sessionName, atomicTradeBust, isMarketMakerRequestedBust, marketMakerSide);
1822                                    bustManagerList.add(bustMgr);
1823                                }
1824                            }
1825                        }
1826                    }
1827                }
1828                
1829                //Execute the strategy package trade bust.
1830                // Issue one BustReportManager per atomic trade. Each BustReportManagaer
1831                // is handed to an AcceptTradeBustCommand. The command is executed in an
1832                // independent transaction, thus we want to take advantage of ensuring that
1833                // if one atomic trade bust fails that not all atomic trade busts are not
1834                // rolled back. Otherwise we have to start inner transaction on a per
1835                // atomic trade basis. Let's avoid that. 
1836                for (BustTradeStruct aTradeBust : tradesToBust)
1837                {                    
1838                    BustManager bustMgr = doExecute(productKey, tradeReport, tradingSessionName, aTradeBust, isMarketMakerRequestedBust, marketMakerSide);
1839                    bustManagerList.add(bustMgr);
1840                }
1841            }
1842            else
1843            {
1844                int strategyProductKey = parentTradeReport.getProduct();
1845                int reqBustLegQty = 0;
1846                //Cache the original BustStructs
1847                for (BustTradeStruct theBustStruct : tradesToBust)
1848                {
1849                    reqBustLegQty += theBustStruct.bustedQuantity;
1850                }
1851                 
1852                try
1853                {
1854                    long theTradeId = parentTradeReport.getTradeId();
1855                    TradeReport parentReport = getTradeReport(theTradeId);
1856                    ((TradeReportImpl) parentReport).turnOffPersistentBObjectInterceptor(true);
1857                    TradeReportStruct parentReportStruct = parentReport.toStruct(true);
1858                    int packageBustQty = getAdjustBustQuantity(productKey, reqBustLegQty, parentReport, strategyProductKey);
1859                    //get bust struct for package level
1860                    BustTradeStruct[] bustStructs = getTradesToBustStructs(parentReport, parentReportStruct, packageBustQty, false);
1861                    // Execute the strategy leg trade bust first
1862                    for (BustTradeStruct aTradeBust : tradesToBust) 
1863                    {
1864                        BustManager bustMgr = doExecute(productKey, tradeReport,tradingSessionName, aTradeBust, isMarketMakerRequestedBust, marketMakerSide);
1865                        bustManagerList.add(bustMgr);
1866                    }
1867                    
1868                    if (bustStructs.length > 0) {
1869                        //Execute the strategy package trade bus
1870                        for (BustTradeStruct aTradeBust : bustStructs) 
1871                        {
1872                            BustManager theBustMgr = doExecute(parentReportStruct.productKey, parentReport, parentReportStruct.sessionName,aTradeBust, isMarketMakerRequestedBust, marketMakerSide);
1873                            bustManagerList.add(theBustMgr);
1874                        }
1875                    }
1876                }
1877                catch (Exception e)
1878                {
1879                    String msg = "Unable to bust the Trade Report for given tradeId = "  + tradeReport.getTradeId();
1880                    Log.exception(this,msg, e);
1881                    throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(msg, DataValidationCodes.INVALID_ID);                            
1882                }
1883            }
1884        }
1885        else
1886        {
1887            for (BustTradeStruct aTradeBust : tradesToBust) 
1888            {
1889                BustManager bustMgr = doExecute(productKey, tradeReport,tradingSessionName, aTradeBust, isMarketMakerRequestedBust, marketMakerSide);
1890                bustManagerList.add(bustMgr);
1891            }
1892        }
1893        return collectTradeBustResults(bustManagerList);
1894    }
1895    
1896    private List<TradeBustResponseStruct> collectTradeBustResults(List<BustManager> bustManagers)
1897    {
1898        ArrayList<TradeBustResponseStruct> bustResults = new ArrayList<TradeBustResponseStruct>();
1899        for (BustManager aBustManager : bustManagers)
1900        {
1901            bustResults.addAll(aBustManager.getBustResults());
1902        }
1903        return bustResults;
1904    }
1905    
1906    private BustManager doExecute(int prodKey, TradeReport tradeReport, String tradingSessionName,
1907             BustTradeStruct tradeToBust,  boolean parTradeMMSideBust, char parTradeMMSide) throws DataValidationException, NotAcceptedException
1908    {
1909        // get the trading product
1910        TradingProduct product = findTradingProduct(prodKey);
1911 
1912        // find the appropriate BustTradeStrategy
1913        TradeValidationStrategy tradeValidationStrategy = getTradeValidationStrategy(tradingSessionName, product.getProductKeys().productType);
1914        BustManager bustMgr = executeCommand(product, tradeReport, tradeValidationStrategy, tradeToBust, parTradeMMSideBust, parTradeMMSide);
1915        return bustMgr;
1916    }
1917    
1918    private BustManager executeCommand(TradingProduct product, TradeReport tradeReport,
1919            TradeValidationStrategy tradeValidationStrategy, BustTradeStruct tradeToBust,  boolean parTradeMMSideBust, char parTradeMMSide) 
1920    throws DataValidationException, NotAcceptedException
1921    {
1922        BustManager bustManager = new BustReportManager(this, tradeReport, tradeToBust, parTradeMMSideBust, parTradeMMSide);
1923        bustManager.validateTheBust(tradeValidationStrategy);
1924 
1925        if (bustManager.isElgibleForClassLock())
1926        {
1927            processTradeBustWithLock(product, bustManager);
1928    }
1929        else
1930        {
1931            processTradeBustWithoutLock(bustManager);
1932        }
1933        return bustManager;
1934    }
1935    private void processTradeBustWithLock(TradingProduct product, BustManager bustManager)
1936    {
1937        boolean tradeReportBusted = false;
1938        boolean tradablesBusted = false;
1939        boolean transactionSuccess = false;
1940        boolean tradablesBustRequired = false;
1941 
1942        try 
1943        {
1944            Transaction.startTransaction();
1945            try
1946            {
1947                tradeReportBusted = bustManager.bustTradeReport(myIdService);
1948                tradablesBustRequired = bustManager.isBustTradablesRequired();
1949                if (tradeReportBusted && tradablesBustRequired)
1950                {                        
1951                    AcceptTradableBustCommand tradableBustCommand = new AcceptTradableBustCommand(bustManager);
1952                    product.acceptCommand(tradableBustCommand, false);
1953                    
1954                    // The AcceptTradableBustCommand executed via the CommandProcessor to 
1955                    // perform the bust of tradables inside class-level lock. The CommandProcessor
1956                    // for the trading class does not convey the Exceptions thrown during the 
1957                    // bust operations executed from within the AcceptTradableBustCommand.
1958                    // Therefore it is necessary to check the bust result from BustManager to 
1959                    // ensure that the tradable busting was successful. If not, then we
1960                    // need to roll-back the busting of the trade report that is performed
1961                    // outside of the CommandProcessor.
1962                    tradablesBusted = true;
1963                    List<TradeBustResponseStruct> allResponses = bustManager.getBustResults();
1964                    for (TradeBustResponseStruct bustResponse : allResponses) {
1965                        if (bustResponse.errorCode != ServerResponseCodes.SUCCESS)
1966                        {
1967                            tradablesBusted = false;
1968                            break;
1969                        }
1970                    }
1971                }                    
1972            }
1973            catch (Exception e)
1974            {
1975                // Do nothing. All exceptions are already handled
1976                // by the BustManager.bust() in that the exception error codes are recorded
1977                // in the TradeBustResponse struct, and the trade bust
1978                // is marked as UNSUCCESSFUL.
1979            }
1980            if (tradeReportBusted && (!tradablesBustRequired))  {
1981                transactionSuccess = Transaction.commit();
1982            }
1983            else {
1984                if (tradeReportBusted && tradablesBusted) {
1985                    transactionSuccess = Transaction.commit();
1986                }
1987            }
1988        }
1989        finally
1990        {
1991            if(!transactionSuccess)
1992            {
1993                Transaction.rollback();
1994            }
1995        }
1996    }
1997    
1998    private void processTradeBustWithoutLock(BustManager bustManager)
1999    {
2000        boolean tradeReportBusted = false;
2001        boolean tradablesBusted = false;
2002        boolean tradablesBustRequired = false;
2003        boolean transactionSuccess = false;
2004        try 
2005        {
2006            Transaction.startTransaction();
2007            try
2008            {
2009                tradeReportBusted = bustManager.bustTradeReport(myIdService);
2010                tradablesBustRequired = bustManager.isBustTradablesRequired();
2011                if (tradeReportBusted && tradablesBustRequired)
2012                {                        
2013                    tradablesBusted = bustManager.bustTradables();
2014                    bustManager.reinstateOrders();
2015                }                    
2016            }
2017            catch (Exception e)
2018            {
2019                // Do nothing. All exceptions are already handled
2020                // by the BustManager.bust() in that the exception error codes are recorded
2021                // in the TradeBustResponse struct, and the trade bust
2022                // is marked as UNSUCCESSFUL.
2023            }
2024            if (tradeReportBusted && (!tradablesBustRequired))  {
2025                transactionSuccess = Transaction.commit();
2026            }
2027            else {
2028                if (tradeReportBusted && tradablesBusted) {
2029                    transactionSuccess = Transaction.commit();
2030                }
2031            }
2032        }
2033        finally
2034        {
2035            if(!transactionSuccess)
2036            {
2037                Transaction.rollback();
2038            }
2039        }
2040    }

2044    {
2045        String key = productKey + userAcronym.acronym + userFirm.firmNumber;

2047    }

2049    public String flushSucceededFloorTradeDeletesCache()
2050    {
2051        String outputMsg = "\n" + "Clearing all entries in floor trade deletes cache ... " + "\n";
2052        synchronized (TradeServiceImpl.class)
2053        {
2054            succeededFloorTradeDeletesCache.clear();
2055        }
2056        if(Log.isDebugOn())
2057        {
2058            String msg = "Clearing all entries in floor trade deletes cache ... ";
2059            Log.debug(this, msg);
2060        }
2061        return outputMsg;
2062    }

2064    public String showSucceededFloorTradeDeletesCache()
2065    {
2066 
2067            String outputMsg = "\n" + "    FLOOR TRADE DELETE CACHE \n" +
2068                                      "    ------------------------ \n"+ 
2069                                      "PrdKeyAckFrmNum highTid  lowTid \n"+
2070                                      "--------------- ------- --------- \n";
2071            synchronized (TradeServiceImpl.class)
2072            {
2073                Enumeration<String> keys = succeededFloorTradeDeletesCache.keys();
2074                while(keys.hasMoreElements())
2075                {

2080                }
2081            }
2082            outputMsg = outputMsg + "--------------------------------- \n";
2083            return outputMsg;
2084        
2085    }
