2087    public boolean isFloorTradeDeleteRequestInSuceededCache(int productKey, CboeIdStruct tradeId, ExchangeAcronymStruct userAcronym, ExchangeFirmStruct userFirm)
2088    {
2089        String key = productKey + userAcronym.acronym + userFirm.firmNumber;
2090        CboeIdStruct recordedTtradeId = succeededFloorTradeDeletesCache.get(key);
2091        if(recordedTtradeId != null && recordedTtradeId.highCboeId == tradeId.highCboeId && recordedTtradeId.lowCboeId == tradeId.lowCboeId)
2092        {
2093            return true;
2094        }
2095        return false;
2096    }
2097    /**
2098     * Delete an entire trade. This method is meant to delete the full quantity of each and every
2099     * one of the parties (atomic trades) constituting a trade. It's original purpose is to handle
2100     * the deletion of handheld trades.
2101     * 
2102     * @param tradingSessionName The trading session name
2103     * @param productKey traded product
2104     * @param tradeId the trade id of the trade to delete
2105     * @param reasonDescription A text description of the reason the bust was performed
2106     * @throws SystemException
2107     * @throws CommunicationException
2108     * @throws AuthorizationException
2109     * @throws DataValidationException
2110     * @throws NotAcceptedException
2111     * @throws TransactionFailedException
2112     * @throws NotFoundException
2113     * 
2114     * @author Francisco Ojeda
2115     */
2116    private void deleteTrade(String tradingSessionName, int productKey, CboeIdStruct tradeId,
2117            ExchangeAcronymStruct userAcronym, ExchangeFirmStruct userFirm, String reasonDescription)
2118            throws SystemException, CommunicationException, AuthorizationException,
2119            DataValidationException, NotAcceptedException, TransactionFailedException,
2120            NotFoundException
2121    {
2122        if(Log.isDebugOn())
2123    {
2124        Log.debug(this, "In " + getClass().getName() + ".deleteTrade() ");
2125        }
2126 
2127        TradeReport tradeReport;
2128        
2129        //Validate tradeId, get TradeReportStruct and TradeReport for this trade
2130        try
2131        {
2132            tradeReport = getTradeReport(CboeId.longValue(tradeId));
2133        }
2134        catch (NotFoundException nfe)
2135        {
2136            throw ExceptionBuilder.notFoundException("Unable to find trade report "
2137                    + "for tradeId: " + tradeId.highCboeId + " " + tradeId.lowCboeId, 0);
2138        }
2139 
2140        // Validate trade source
2141        if (tradeReport.getTradeSource().equals(TradeSources.SYSTEM))
2142        {
2143            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(
2144                    "Busts for trades with source system are not allowed. Invalid trade souce "
2145                            + "for trade with tradeId: " + tradeId.highCboeId + " "
2146                            + tradeId.lowCboeId, DataValidationCodes.INVALID_TRADE_SOURCE);
2147            }
2148 
2149        // Validate productKey
2150        if( productKey != tradeReport.getProduct() )
2151        {
2152            String message = "Product key " + productKey + " does not match trade's product key "
2153                    + tradeReport.getProduct() + " for trade with tradeId: " + tradeId.highCboeId
2154                    + " " + tradeId.lowCboeId;
2155            throw ExceptionBuilder.notAcceptedException(message, NotAcceptedCodes.INVALID_REQUEST);            
2156        }
2157        
2158        // Validate acronym presence 
2159        if( userAcronym == null ) 
2160        {
2161            String message = "Invalid userAcronym: user acronym cannot be null. "; 
2162            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(message,
2163                    DataValidationCodes.INVALID_EXECUTING_BROKER);
2164        }
2165        
2166        if (userAcronym.exchange == null || userAcronym.exchange.length() <= 0 || 
2167            userAcronym.acronym == null || userAcronym.acronym.length() <= 0)
2168        {
2169            String message = "Invalid userAcronym: user acronym cannot contain null or empty values" +
2170            " userAcronym.exchange: " + userAcronym.exchange +
2171            ", userAcronym.acronym: " + userAcronym.acronym;
2172            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(message,
2173                    DataValidationCodes.INVALID_EXECUTING_BROKER);
2174        }        
2175 
2176        // Validate firm presence
2177        if (userFirm == null)
2178        {
2179            String message = "Invalid userFirm: user firm cannot be null. ";
2180            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(message,
2181                    DataValidationCodes.INVALID_EXECUTING_BROKER_FIRM);
2182        }
2183        
2184        if (userFirm.exchange == null || userFirm.exchange.length() <= 0 || 
2185            userFirm.firmNumber == null || userFirm.firmNumber.length() <= 0)
2186        {
2187            String message = "Invalid userFirm: user firm cannot contain null or empty values" +
2188            " userFirm.exchange: " + userFirm.exchange +
2189            ", userFirm.firmNumber: " + userFirm.firmNumber;
2190            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(message,
2191                    DataValidationCodes.INVALID_EXECUTING_BROKER_FIRM);
2192        }        
2193        
2194        // Verify that it is not duplicated request.
2195        if(isFloorTradeDeleteRequestInSuceededCache(productKey, tradeId, userAcronym, userFirm))
2196        {
2197            String message = "Duplicated request: user attempted to delete an already deleted trade with tradeId: " 
2198                    + tradeId.highCboeId + " " + tradeId.lowCboeId;
2199            throw ExceptionBuilder.notAcceptedException(message, NotAcceptedCodes.INVALID_REQUEST);           
2200        }
2201 
2202        ExchangeAcronymContainer userAcronymContainer = new ExchangeAcronymContainer(userAcronym);
2203 
2204        // Get the number of trades to delete and if trade is PAR trade, it also determines if a
2205        // market maker requested the delete.
2206        int numOfTradesToDelBuyer = 0;
2207        int numOfTradesToDelSeller = 0;
2208        int numOfTradesToDel = 0;
2209        char marketMakerSide = Sides.UNSPECIFIED;
2210        boolean isMarketMakerRequestedDelete = false; // tells if delete is requested by the market
2211                                                      // maker. This is needed for PAR trades only.
2212        TradeReportEntry[] tradeReportEntries = tradeReport.getEntries(true);
2213        for (int i = 0; i < tradeReportEntries.length; ++i)
2214        {
2215            ExchangeAcronymContainer buyerBrokerContainer = new ExchangeAcronymContainer(
2216                    tradeReportEntries[i].getBuyer());
2217            ExchangeAcronymContainer sellerBrokerContainer = new ExchangeAcronymContainer(
2218                    tradeReportEntries[i].getSeller());
2219 
2220            if(Log.isDebugOn())
2221            {
2222                String message = "In " + getClass().getName() + ".deleteTrade()"
2223                        + " passed user acronym: " + userAcronymContainer
2224                        + " tradeReportEntry buyer broker: " + buyerBrokerContainer
2225                        + " tradeReportEntry seller broker: " + sellerBrokerContainer;
2226                Log.debug(this, message);
2227            }
2228            
2229            if (buyerBrokerContainer.equalsIgnoringExchange(userAcronymContainer))
2230            {
2231                marketMakerSide = getMarketMakerSide(tradeId, tradeReportEntries[i], tradeReport
2232                        .getTradeType(), Sides.BUY);
2233                ++numOfTradesToDelBuyer;
2234            }
2235            else if (sellerBrokerContainer.equalsIgnoringExchange(userAcronymContainer))
2236            {
2237                marketMakerSide = getMarketMakerSide(tradeId, tradeReportEntries[i], tradeReport
2238                        .getTradeType(), Sides.SELL);
2239                ++numOfTradesToDelSeller;
2240            }
2241        }
2242 
2243        if( numOfTradesToDelBuyer == 0 && numOfTradesToDelSeller == 0 ) 
2244        {
2245            String message = "User acronym mismatch. User acronym "
2246                    + userAcronymContainer.getAcronym()
2247                    + " does not match any acronym inside trade report with" + " tradeId: "
2248                    + tradeId.highCboeId + " " + tradeId.lowCboeId;
2249            throw ExceptionBuilder.notAcceptedException(message, NotAcceptedCodes.INVALID_REQUEST);                
2250        }
2251        
2252        if (numOfTradesToDelBuyer > numOfTradesToDelSeller)
2253        {
2254            numOfTradesToDel = numOfTradesToDelBuyer;
2255            isMarketMakerRequestedDelete = tradeReport.getTradeType() == TradeTypes.PAR_TRADE
2256                    && marketMakerSide == Sides.BUY;
2257            
2258            if(Log.isDebugOn())
2259            {
2260                String msg1 = "In " + getClass().getName() + " will delete " + Sides.BUY
2261                        + " side trades, numOfTradesToDel = " + numOfTradesToDel
2262                        + ", isMarketMakerRequestedDelete = " + isMarketMakerRequestedDelete;
2263                Log.debug(this, msg1);
2264            }
2265        }
2266        else if (numOfTradesToDelBuyer < numOfTradesToDelSeller)
2267        {
2268            numOfTradesToDel = numOfTradesToDelSeller;
2269            isMarketMakerRequestedDelete = tradeReport.getTradeType() == TradeTypes.PAR_TRADE
2270                    && marketMakerSide == Sides.SELL;
2271            if(Log.isDebugOn())
2272            {
2273                String msg1 = "In " + getClass().getName() + " will delete " + Sides.SELL
2274                        + " side trades, numOfTradesToDel = " + numOfTradesToDel
2275                        + ", isMarketMakerRequestedDelete = " + isMarketMakerRequestedDelete;
2276                Log.debug(this, msg1);
2277            }
2278        }
2279            
2280 
2281        // Generate the list of trades to delete
2282        if (numOfTradesToDel > 0)
2283        {
2284            BustTradeStruct[] tradesToDel = new BustTradeStruct[numOfTradesToDel];
2285            int j = 0;
2286            for ( int i = 0; i < tradeReportEntries.length; ++i )
2287            {
2288                if ((numOfTradesToDelBuyer > 0 && new ExchangeAcronymContainer(
2289                        tradeReportEntries[i].getBuyer())
2290                        .equalsIgnoringExchange(userAcronymContainer))
2291                        || (numOfTradesToDelSeller > 0 && new ExchangeAcronymContainer(
2292                                tradeReportEntries[i].getSeller())
2293                                .equalsIgnoringExchange(userAcronymContainer)))
2294                {
2295                    // This validation is just a precaution against a potential buffer overflow
2296                    // (array out of bounds) exception.
2297                    // Although not likely to happen the fact of dealing with two independent
2298                    // indexes (i & j) makes this
2299                    // a situation to prevent against of.
2300                    if( j > numOfTradesToDel )
2301                    {
2302                        String message = "Error computing the number of trades for trade report with"
2303                                + " tradeId: "
2304                                + tradeId.highCboeId
2305                                + " "
2306                                + tradeId.lowCboeId
2307                                + ". No trades were deleted.";
2308                        throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(message,
2309                                DataValidationCodes.INVALID_LIMITS);
2310                    }                              
2311 
2312                    BustTradeStruct tradeToDel = new BustTradeStruct();
2313                    tradeToDel.atomicTradeId = CboeId.toStruct(tradeReportEntries[i]
2314                            .getAtomicTradeId());
2315                    tradeToDel.bustedQuantity = tradeReportEntries[i].getQuantity();
2316                    tradeToDel.buyerReinstateRequested = false;
2317                    tradeToDel.sellerReinstateRequested = false;
2318                    tradesToDel[j] = tradeToDel;
2319                    ++j;
2320                } // end if
2321            }
2322                
2323            // Delete the list of trades to delete
2324            acceptTradeBustV2(tradingSessionName, productKey, tradeId, tradesToDel,
2325                    reasonDescription, isMarketMakerRequestedDelete, marketMakerSide);
2326            
2327            // At this point the delete trade request has been successful so it is add to the cache
2328            addToSucceededFloorTradeDeletesCache(productKey, tradeId, userAcronym, userFirm);
2329        }
2330        else
2331        {
2332            String message = "No trades inside trade report with " + " tradeId: "
2333                    + tradeId.highCboeId + " " + tradeId.lowCboeId + " matched user acronym: "
2334                    + userAcronymContainer + ". No trades were deleted.";
2335 
2336            Log.information(this, "In " + getClass().getName() + ".deleteTrade : " + message);
2337        }
2338    }

2340    /**
2341     * Returns the side the market maker is on (B or S) in a PAR trade. For all other trade types U
2342     * (UNSPECIFIED) is returned.
2343     * 
2344     * @param tradeId the trade id of the trade
2345     * @param tradeReportEntry report entry to analyze
2346     * @param tradeType trade type to act accordingly. 
2347     * @throws DataValidationException
2348     * @throws NotAcceptedException
2349     * 
2350     * @author Francisco Ojeda
2351     */    
2352    private char getMarketMakerSide(CboeIdStruct tradeId, TradeReportEntry tradeReportEntry,
2353            char tradeType, char side) throws DataValidationException, NotAcceptedException
2354    {
2355        char marketMakerSide = Sides.UNSPECIFIED; 
2356        if(tradeType == TradeTypes.PAR_TRADE)
2357        {
2358            String extensions = tradeReportEntry.getExtensions();   
2359            if(Log.isDebugOn())
2360            {
2361                Log.debug(this, "In " + getClass().getName()
2362                        + ".getMarketmakerSide(...) tradeReportEntry.getExtensions() = " + extensions);
2363            }
2364            
2365            ExtensionsHelper extensionsHelper;
2366            try
2367            {
2368                extensionsHelper =  new ExtensionsHelper(extensions);
2369                extensionsHelper.setFieldDelimiter(TradeReportEntryImpl.FIELD_VALUE_SEPARATOR);
2370            }
2371            catch(ParseException pe)
2372            {
2373                String msg = "Attempted to delete a PAR that has invalid extensions."
2374                        + " TradeId: " + tradeId.highCboeId + " " + tradeId.lowCboeId
2375                        + " extensions: " + extensions;
2376                throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(msg,
2377                        DataValidationCodes.INVALID_EXTENSIONS);
2378            }
2379 
2380            // Check that PAR trade was not deleted already. PAR trades already deleted contain the
2381            // OrigATId=... in the extensions field.
2382            String origATId = extensionsHelper
2383                    .getValue(TradeReportEntryImpl.ORIGINAL_ATOMIC_TRADE_ID);
2384            int indexOfOrigATId = extensions.indexOf(TradeReportEntryImpl.ORIGINAL_ATOMIC_TRADE_ID);
2385            if (origATId != null || (indexOfOrigATId >= 0))
2386            {
2387                String msg = "Attempted to delete a PAR trade that was already deleted."
2388                        + " TradeId: " + tradeId.highCboeId + " " + tradeId.lowCboeId
2389                        + " extensions: " + extensions;
2390                throw ExceptionBuilder.notAcceptedException(msg, NotAcceptedCodes.INVALID_REQUEST); 
2391            }
2392            
2393            // Get MM side by getting value of 'MMTN' from the extensions field.
2394            String mMSide = extensionsHelper.getValue(com.cboe.idl.constants.ExtensionFields.MMTN);
2395            if(mMSide != null)
2396            {
2397                if (mMSide.equals(com.cboe.idl.constants.ExtensionFields.BUY_SIDE))
2398                {
2399                    marketMakerSide = Sides.BUY;
2400                }
2401                else if (mMSide.equals(com.cboe.idl.constants.ExtensionFields.SELL_SIDE))
2402                {
2403                    marketMakerSide = Sides.SELL;
2404                }
2405            }
2406            else
2407            {
2408                String msg = "Attempted to delete a PAR trade that has no MM side in extensions."
2409                        + " TradeId: " + tradeId.highCboeId + " " + tradeId.lowCboeId
2410                        + " extensions: " + extensions;
2411                throw ExceptionBuilder.notAcceptedException(msg, NotAcceptedCodes.INVALID_REQUEST);
2412            }
2413            if(Log.isDebugOn())
2414            {
2415                Log.debug(this, "In " + getClass().getName() + " PAR trade with marketMakerSide = "
2416                        + marketMakerSide);
2417            }
2418        }   
2419        else if (tradeType == TradeTypes.HANDHELD_TRADE)
2420        {
2421            marketMakerSide = side;
2422        }
2423        return marketMakerSide;
2424    }

2724        /**
2725         * @deprecated use deCodeExtensionsCompatible(String extensions)
2726         * @param extensions
2727         * @return
2728         */
2729        private List deCodeExtensions(String extensions)
2730        {
2731            String PDPM_EXT = "PDPM";
2732            List tieredPdpms = new ArrayList();
2733            String pdpms;
2734 
2735            try
2736            {
2737                ExtensionsHelper extHelper = new ExtensionsHelper(extensions);
2738                pdpms = extHelper.getValue(PDPM_EXT);
2739            if (pdpms != null && pdpms.trim().length() > 0)
2740                {
2741                    int start = 0;
2742                    pdpms = pdpms.trim();
2743 
2744                    while (start < pdpms.length())
2745                    {
2746                        tieredPdpms.add(pdpms.substring(start, start + 3));
2747                        start += 3;
2748                    }
2749                }
2750            }
2751            catch (ParseException pe)
2752            {
2753            Log.alarm(this, "Extensions field parsing failed: " + extensions + " exception: " + pe);
2754            }
2755 
2756            return tieredPdpms;
2757        }
2758 
2759        protected List deCodeExtensionsCompatible(String extensions)
2760        {
2761            List tieredPdpms = new ArrayList();
2762                        
2763            if (extensions != null && extensions.trim().length() > 0)
2764            {
2765                String pdpms = PDPMExtensionsCompatibleHelper.getField(extensions);
2766                
2767            if (pdpms.length() > 0)
2768            {
2769                    pdpms = pdpms.trim();
2770                }
2771 
2772            if (pdpms != null && pdpms.length() > 0)
2773                {
2774                    int start = 0;
2775                    while ((start + 3) <= pdpms.length())
2776                    {
2777                        tieredPdpms.add(pdpms.substring(start, start + 3));
2778                        start += 3;
2779                    }
2780                }
2781            }
2782            return tieredPdpms;
2783        }
2784 
2785    /**
2786     * This method is used to match the ParticipantList of the buyers to the ParticipantList of the
2787     * sellers and when possible to create trades "one from column A and one from column B"
2788     * 
2789     */
2790    protected TradeReport doTradeMatch(TradingProduct tradingProduct, boolean heldOrderTrade,
2791            ParticipantList biders, ParticipantList askers, Price price, TradeReport parent,
2792            short auctionType) throws DataValidationException, SystemException
2793    {
2794            char tradeType = TradeTypes.REGULAR_TRADE;
2795        if (tradingProduct.isTradableCrossProduct())
2796        {
2797            // set trade type of spread level and option level report to CROSS_PRODUCT_CROSS_TRADE
2798            // ('S') as well
2799            // required by new GUI  and back office enhancement
2800            if (auctionType == AuctionTypes.AUCTION_INTERNALIZATION)
2801            {
2802                tradeType = TradeTypes.CROSS_PRODUCT_AIM_CROSS_TRADE;
2803                                           
2804                Log.information(this, "set trade type to (" + tradeType + "), for product key ="
2805                        + tradingProduct.getProductKey());
2806            }
2807            else
2808            {
2809            tradeType = TradeTypes.CROSS_PRODUCT_CROSS_TRADE;
2810            if (Log.isDebugOn())
2811            {
2812                    Log.debug(this, "set trade type of both spread and local legs level to ("
2813                            + TradeTypes.CROSS_PRODUCT_CROSS_TRADE + "), for product key ="
2814                            + tradingProduct.getProductKey());
2815            }
2816        }
2817        }
2818        return doTradeMatch((TradeReportImpl) null, tradingProduct, tradeType,
2819                TradeTypes.REGULAR_TRADE, heldOrderTrade, biders, askers, price, parent,
2820                    auctionType);
2821    }

2823    private TradeReport doTradeMatch(TradeReportImpl tradeReport, TradingProduct tradingProduct,

2850    private TradeReport doTradeMatch(TradeReportImpl tradeReport, TradingProduct tradingProduct,
2851            char tradeType, char settlementTradeType, boolean heldOrderTrade,
2852            ParticipantList biders, ParticipantList askers, Price price, TradeReport parent)
2853            throws DataValidationException, SystemException
2854    {
2855        ArrayList atomicTrades = new ArrayList();
2856        int matchQty = createAtomicTrades(biders, askers, atomicTrades, tradingProduct);
2857        if (matchQty<=0)
2858                throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("Create atomic trade for::"+tradingProduct+" at "+price+" returned 0 match qty", 0);
2859 
2860        tradeReport = createTrade(tradeReport, tradingProduct, tradeType, settlementTradeType,
2861                heldOrderTrade, matchQty, price, atomicTrades, parent);
2862            tradeReport.setBidList(biders);
2863            tradeReport.setAskList(askers);
2864            return tradeReport;
2865        }
2866 
2867    /**
2868     * create atomic trades
2869     */
2870    protected int createAtomicTrades(ParticipantList biders, ParticipantList askers,
2871            ArrayList atomicTrades, TradingProduct product) throws DataValidationException
2872    {
2873        boolean isExceptionExit = true ;
2874        epCreateAtomicTrades.enter();
2875        try
2876        {
2877                Enumeration buyItems = biders.elements();
2878                Enumeration sellItems = askers.elements();
2879        if ((buyItems == null) || (sellItems == null))
2880        {
2881            isExceptionExit = false;
2882            return 0;
2883        }
2884        if ((!buyItems.hasMoreElements()) || (!sellItems.hasMoreElements()))
2885        { // initial checking
2886            isExceptionExit = false;
2887            return 0;
2888        }
2889        ParticipantItem buyer  = null;
2890        ParticipantItem seller = null;
2891        int buyQty   = 0;
2892        int sellQty  = 0;
2893        int matchQty = 0;
2894        int tradeQty = 0;
2895        while ((buyQty > 0 || buyItems.hasMoreElements())
2896                && (sellQty > 0 || sellItems.hasMoreElements()))
2897        {
2898            if (buyQty <= 0)
2899            {
2900                buyer = (ParticipantItem) buyItems.nextElement();
2901                buyQty = buyer.getParticipantQuantity();
2902                if (buyQty <= 0)
2903                {
2904                    Log.information("TradeServiceImpl.doTradeMatch>> participant item has no participant quantity::"+buyer);
2905                    continue;
2906                }
2907            }
2908            if (sellQty <= 0)
2909            {
2910                seller = (ParticipantItem) sellItems.nextElement();
2911                sellQty = seller.getParticipantQuantity();
2912                if (sellQty <= 0)
2913                {
2914                    Log.information("TradeServiceImpl.doTradeMatch>> participant item has no participant quantity::"+seller);
2915                    continue;
2916                }
2917            }
2918            tradeQty = (buyQty < sellQty)
2919                    ? buyQty
2920                    : sellQty;
2921            AtomicTrade atomicTrade = new AtomicTradeImpl(buyer, seller, tradeQty, product);
2922            atomicTrades.add(atomicTrade);
2923            buyQty   -= tradeQty;
2924            sellQty  -= tradeQty;
2925            matchQty += tradeQty; // keep track of the sum of all the individual AtomicTrades
2926        }
2927        isExceptionExit = false;
2928        return matchQty;
2929    }
2930        finally
2931        {
2932            epCreateAtomicTrades.exit(isExceptionExit);  
2933        }
2934         
2935      
2936   
2937    }
2938 
2939        /**
2940         * Will obtain a a TradeReport given a tradeId
2941         *
2942         * author Matt Sochacki
2943         *
2944         * @return TradeReportStruct
2945         */
2946    private TradeReport getTradeReport(long tradeId) throws NotFoundException, SystemException
2947    {
2948        TradeReport tradeReport;
2949 
2950        try
2951        {
2952            tradeReport = getTradeReportHome().findByKey(tradeId);
2953        }
2954        catch (TransactionFailedException pe)
2955        {
2956                        String msg = "Unable to retrieve TradeReport due to persistenceException, and going to throw SystemException";
2957            Log.exception(this, msg, pe);
2958            throw ExceptionBuilder.systemException(msg, 0);
2959                }
2960        if (tradeReport == null || !tradeReport.isReportForLocalTradeServer())
2961        {
2962            Log.information(this, "Dismissing the found trade report with trade id " + tradeId
2963                    + ". The report is not for product assigned to the local trade server.");
2964            throw ExceptionBuilder.notFoundException("Trade report not found", 0);
2965        }
2966                return tradeReport;
2967        }

3214    protected TradeReport tradeMatch(TradingProduct tradingProduct, char tradeType,
3215            char settlementTradeType, ParticipantList biders, ParticipantList askers,
3216            Price tradePrice, TradeReport parent, boolean isTBForCOB) throws SpreadProcessingException,
3217            DataValidationException, SystemException
3218    {

3226        isExceptionExit = false; 
3227        return tradeReport;
3228        }
3229        finally
3230        {
3231            epTradeMatch.exit(isExceptionExit);
3232        }    
3233    }

3235    protected TradeReport tradeMatch(TradingProduct tradingProduct, char tradeType,
3236            char settlementTradeType, boolean heldOrderTrade, ParticipantList biders,
3237            ParticipantList askers, Price tradePrice, TradeReport parent, Tradable tradable, boolean isQualifiedContingentTrade, boolean isTBForCOB)
3238            throws SpreadProcessingException,
3239            DataValidationException, SystemException
3240    {
3241        
3242        long id = metricsHandler.generateTradeMatchMetricId(tradingProduct.getProductKey(),
3243                tradingProduct.getTradingClass().getSessionName(), biders.getTotalTradeQuantity());
3244        metricsHandler.sendMethodEvent(PerformanceMetricsTradeMatchHandler.TRADE_COLLECTOR_TYPE,
3245                id, 0);
3246        TradeReport theReport = null;
3247        if (tradingProduct.isStrategy())
3248        {
3249            theReport = doTradeMatchForSpread(tradingProduct, tradeType, settlementTradeType,
3250                    heldOrderTrade, biders, askers, tradePrice,tradable,isQualifiedContingentTrade, isTBForCOB);
3251        }
3252        else
3253        {
3254            theReport = doTradeMatch(tradingProduct, tradeType, settlementTradeType,
3255                    heldOrderTrade, biders, askers, tradePrice, parent);
3256        }
3257 
3258        metricsHandler.sendMethodEvent(PerformanceMetricsTradeMatchHandler.TRADE_COLLECTOR_TYPE,
3259                id, 1);
3260        return theReport;
3261   
3262    }

3354    /**
3355         *  Creates a trade for the cross
3356     * 
3357         *  @param aCross - the cross to be executed
3358     *  @exception DataValidationException if the cross is for an unknown product.
3359         */
3360    public void createCrossTrade(Cross aCross, Price tradingPrice, OrderBook book)
3361            throws SpreadProcessingException, DataValidationException, SystemException
3362    {
3363        Order buyOrder = aCross.getBuyOrder();
3364        Order sellOrder = aCross.getSellOrder();
3365 
3366        int tradeQuantity = Math.min(buyOrder.getQuantityAllowed(), sellOrder.getQuantityAllowed());
3367 
3368        if (tradeQuantity > 0)
3369        {
3370            boolean isLinkedAwayTradeAndBuySideIsLinkedAway = false;
3371            boolean isLinkedAwayTradeAndSellSideIsLinkedAway = false;
3372            try
3373            {
3374                isLinkedAwayTradeAndBuySideIsLinkedAway = aCross.isCrossWithAutoLinkedPAOrder()
3375                        && aCross.isLinkedAwaySideABuy();
3376                isLinkedAwayTradeAndSellSideIsLinkedAway = aCross.isCrossWithAutoLinkedPAOrder()
3377                        && (!aCross.isLinkedAwaySideABuy());
3378            }
3379            catch (NotSupportedException e)
3380            {
3381                // ignore, which means the cross does not support link away; keep default FALSE for
3382                // both
3383            }
3384 
3385            ParticipantList buyList = new ParticipantListImpl();
3386            ParticipantItem buyer = new ParticipantItemImpl(buyOrder, tradeQuantity,
3387                    isLinkedAwayTradeAndBuySideIsLinkedAway
3388                            ? ParticipantItem.LINKED_AWAY
3389                            : ParticipantItem.NONE);
3390            buyList.addElement(buyer);
3391 
3392            ParticipantList sellList = new ParticipantListImpl();
3393            ParticipantItem seller = new ParticipantItemImpl(sellOrder, tradeQuantity,
3394                    isLinkedAwayTradeAndSellSideIsLinkedAway
3395                            ? ParticipantItem.LINKED_AWAY
3396                            : ParticipantItem.NONE);
3397            sellList.addElement(seller);
3398 
3399            char tradeTypeToUse = getTradeType(aCross, book);
3400 
3401            TradeReport report = tradeMatch(book.getTradingProduct(), tradeTypeToUse,
3402                    getSettlementTradeType(aCross, book), aCross.isProcessingOutOfSequence(), buyList,
3403                    sellList, tradingPrice, (TradeReport) null, null,false, false);
3404            report.completeTrade(false, null);
3405        }
3406        else
3407        {
3408            Log.alarm(this, "createCrossTrade::trade quantity is 0.");
3409        }
3410    }

3556     * this processor is product-specific and we need to execute a command using a class-level lock.

3571    protected int tradeCrossProductLegs(Order strategyOrder, TradingProduct strategy,
3572            DerivedQuote derivedQuote, AuctionInternal auction) throws SystemException,
3573            DataValidationException
3574    {
3575        Broker broker = strategy.getBroker();
3576        Log.information("Attempting leg trading on Order["+strategyOrder.toString()+"]...");
3577        ProcessStrategyLegsCommand cmd = StrategyTradeServiceHelper
3578                .createProcessStrategyLegsCommand(strategyOrder, broker, derivedQuote, strategy,
3579                        auction);
3580        try
3581        {  
3582            getClassBroker(strategy.getTradingClass().getProductClassKey()).acceptCommand(cmd,
3583                    false/* !ignoreQueueLimit ("execute now") */);
3584            cmd.waitForCompletion();  // (support possible asynchronous execution)
3585        }
3586        catch (Exception e)
3587        {
3588            Log
3589            .exception(
3590                    "ProcessStrategyLegsCommand as a sub-command call failed, but proceed to the next step regardless",
3591                    e);
3592            return 0;
3593        }
3594        int qtyTraded = cmd.getSpreadTradeQuantity();
3595        if (qtyTraded == 0)
3596        {
3597            Log.information("Attempted leg trading on Order[" + strategyOrder.toString()
3598                    + "] but NO TRADE");
3599        }
3600        else
3601        {
3602            Log.information("Order[" + strategyOrder.toString() + "] leg trading filled qty="
3603                    + qtyTraded);
3604        }
3605        return qtyTraded;
3606    }

3608    public int createTradeForBookedCPSpreadsWithLegs(OrderBook aBook, Side tradeSide,
3609            DerivedQuote derivedQuote) throws SpreadProcessingException, DataValidationException,
3610            SystemException
3611    {
3612        int total = 0;
3613        Enumeration tradables;
3614        Tradable nextTradable;
3615        TradingProduct tProduct = aBook.getTradingProduct();
3616        tradables = aBook.getTradables(tradeSide);
3617        while(tradables.hasMoreElements())
3618        {
3619            nextTradable = (Tradable) tradables.nextElement();
3620            if (!StrategyTradeServiceHelper.isStrategyLegNBBO((Order) nextTradable, tProduct,
3621                    derivedQuote))
3622            {
3623                Log.information("createTradeForBookedCPSpreadsWithLegs(): Order: " + nextTradable
3624                        + " can't trade with leg because of at least one of legs is not NBBO");
3625                break;
3626            }
3627            if (Log.isDebugOn())
3628            {
3629                Log.debug("Trying leg trade:" + nextTradable);
3630            }
3631            total = tradeCrossProductLegs((Order)nextTradable, tProduct, derivedQuote,null);
3632        }
3633        return total;
3634    }

3636    /**
3637     * Creates a trade for the booked spread with contingency legs
3638     */
3639    public int createTradeForBookedSpreadsWithLegs(OrderBook aBook, Side tradeSide,
3640            DerivedQuote derivedQuote) throws SpreadProcessingException, DataValidationException,
3641            SystemException
3642    {
3643        StrategyLegTradeContainer legTradeContainer = StrategyTradeServiceHelper
3644                .getStrategyLegTradeContainer(aBook, tradeSide, derivedQuote);
3645        int total = 0;
3646        int allocatedQ = 0;
3647        Price spreadSidePrice;
3648        DerivedQuote newDerivedQuote;
3649        
3650        if(aBook.getTradingProduct().isBuyWrite())
3651        {
3652                return createTradeForBookedCPSpreadsWithLegs(aBook, tradeSide, derivedQuote);
3653        }
3654        
3655        while (legTradeContainer.getCanTradeWithLegs())
3656        {
3657            spreadSidePrice = StrategyTradeServiceHelper
3658                    .getTradePriceForOtherSide(legTradeContainer.getTradablePrice());
3659            ParticipantList spreadList = new ParticipantListImpl();
3660            allocatedQ = allocateSpreadTradables(spreadList, aBook, spreadSidePrice, tradeSide,
3661                    legTradeContainer.getQuantity());
3662            if (allocatedQ == 0)
3663            {
3664                break;
3665            }
3666            total = total + allocatedQ;
3667            ParticipantList derivedList = new ParticipantListImpl(ParticipantList.DERIVED_LIST,
3668                    legTradeContainer.getUseContingentBest());
3669            derivedList.addElement(new ParticipantItemImpl(legTradeContainer.getTradable(),
3670                    allocatedQ));
3671            derivedList.setLegTradePrices(legTradeContainer.getLegPrices());
3672 
3673            TradeReport report;
3674            
3675            // This is for DAIM Allocation.
3676            Tradable tradable = getTradableForDAIMAllocation(aBook,tradeSide);
3677            
3678            if (tradeSide.isAsDefinedSide())
3679            {
3680                report = tradeMatch(aBook.getTradingProduct(), spreadList, derivedList,
3681                        spreadSidePrice, tradable);
3682            }
3683            else
3684            {
3685                report = tradeMatch(aBook.getTradingProduct(), derivedList, spreadList,
3686                        legTradeContainer.getTradablePrice(), tradable);
3687            }
3688            report.completeTrade(true, null);
3689            newDerivedQuote = StrategyTradeServiceHelper.getDerivedQuote(aBook.getTradingProduct());
3690            if (newDerivedQuote == null)
3691            {
3692                break;
3693            }
3694            legTradeContainer = StrategyTradeServiceHelper.getStrategyLegTradeContainer(aBook,
3695                    tradeSide, newDerivedQuote);
3696        }
3697        return total;
3698    }
3699 
3700    /*
3701     * This change for the specific case when an incoming DAIM Spread order changes the state of the
3702     * spread product from ON_HOLD to OPEN. In this case, the daim participants should be penalized.
3703     * But in the scenario where there is a resting DAIM spread order and a leg market change is
3704     * triggering the state change from ON_HOLD to OPEN, there should be no penalization since the
3705     * DAIM order has already booked.
3706         */
3707    protected Tradable getTradableForDAIMAllocation(OrderBook aBook, Side tradeSide)
3708    {
3709            Tradable tradable = null;
3710                OrderBookSideItem orderBookSideItem;                                  
3711                OrderBookImpl orderBook = null;
3712                if(aBook instanceof OrderBookImpl)
3713                        orderBook= (OrderBookImpl)aBook;                                  
3714 
3715                if(orderBook.getBuySideItem().getSide().isSameSide(tradeSide))
3716                {
3717                        orderBookSideItem = orderBook.getBuySideItem();
3718                }
3719                else
3720                {
3721                        orderBookSideItem = orderBook.getSellSideItem();
3722                 }
3723                  
3724                 if(orderBookSideItem.getFirstLimitPriceItem().getNextItem() == null)
3725                 {
3726            PriceDetailIterator iterator = orderBookSideItem.getFirstLimitPriceItem()
3727                    .getPriceDetails();
3728                          OrderBookPriceDetailImpl firstPriceDetail=null;
3729                          while(iterator!=null && iterator.hasNext())
3730                          {
3731                                        firstPriceDetail = (OrderBookPriceDetailImpl)iterator.next();
3732                                        if(!iterator.hasNext())
3733                                        {
3734                                                tradable = firstPriceDetail.getTradable();
3735                                                if( tradable instanceof OrderImpl)
3736                                                {
3737                        if (((OrderImpl) tradable).isDirectedAIMOrderMatched()
3738                                && ((OrderImpl) tradable).getDAIMedUserList() != null
3739                                && ((OrderImpl) tradable).getDAIMedUserList().size() > 0)
3740                                                        {
3741                                                                ((OrderImpl)tradable).setDirectedAIMOrderAndNotMatched(false);
3742                                                        }
3743                                                        else
3744                                                        {
3745                                                                tradable =null;
3746                                                        }
3747                                                }
3748                                                else
3749                                                {
3750                                                        tradable =null;
3751                                                }
3752                                        }
3753                          }
3754                  }
3755                 return tradable;
3756    }

3758    public List<Tradable> getPrioritizedTradables(Order anOrder, Side side, OrderBook book,
3759            Price endingPrice, boolean nonQTrade) throws SystemException, DataValidationException
3760    {
3761 
3762        Iterator sets;
3763        PriorityTradableSet nextSet;
3764        OrderBookPriceDetail priceDetail;
3765        List<Tradable> tradables = new ArrayList<Tradable>();
3766 
3767        AllocationTradeContextImpl allocationContext;
3768        allocationContext = new AllocationTradeContextImpl(AllocationTradeTypes.REGULAR);
3769        allocationContext.setNonQAllocation(nonQTrade);
3770        //DAIM change: Set the tradable in the allocation Context.
3771        if (!anOrder.isBookedByAuction())// The penalization should not take place if the order has
3772                                         // auctioned.
3773        {
3774                allocationContext.setTradable(((Tradable) anOrder));
3775        }
3776 
3777        List preferredFirmAcronym = getPreferredFirmAcronym(anOrder);
3778        int legRatio = calculateLegRatio(anOrder.getProductKey(), book.getTradingProduct()
3779                .getProductKey());
3780        if (preferredFirmAcronym != null && preferredFirmAcronym.size() != 0)
3781        {
3782            allocationContext.setPreferredFirm(preferredFirmAcronym);
3783            allocationContext.setQtyForPmmAllocation(anOrder.getQuantityAllowed()*legRatio);
3784        }
3785        
3786        sets = book.getPrioritySets(side, endingPrice, Integer.MAX_VALUE, allocationContext);
3787 
3788        while (sets.hasNext())
3789        {
3790            nextSet = (PriorityTradableSet) sets.next();
3791            while (nextSet.hasMoreElements())
3792            {
3793                priceDetail = (OrderBookPriceDetail) nextSet.nextElement();
3794               tradables.add(priceDetail.getTradable());
3795               priceDetail.dellocateLastAllocated();
3796            }
3797        }
3798        return tradables;
3799    }

3801      /**

3805     * @param legProductKey
3806     * @return
3807     */
3808    private int calculateLegRatio(int strategyProductKey, int legProductKey)
3809    {

3835    public int createRegularTradeForALeg(Tradable[] legTradables, int[] qtySplits, int qtyToTrade,
3836            TradingProduct legProduct, OrderBook legBook, Price endingPrice,
3837            boolean needsSingleFillOnly, TradeReport parent, AuctionInternal auction)
3838            throws SpreadProcessingException, DataValidationException, SystemException
3839    {

3842        try
3843        {
3844            // Bug Fix CBOqa06679 - try internalCreateRegularTrade() first for Regular orders
3845            // Note the method internalCreateRegularTrade() has one more parameter for
3846            // adjustedQuantity for
3847            // taking out the volume contingencies. If transaction fails - meaning no trade was
3848            // possible because allocation
3849            // was 0, try the trade without volume contingency by calling the method again with an
3850            // adjustment quantity
3851            // for volume contingency. This adjustment quantity is obtained by a call to new method
3852            // getAdjustedQuantityForVolumeContingency(). This process is caried out only if book
3853            // has volume contingency
3854            //
3855            //

3857                    .asList(legTradables));

3859            allocatedQuantity = internalCreateRegularTradeForALeg(sameSides, legTradables[0]
3860                    .getSide().getOtherSide(), getPreferredFirmAcronym(legTradables[0]),

3957    private int createParticipantListsBasedOnKnownSide(int[] knownSideQtySplits,
3958            ArrayList outputParticipantList, ArrayList outputTradePrices,
3959            ArrayList outputTradeQuantityList, List preferredFirmAcronym,
3960            String preferredFirmExchange, TradingProduct aProduct, OrderBook book,
3961            Side tradableSide, Price endingPrice, int quantityToAllocate,
3962            boolean needsSingleFillOnly, Tradable tradable,AuctionInternal auction)
3963     {
3964        boolean nonQTrade = false;
3965                Tradable spreadTradable  = null;
3966                if(tradable instanceof SpreadTradableImpl)
3967                        spreadTradable = ((SpreadTradableImpl)tradable).getTradable();
3968 
3969            int allocatedQty = 0;
3970        if(auction != null)
3971        {
3972                allocatedQty = createParticipantListsForCPSCOA( outputParticipantList,
3973                    outputTradePrices, outputTradeQuantityList, preferredFirmAcronym,
3974                    preferredFirmExchange, aProduct, book, tradableSide, endingPrice,
3975                    quantityToAllocate, nonQTrade, needsSingleFillOnly, spreadTradable, auction);
3976        }
3977        //PMM-END
3978        else
3979        {
3980                allocatedQty = createParticipantLists(outputParticipantList, outputTradePrices,
3981                outputTradeQuantityList, preferredFirmAcronym, preferredFirmExchange, aProduct,
3982                book, tradableSide, endingPrice, quantityToAllocate, nonQTrade,
3983                    needsSingleFillOnly, false, spreadTradable, false);
3984        }
3985 
3986        if (knownSideQtySplits == null)
3987            return allocatedQty;
3988        // TODO: This is totally coupled with the cross product leg trading logic
3989        //      which supposely should always have 1-1 trading
3990        //      This special case should only happen on an attempt to trade
3991        //           at pre-determined multiple qty levels with a resting AON order
3992        //      Note, the code only attempts to work on this one condition
3993        //      This is in place when no better solution is available without massive code change
3994        //      2007/08/14
3995        int oppoSideSplits = outputParticipantList.size();
3996        if (allocatedQty == quantityToAllocate)
3997        {
3998            if (oppoSideSplits < knownSideQtySplits.length)
3999            {
4000                int j = 0;
4001                for (int i = 0; i < oppoSideSplits; i++)
4002                {
4003                    int cur = ((Integer) outputTradeQuantityList.get(i)).intValue();
4004                    if (cur > knownSideQtySplits[j])
4005                    {
4006                        outputParticipantList.add(i + 1, outputParticipantList.get(i));
4007                        outputTradePrices.add(i + 1, outputTradePrices.get(i));
4008                        outputTradeQuantityList.remove(i);
4009                        outputTradeQuantityList.add(i, new Integer(knownSideQtySplits[j]));
4010                        outputTradeQuantityList
4011                                .add(i + 1, new Integer(cur - knownSideQtySplits[j]));
4012                        oppoSideSplits += 1;
4013                        j += 1;
4014                    }
4015                    else if (cur == knownSideQtySplits[j])
4016                    {
4017                        continue;
4018                    }
4019                    else
4020                    {
4021                        Log.alarm("Allocation issue: expect to fill " + knownSideQtySplits[j]
4022                                + " at one price, but only got " + cur
4023                                + "; abort CP option leg trading");
4024                        return 0;
4025                    }
4026                }
4027                return allocatedQty;
4028            }
4029            else if (oppoSideSplits == knownSideQtySplits.length)
4030            {
4031                return allocatedQty;
4032            }
4033            else
4034            {
4035                Log.alarm("Allocation issue: expect to fill at " + knownSideQtySplits.length
4036                        + " price levels, but got " + oppoSideSplits);
4037                return 0;
4038            }
4039        }
4040        else
4041        {
4042            Log.alarm("Allocation issue: expect to fill " + quantityToAllocate + ", but only got "
4043                    + allocatedQty);
4044           return 0;
4045        }
4046    }

4115    private int internalCreateRegularTrade(Tradable tradable, Enumeration sameSideMarkets,

4144        int oppositeAllocatedQuantity = createParticipantLists(oppositeParticipantLists,
4145                tradePrices, tradeQuantities, preferredFirmAcronym, preferredFirmExchange,
4146                aProduct, book, otherSide, endingPrice, quantityToAllocate, false,
4147                needsSingleFillOnly, treatedLikeCustomerTrade, tradable, false);
4148 
4149        if (oppositeAllocatedQuantity > 0)
4150        {
4151            ArrayList sameParticipantLists = new ArrayList();
4152 
4153            // now allocate and check if the same side can allocate the quantity to match the
4154            // opposite side allocated
4155            int sameSideAllocatedQuantity = createParticipantLists(sameParticipantLists,
4156                    tradePrices, tradeQuantities, tradable, sameSideMarkets,
4157                    oppositeAllocatedQuantity, aProduct.getTradingClass());
4158 
4159                if (sameSideAllocatedQuantity == oppositeAllocatedQuantity)
4160                {
4161                    allocatedQuantity = sameSideAllocatedQuantity;
4162                }
4163 
4164                if (allocatedQuantity > 0)
4165                {
4166                // If tradableIsBooked or other orders from the book are used, then update both
4167                // sides of the book otherwised just update the opposite side.
4168                Side updatedSide = (tradableIsBooked == true || sameSideMarkets != null)
4169                        ? null
4170                        : otherSide;
4171                    // Determine if the tradable we are allocating is booked or not. If not booked,
4172                    // the
4173                // order book will need to ignore it when unbooking tradables
4174                Tradable unBookedTradable = (tradableIsBooked == true)
4175                        ? null
4176                        : tradable;
4177 
4178                    verifyAonTradePrice(oppositeParticipantLists, sameParticipantLists, tradePrices, tradable);
4179 
4180                    completeTrades(unBookedTradable, tradeType, tradeType,
4181                            otherSide.getOtherSide(), sameParticipantLists,
4182                            oppositeParticipantLists, tradePrices, tradeQuantities, book,
4183                            updatedSide, (TradeReport) null);
4184 
4185                    tradeHappened = true;
4186                }
4187            }
4188        }
4189        finally
4190        {
4191            if (!tradeHappened)
4192            {
4193                OrderBookPriceDetailUndoLog.undoChange();
4194            }
4195            else
4196            {
4197                OrderBookPriceDetailUndoLog.clear();
4198            }
4199        }
4200 
4201        return  allocatedQuantity;
4202    }

4252            throws SpreadProcessingException, DataValidationException, SystemException

4258    protected void completeTrades(Tradable unBookedTradable, char tradeType,
4259            char settlementTradeType, Side sameSide, ArrayList sameSideLists,
4260            ArrayList oppoSideLists, ArrayList prices, ArrayList quantities, OrderBook book,
4261            Side updateSide, TradeReport parent) throws SpreadProcessingException,
4262            DataValidationException, SystemException
4263        {
4264        //            first validate that both lists are same size
4265            int tradeCount = sameSideLists.size();
4266        if (oppoSideLists.size() != tradeCount || prices.size() != tradeCount
4267                || quantities.size() != tradeCount)
4268        {
4269                throw new IllegalArgumentException("all ArrayLists must have same number of elements");
4270            }
4271 
4272        if (tradeCount == 0)
4273        {
4274            return;
4275        }
4276 
4277        boolean success = false;
4278        try
4279        {
4280            Transaction.startTransaction();
4281 
4282            TradeReport[] reports = new TradeReport[sameSideLists.size()];
4283            boolean isTBForCOB = false;
4284            if (null != unBookedTradable
4285                                && unBookedTradable.isTradable(TradableTypes.ORDER)
4286                                && ((Order) unBookedTradable).isTBForCOB()) {
4287                isTBForCOB = true;
4288            }
4289 
4290        //            now actually create the trades
4291        for (int i = 0; i < sameSideLists.size(); i++)
4292        {
4293            ParticipantList nextSame = (ParticipantList) sameSideLists.get(i);
4294            ParticipantList nextOppo = (ParticipantList) oppoSideLists.get(i);
4295 
4296            Price tradePrice = (Price) prices.get(i);
4297 
4298 
4299            reports[i] = tradeMatch(book.getTradingProduct(), tradeType, settlementTradeType,
4300                    (sameSide.isBuySide() || sameSide.isAsDefinedSide())
4301                            ? nextSame
4302                            : nextOppo, (sameSide.isBuySide() || sameSide.isAsDefinedSide())
4303                            ? nextOppo
4304                            : nextSame, tradePrice, parent, isTBForCOB);
4305       if(!book.getTradingProduct().isBuyWrite())
4306            {
4307            if (parent == null)
4308                reports[i].completeTrade(true, unBookedTradable);
4309            else
4310                parent.setLastestAddedChildTradeReports(reports);
4311                }
4312        }
4313            success = Transaction.commit();
4314        }
4315        finally
4316        {
4317            if (!success)
4318            {
4319                Transaction.rollback();
4320            }
4321        }
4322        }

4324    /**
4325     * This method will create trade for the given tradable against the given list of tradables.
4326     * Assumptions:- All trades will be at one price, that will be price of tradable. Trade quantity
4327     * will be lesser of 'availabel qty' for tradable OR 'available qty' for all the tradables on
4328     * opposite side.
4329     * 
4330     * @param tradable - Order which needs to be traded against the customer orders which need
4331     * satisfaction. OR B. Inbound Satisfaction Order.
4332     * @param oppositeSideTradables - Tradebles on the opposite side. A. customer order needs
4333     * satisfaction OR B. MM orders to be traded with inbound Satisfaction order.
4334     * @param book
4335     * @param maxAllowedQuantity - Max quantity which should get traded.
4336     * @param needsBookUpdate - If order book needs to be updated or not.A. true for
4337     * customerOrderSatisfy B. false when inbound S order tradeWithCrowd
4338     * @return quantity traded
4339     * @throws SpreadProcessingException
4340     * @throws DataValidationException
4341     * @throws SystemException
4342     */
4343    public int createSatisfactionOrderTrade(Tradable tradable, Enumeration oppositeSideTradables,
4344            OrderBook book, int maxAllowedQuantity, boolean needsBookUpdate)
4345            throws SpreadProcessingException, DataValidationException, SystemException
4346    {
4347        if (Log.isDebugOn())
4348        {
4349            Log.debug(this, "Creating trade for Satisfaction order.");
4350        }
4351 
4352        ArrayList tradableSideList = new ArrayList();
4353        ArrayList oppositeSideList = new ArrayList();
4354        ArrayList priceList = new ArrayList();
4355        ArrayList quantities = new ArrayList();
4356        Side tradableSide;
4357        int tradeQuantity = 0;
4358 
4359        tradableSide = tradable.getSide();
4360 
4361        // Create Opposite side participant list.
4362        int oppositeSideQuantity = createParticipantListForSatisfaction(oppositeSideList,
4363                oppositeSideTradables, maxAllowedQuantity);
4364 
4365        tradeQuantity = (oppositeSideQuantity < maxAllowedQuantity)
4366                ? oppositeSideQuantity
4367                : maxAllowedQuantity;
4368 
4369        // Create tradableside Participant list
4370        ParticipantList tradableParticipantList = new ParticipantListImpl();
4371        createParticipantItem(tradable, tradeQuantity, tradableParticipantList);
4372        tradableSideList.add(tradableParticipantList);
4373 
4374        quantities.add(new Integer(tradeQuantity));
4375        priceList.add(tradable.getPrice());
4376 
4377        if (tradableSide.isBuySide())
4378        {
4379            completeSatisfactionTrades(tradable, tradableSideList, oppositeSideList, priceList,
4380                    quantities, book, tradableSide.getOtherSide()/* side to be updated */,
4381                    needsBookUpdate);
4382        }
4383        else
4384        {
4385            completeSatisfactionTrades(tradable, oppositeSideList, tradableSideList, priceList,
4386                    quantities, book, tradableSide.getOtherSide()/* side to be updated */,
4387                    needsBookUpdate);
4388        }
4389        return tradeQuantity;
4390    }

4396     * @param sellLists

4399     * @param book

4405    protected void completeSatisfactionTrades(Tradable unBookedTradable, ArrayList buyLists,
4406            ArrayList sellLists, ArrayList prices, ArrayList quantities, OrderBook book, Side side,
4407            boolean needsBookUpdated) throws SpreadProcessingException, DataValidationException,
4408            SystemException
4409    {
4410        // first validate that both lists are same size
4411        int tradeCount = buyLists.size();
4412        if (sellLists.size() != tradeCount || prices.size() != tradeCount
4413                || quantities.size() != tradeCount)

4433    /**
4434     */
4435    private int createParticipantListForSatisfaction(ArrayList oppositeSideList,
4436            Enumeration oppositeSideTradables, int tradableQuantity)
4437    {
4438        ParticipantListImpl oppositeParticipantList = new ParticipantListImpl();
4439        int tradedQuantity = 0;
4440        int qty = 0;
4441        int remainingQty = tradableQuantity;
4442        Tradable oppositeTradable;
4443        while (oppositeSideTradables.hasMoreElements() && tradedQuantity < tradableQuantity)
4444        {
4445            oppositeTradable = (Tradable) oppositeSideTradables.nextElement();
4446            qty = (oppositeTradable.getQuantityAllowed() < remainingQty)
4447                    ? oppositeTradable.getQuantityAllowed()
4448                    : remainingQty;
4449 
4450            tradedQuantity += qty;
4451            remainingQty -= qty;
4452 
4453            if (qty != 0)
4454            {
4455                createParticipantItem(oppositeTradable, qty, oppositeParticipantList);
4456            }
4457        }
4458 
4459        oppositeSideList.add(oppositeParticipantList);
4460 
4461        return tradedQuantity;
4462    }
4463 
4464    /**
4465     * Gets next tradable TODO: before this method, oppositeSideMarkets is always called
4466     * sameSideMarkets which one is correct???
4467     */
4468    private Tradable getNextTradable(Tradable currentTradable, Enumeration oppositeSideMarkets,
4469            Tradable lastTradable, int quantityRemaining, TradingClass tradingClass)
4470    {
4471 
4472        if (lastTradable == null && oppositeSideMarkets == null)
4473        {
4474            return null;
4475        }
4476        if (lastTradable != null && currentTradable == lastTradable)
4477        {
4478            return null;
4479        }
4480 
4481        while (oppositeSideMarkets != null && oppositeSideMarkets.hasMoreElements())
4482        {
4483                        Tradable nextTradable = (Tradable) oppositeSideMarkets.nextElement();
4484            if (getMinQuantity(tradingClass, nextTradable) <= quantityRemaining)
4485            {
4486                                return nextTradable;
4487                        }
4488                }
4489        if (lastTradable != null && getMinQuantity(tradingClass, lastTradable) <= quantityRemaining)
4490        {
4491                        return lastTradable;
4492                }
4493                return null;
4494        }

4496        /**
4497         * Creates a <code>ParticipantItem</code> for the <code>Tradable</code> and adds it to the
4498         * appropriate <code>ParticipantList</code>.  Note that a <code>ParticipantItem</code> will only
4499         * be created if the quantity is greater than 0.
4500         *
4501         * @param tradable                Tradable to have create item for
4502         * @param quantity                quantity being traded
4503         * @param participants        ParticipantList for item
4504         * @since Increment 4
4505         */
4506    private void createParticipantItem(Tradable tradable, int quantity, ParticipantList participants)
4507    {

4509        {
4510                        ParticipantItem tradableItem = new ParticipantItemImpl(tradable, quantity);
4511                        participants.addElement(tradableItem);
4512                }

4515    /**
4516     * Allocate spread tradables based on the price and quantityRequested. Return allocated
4517     * quantity. The allocated quantity may be less than or equal to the quantityRequested. When if
4518     * less, it is because 1. there may be not enough quantity in the book to be allocated. 2. there
4519     * may be contingent tradables whose contingent quantities can not be satisfied by
4520     * quantityRequested
4521     */
4522    protected int allocateSpreadTradables(ParticipantList list, OrderBook anOrderBook,
4523            Price tradePrice, Side sideOfAllocation, int quantityRequested)
4524    {
4525                int remainingQuantity = quantityRequested;
4526                PriorityTradableSet nextSet;
4527        AllocationTradeContextImpl allocationContext;
4528        Iterator prioritySets;
4529        allocationContext = new AllocationTradeContextImpl(AllocationTradeTypes.REGULAR);
4530        prioritySets = anOrderBook.getPrioritySets(sideOfAllocation, tradePrice, quantityRequested,
4531                allocationContext);
4532        while (remainingQuantity > 0 && prioritySets.hasNext())
4533        {
4534                        nextSet = (PriorityTradableSet) prioritySets.next();
4535                        remainingQuantity -= nextSet.allocate(list, remainingQuantity);
4536                        nextSet.resetElements();
4537                }
4538        return quantityRequested - remainingQuantity;
4539        }

4546     */
4547    protected int getAvailableQuantity(TradingClass aTradingClass, Tradable tradable)

4557    protected int getAdjustedQuantityForVolumeContingency(OrderBook book, Tradable tradable,

4576    /**

4583    protected boolean hasBookVolumeContingency(OrderBook book, Tradable tradable)

4599    /**

4601     * actual min quantity for this implementation. The Stock subclass will redifine this method in

4605    protected int getMinQuantity(TradingClass aTradingClass, Tradable tradable)
4606    {
4607        return tradable.getMinQuantity();
4608    }

4610    /**
4611     * Creates Lists of ParticipantList from the tradable and its same side market tradables based
4612     * on the allocated price and quantity from the other side

4618     * @param sameSideMarkets                            other tradables in the same side

4622    protected int createParticipantLists(ArrayList outputParticipantList,
4623            ArrayList inputTradePrices, ArrayList inputTradeQuantityList, Tradable tradable,
4624            Enumeration sameSideMarkets, int quantityAllocateFromOpposite, TradingClass tradingClass)

4631    /**
4632     * Creates Lists of ParticipantList from the tradable and its same side market tradables based
4633     * on the allocated price and quantity from the other side
4634     *
4635     * @param outputParticipantList     list of <code> ParticipantList</code> to be created
4636     * @param inputTradePrices                list of trade prices for each ParticipantList to be created
4637     * @param inputTradeQuantityList        list of trade quantities for each ParticipantList to be created
4638     * @param tradable                            the tradable
4639     * @param sameSideMarkets                            other tradables in the same side
4640     * @param quantityAllocateFromOpposite                total quantity allocate from the opposite side
4641     * @param allcoateSameSideBookFirst a flag to indicate to allocate to the markets exisiting in
4642     * the order book first
4643     * @return total allocated quantity for this side
4644     */
4645    public int createParticipantLists(ArrayList outputParticipantList, ArrayList inputTradePrices,
4646            ArrayList inputTradeQuantityList, Tradable tradable, Enumeration sameSideMarkets,
4647            int quantityAllocateFromOpposite, TradingClass tradingClass,
4648            boolean allcoateSameSideBookFirst)
4649    {
4650        Tradable currentTradable = null;
4651        int unallocatedTradableQuantity = 0;
4652        int sameAllocated = 0;
4653        int remainingQuantity = quantityAllocateFromOpposite;
4654        for (int i = 0; i < inputTradeQuantityList.size() && remainingQuantity > 0; i++)
4655        {
4656            // Price oppositePrice = (Price) inputTradePrices.get(i);
4657            int currentQuantity = ((Integer) inputTradeQuantityList.get(i)).intValue();
4658            ParticipantList currentSame = new ParticipantListImpl();
4659            while (currentQuantity > 0)
4660            {
4661                if (unallocatedTradableQuantity == 0)
4662                {
4663                    if (allcoateSameSideBookFirst)
4664                    {
4665                        currentTradable = getNextTradable(currentTradable, sameSideMarkets,
4666                                tradable, remainingQuantity, tradingClass);
4667                    }
4668                    else
4669                    {
4670                        currentTradable = getNextTradableFromCurrent(currentTradable,
4671                                sameSideMarkets, tradable, remainingQuantity, tradingClass);
4672                    }
4673                    if (currentTradable == null)
4674                    {
4675                        // We ran out of quantity on the new tradable side so we want to break out
4676                        // of the loop.
4677                        remainingQuantity = 0;
4678                        break;
4679                    }
4680                    unallocatedTradableQuantity = getAvailableQuantity(tradingClass,
4681                            currentTradable);
4682                }
4683                int currentAllocation;
4684                if (unallocatedTradableQuantity > currentQuantity)
4685                {
4686                    currentAllocation = currentQuantity;
4687                }
4688                else
4689                {
4690                    currentAllocation = unallocatedTradableQuantity;
4691                }
4692                createParticipantItem(currentTradable, currentAllocation, currentSame);
4693                unallocatedTradableQuantity -= currentAllocation;
4694                currentQuantity -= currentAllocation;
4695                remainingQuantity -= currentAllocation;
4696                sameAllocated += currentAllocation;
4697            }
4698 
4699            outputParticipantList.add(currentSame);
4700        }
4701        return sameAllocated;
4702    }

4710            String preferredFirmSession = TradingSessionNameHelper

4725    protected List getPreferredFirmAcronym(Tradable tradable)
4726    {

4730        {

4733            {

4735                {

4739

4741                        break;

4744 
4745                    if (preferredFirmAcronym == null || preferredFirmAcronym.size() == 0)
4746                            break;

4748                            + ") Order(" + thisOrder + ")");
4749                } while (false);
4750            }
4751            catch (Exception ex)

4754                        + ") exception: " + ex);
4755            }
4756        }
4757

4759    }

4761    /**
4762     * Creates Lists of ParticipantList, trade prices and trade quantity for each price to
4763     * participant in trade using the book for tradables have price better than the ending price

4774     * @param quantityToAllocate                total quantity to allocate
4775     * @return         total allocated quantity
4776     */
4777    private int createParticipantLists(ArrayList outputParticipantList,
4778            ArrayList outputTradePrices, ArrayList outputTradeQuantityList,
4779            List preferredFirmAcronym, String preferredFirmExchange, TradingProduct aProduct,
4780            OrderBook book, Side tradableSide, Price endingPrice, int quantityToAllocate,
4781            boolean nonQTrade, boolean needsSingleFillOnly, boolean treatedLikeCustomerTrade,
4782            Tradable tradable, boolean nonContingency)
4783    {
4784        int allocatedQuantity = 0;
4785        ParticipantList currentOpposite = null;
4786        Price currentPrice = new NoPrice();
4787        int allocatedAtCurrentPrice = 0;
4788        AllocationTradeContextImpl allocationContext;
4789        Iterator sets;
4790 
4791        int legRatio = 1;
4792 
4793        if(tradable!=null && !aProduct.isStrategy())
4794        {
4795                legRatio = calculateLegRatio(tradable.getProductKey(), aProduct.getProductKey());
4796        }
4797 
4798        // setting up the required details in allocation context
4799        allocationContext = new AllocationTradeContextImpl(AllocationTradeTypes.REGULAR);
4800        allocationContext.setNonQAllocation(nonQTrade);
4801        allocationContext.setTreatedLikeCustomerAllocation(treatedLikeCustomerTrade);
4802        allocationContext.setNonContingencyAllocation(nonContingency);
4803 
4804        //Setting the preferred firm in allocation context.
4805        if(tradable != null && !(preferredFirmAcronym != null && preferredFirmAcronym.size() > 0))
4806        {
4807                preferredFirmAcronym = getPreferredFirmAcronym(tradable);
4808                allocationContext.setQtyForPmmAllocation(tradable.getQuantityAllowed()*legRatio);
4809        }
4810 
4811        //Setting the preferred firm in allocation context.
4812        if(tradable != null && !(preferredFirmAcronym != null && preferredFirmAcronym.size() > 0))
4813        {
4814                preferredFirmAcronym = getPreferredFirmAcronym(tradable);
4815                allocationContext.setQtyForPmmAllocation(tradable.getQuantityAllowed()*legRatio);
4816        }
4817 
4818        allocationContext.setTradable(tradable);
4819        
4820        if (preferredFirmAcronym != null && preferredFirmAcronym.size() != 0)
4821        {
4822            allocationContext.setPreferredFirm(preferredFirmAcronym);
4823                            if (preferredFirmExchange == null || preferredFirmExchange.length() == 0)

4825                                preferredFirmExchange = "CBOE";
4826                            }
4827 
4828                }
4829 
4830        sets = book.getPrioritySets(tradableSide, endingPrice, quantityToAllocate,
4831                allocationContext);

4833        {
4834            PriorityTradableSet nextSet = (PriorityTradableSet) sets.next();
4835            if (nextSet.getPrice() != currentPrice && !currentPrice.isNoPrice()
4836                    && needsSingleFillOnly)
4837            {
4838                break;
4839            }
4840            else if (nextSet.getPrice() != currentPrice)
4841            {
4842                // The first time through, currentPrice will be a NoPrice.
4843                // If this is not the first time through, we have hit a new price that we
4844                // need to allocate quantity for, so we save the last price information.
4845                if (!currentPrice.isNoPrice())
4846                {
4847                    outputTradePrices.add(TradeHelper.determineTradePrice(tradableSide,
4848                            currentPrice, aProduct));
4849                    outputTradeQuantityList.add(new Integer(allocatedAtCurrentPrice));
4850                    outputParticipantList.add(currentOpposite);
4851                }
4852                // get ready to allocate quantity at a new price.
4853                currentOpposite = new ParticipantListImpl();
4854                currentPrice = nextSet.getPrice();
4855                allocatedAtCurrentPrice = 0;
4856            }
4857            int nextAllocatedQuantity = nextSet.allocate(currentOpposite, quantityToAllocate
4858                    - allocatedQuantity);
4859            allocatedQuantity += nextAllocatedQuantity;
4860            allocatedAtCurrentPrice += nextAllocatedQuantity;
4861        }
4862        if (allocatedQuantity > 0)
4863        {
4864            // If we were able to find opposite side quantity, we now need to create corresponding
4865            // participant lists for the same side tradables (the new one and any we are trading
4866            // ahead)
4867            outputTradePrices.add(TradeHelper.determineTradePrice(tradableSide, currentPrice,
4868                    aProduct));
4869            outputTradeQuantityList.add(new Integer(allocatedAtCurrentPrice));
4870            outputParticipantList.add(currentOpposite);
4871        }
4872 
4873        return allocatedQuantity;

5016    /**

5018     * locked Quotes and allocate trade quantity to participant in trade using the book for Q like
