5026     * @param book                      the order book
5027     * @param participantsSide                        side for participants
5028     * @param endingPrice                        crossing end price for each tradable to be able to trade on
5029     * @param quantityToAllocate                total quantity to allocate
5030     * @return         total allocated quantity
5031     */
5032    private int createParticipantListsOfQuoteLockMinTrade(ArrayList outputParticipantList,
5033            ArrayList outputTradePrices, ArrayList outputTradeQuantityList,
5034            TradingProduct aProduct, OrderBook book, Side participantsSide, Price endingPrice,
5035                                    int quantityToAllocate)
5036    {
5037        int allocatedQuantity = 0;
5038        ParticipantList currentOpposite = null;
5039        Price currentPrice = new NoPrice();
5040        int allocatedAtCurrentPrice = 0;
5041        AllocationTradeContextImpl allocationContext;
5042        Iterator sets;
5043        allocationContext = new AllocationTradeContextImpl(
5044                AllocationTradeTypes.QUOTE_LOCK_MIN_TRADE);
5045        allocationContext.setQAllocation(true);
5046        allocationContext.setNonContingencyAllocation(true);
5047        sets = book.getPrioritySets(participantsSide, endingPrice, quantityToAllocate,
5048                allocationContext);
5049        while (sets.hasNext() && allocatedQuantity < quantityToAllocate)
5050        {
5051            PriorityTradableSet nextSet = (PriorityTradableSet) sets.next();
5052            if (nextSet.getPrice() != currentPrice)
5053            {
5054                // The first time through, currentPrice will be a NoPrice.
5055                // If this is not the first time through, we have hit a new price that we
5056                // need to allocate quantity for, so we save the last price information.
5057                if (!currentPrice.isNoPrice())
5058                {
5059                    outputTradePrices.add(TradeHelper.determineTradePrice(participantsSide,
5060                            currentPrice, aProduct));
5061                    outputTradeQuantityList.add(new Integer(allocatedAtCurrentPrice));
5062                    outputParticipantList.add(currentOpposite);
5063                }
5064                // get ready to allocate quantity at a new price.
5065                currentOpposite = new ParticipantListImpl();
5066                currentPrice = nextSet.getPrice();
5067                allocatedAtCurrentPrice = 0;
5068            }
5069            int nextAllocatedQuantity = nextSet.allocate(currentOpposite, quantityToAllocate
5070                    - allocatedQuantity);
5071            allocatedQuantity += nextAllocatedQuantity;
5072            allocatedAtCurrentPrice += nextAllocatedQuantity;
5073        }
5074        if (allocatedQuantity > 0)
5075        {
5076            outputTradePrices.add(TradeHelper.determineTradePrice(participantsSide, currentPrice,
5077                    aProduct));
5078            outputTradeQuantityList.add(new Integer(allocatedAtCurrentPrice));
5079            outputParticipantList.add(currentOpposite);
5080        }
5081 
5082        return allocatedQuantity;
5083    }
5084 
5085    /**
5086     * Creates a <code>ParticipantList</code> for a trade at the given price and quantity on the
5087     * given side. The <code>ParticipantItem</code>s in the list will need to be matched with
5088     * <code>ParticipantItem</code>s on the opposite side in order for the trade to be complete.
5089     * 
5090     */
5091 
5092    private ParticipantList createParticipantListForOpening(OrderBook currentOrderBook,
5093            Side tradableSide, Price tradePrice, int tradeQuantity)
5094    {
5095        ParticipantList participants = new ParticipantListImpl();
5096        int allocatedQuantity = 0;
5097        AllocationTradeContext allocationContext = new AllocationTradeContextImpl(
5098                AllocationTradeTypes.OPENING);
5099        Iterator sets = currentOrderBook.getPrioritySets(tradableSide, tradePrice, tradeQuantity,
5100                allocationContext);
5101        PriorityTradableSet nextSet = null;
5102        int nextAllocatedQuantity = 0;
5103        ParticipantList currentList = null;
5104 
5105        while (sets.hasNext() && allocatedQuantity < tradeQuantity)
5106        {
5107            nextSet = (PriorityTradableSet) sets.next();
5108 
5109            currentList = new ParticipantListImpl();
5110            nextAllocatedQuantity = nextSet
5111                    .allocate(currentList, tradeQuantity - allocatedQuantity);
5112            allocatedQuantity += nextAllocatedQuantity;
5113 
5114            // add to the same list since it will be traded all at the same openingPrice
5115            addParticipantToList(currentList, participants);
5116        }
5117 
5118        return participants;
5119    }
5120 
5121    private void addParticipantToList(ParticipantList fromList, ParticipantList toList)
5122    {
5123        if (toList == null || fromList == null)
5124        {
5125            throw new IllegalArgumentException("The List trying to add is NULL");
5126        }
5127        Enumeration participantItemsEnum = fromList.elements();
5128 
5129        while (participantItemsEnum.hasMoreElements())
5130        {
5131            toList.addElement((ParticipantItem) participantItemsEnum.nextElement());
5132        }
5133 
5134    }
5135 
5136    /**
5137     * Creates a <code>ParticipantList</code> for a trade at the given price and quantity on the
5138     * given side. The <code>ParticipantItem</code>s in the list will need to be matched with
5139     * <code>ParticipantItem</code>s on the opposite side in order for the trade to be complete.
5140     * 
5141     */
5142    private ParticipantList createParticipantList(Tradable incomingMarketOrder,
5143            OrderBook currentOrderBook, Side tradableSide, Price tradePrice, int tradeQuantity,
5144            boolean allowContingencies, final boolean marketOrderTrade)
5145    {
5146        // If we receive an incoming market order we must verify it is a market
5147        // order AND the caller is invoking this method for a market order trade
5148        if (incomingMarketOrder != null)
5149        {
5150            if (!incomingMarketOrder.getPrice().isMarketPrice())
5151            {
5152                throw new IllegalArgumentException("method createParticipantList "
5153                        + "received incoming market tradable argument that is not "
5154                        + " a market order!");
5155            }
5156            if (!marketOrderTrade)
5157            {
5158                throw new IllegalArgumentException("method createParticipantList "
5159                        + "called with an incoming market order but marketOrderTrade "
5160                        + "flag is not set as true!");
5161            }
5162        }
5163        ParticipantList participants = new ParticipantListImpl();
5164        int remainingQuantity = tradeQuantity;
5165 
5166        Enumeration tradables;
5167        if (marketOrderTrade)
5168        {
5169            // We only want market orders.
5170            tradables = currentOrderBook.getTradables(tradableSide, PriceFactory
5171                    .create(Price.MARKET_STRING), true);
5172        }
5173        else
5174        {
5175            tradables = currentOrderBook.getTradables(tradableSide);
5176        }
5177 
5178        Tradable nextTradable;
5179        if (tradables.hasMoreElements())
5180        {
5181            nextTradable = (Tradable) tradables.nextElement();
5182        }
5183        else
5184        {
5185            nextTradable = incomingMarketOrder;
5186            incomingMarketOrder = null;
5187        }
5188 
5189        TradingClass tradingClass = currentOrderBook.getTradingProduct().getTradingClass();
5190 
5191        while (remainingQuantity > 0 && nextTradable != null)
5192        {
5193 
5194            // if this is a market order trade, verify the tradable is a market order!
5195            if (marketOrderTrade && !nextTradable.getPrice().isMarketPrice())
5196            {
5197                // If this happens, we've got a code problem.
5198                // The getTradables call on the order book above in this method is supposed
5199                // to be returning only market orders.  Here that didn't happen.
5200                throw new IllegalArgumentException(
5201                        "Invalid order for market order trade: Price is not MKT.");
5202            }
5203 
5204            // end search if current price is not better or equal to trade price
5205            if (!tradableSide.isFirstBetterOrEqual(nextTradable.getPrice(), tradePrice))
5206            {
5207                break;
5208            }
5209            // skip volume contingencies if they are either not allowed or cannot be satisfied by
5210            // the remaining
5211            // quantity.
5212            if (!nextTradable.hasVolumeContingency()
5213                    || (allowContingencies && getMinQuantity(tradingClass, nextTradable) <= remainingQuantity))
5214            {
5215                int tradableQuantity = getAvailableQuantity(tradingClass, nextTradable);
5216                if (tradableQuantity > remainingQuantity)
5217                {
5218                    tradableQuantity = remainingQuantity;
5219                }
5220                createParticipantItem(nextTradable, tradableQuantity, participants);
5221                remainingQuantity -= tradableQuantity;
5222            }
5223 
5224            if (tradables.hasMoreElements())
5225            {
5226                nextTradable = (Tradable) tradables.nextElement();
5227            }
5228            else
5229            {
5230                nextTradable = incomingMarketOrder;
5231                incomingMarketOrder = null;
5232            }
5233        }
5234        return participants;
5235    }
5236 
5237        /**
5238         * Creates trade report for spread product for matched tradables.
5239         *
5240         */
5241        private TradeReport doTradeMatchForSpread(TradingProduct tradingProduct, char tradeType, char settlementTradeType,
5242                        boolean heldOrderTrade, ParticipantList biders, ParticipantList askers, Price tradePrice, Tradable tradable, boolean isQualifiedContingentTrade, boolean isTBForCOB)
5243    throws SpreadProcessingException,
5244            DataValidationException, SystemException
5245    {
5246        // remove the doTradeMatch() call from here and move after calculateTradePricesForLegs()
5247        // call
5248        // TradeReport tradeReport = doTradeMatch(tradingProduct, heldOrderTrade, biders, askers,
5249        // tradePrice, null /* no parent report */);
5250        Side derivedTradeSide;
5251        StrategyLegTradePrice[] legPrices;
5252        if (biders.isRegularList() && askers.isRegularList())
5253        { // spread order trade with spread order
5254            derivedTradeSide = null;        /* value will not be used */
5255            
5256            //For QCT Trades, use a different leg trade price calculations.
5257            if(isQualifiedContingentTrade)
5258            {
5259                legPrices = calculateQCTTradePricesForLegs(biders, askers, tradePrice,
5260                        tradingProduct);
5261                validateQCTLegTradePrices(tradingProduct, legPrices);
5262                //Check if the leg trade prices are at or within NBBO
5263            }
5264            else//Non QCT Trade.
5265            {
5266                    legPrices = calculateTradePricesForLegs(biders, askers, tradePrice, tradingProduct, isTBForCOB);
5267            }
5268        }
5269        else if (biders.isDerivedList() && askers.isRegularList())
5270        {
5271            derivedTradeSide = SideFactory.getAsDefinedSide();
5272            legPrices = biders.getLegTradePrices();
5273        }
5274        else if (biders.isRegularList() && askers.isDerivedList())
5275        {
5276            derivedTradeSide = SideFactory.getOppositeSide();
5277            legPrices = askers.getLegTradePrices();
5278        }
5279        else
5280        {
5281            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(
5282                    "Unexpected combination of participant list types for trade", 0);
5283        }
5284        biders.setLegTradePrices(legPrices);
5285        askers.setLegTradePrices(legPrices);
5286 
5287        // moved the doTradeMatch (above) after calculating Trade Prices for Legs - bug fix
5288        // cboqa06887 and cboqa06809
5289        TradeReport tradeReport = doTradeMatch(tradingProduct, tradeType, settlementTradeType,
5290                heldOrderTrade, biders, askers, tradePrice, null /* no parent report */);
5291        if (tradingProduct.isBuyWrite())
5292        {
5293            AllocationContextImpl context = new AllocationContextImpl();
5294            generateTradeReportForLegs(biders, context, askers, tradeReport,
5295                    AuctionTypes.AUCTION_UNSPECIFIED);
5296        }
5297        else
5298        {
5299            ParticipantList[] bidLists;
5300            ParticipantList[] askLists;
5301            bidLists = biders.getListsForLegs(legPrices, derivedTradeSide, tradable);
5302            askLists = askers.getListsForLegs(legPrices, derivedTradeSide, tradable);
5303            Price[] tradePrices = getTradePricesFrom(legPrices);
5304            Side[] legSides = getLegSidesFrom(legPrices);
5305            TradingProduct[] tradingProducts = getTradingProductsFrom(legPrices);
5306            for (int i = 0; i < tradePrices.length; i++)
5307            {
5308                // need to reverse buy and sell list for legs that are being sold to keep buy and
5309                // sell
5310                // consistent
5311                // in matches
5312                if (legSides[i].isBuySide())
5313                {
5314                    doTradeMatch(tradingProducts[i], tradeType, settlementTradeType,
5315                            heldOrderTrade, bidLists[i], askLists[i], tradePrices[i], tradeReport);
5316                }
5317                else
5318                {
5319                    doTradeMatch(tradingProducts[i], tradeType, settlementTradeType,
5320                            heldOrderTrade, askLists[i], bidLists[i], tradePrices[i], tradeReport);
5321                }
5322                if (Log.isDebugOn())
5323                {
5324                    Log.debug("TradeServiceImpl.doTradeMatchForSpread>>Leg Product: "
5325                            + tradingProducts[i].getProductKey() + " Leg Trade Price is "
5326                            + tradePrices[i].toString());
5327                }
5328            }
5329        }
5330        return tradeReport;
5331    }
5332        
5333        
5334        /**
5335         * Do the following validations for leg Trade prices:
5336         * 1. Must be at or within NBBO.
5337         * 2. Must be better than customer on legs.
5338         * 3. Must be in standard incremental prices.
5339         * 
5340         * @param tradingProduct
5341         * @param legPrices
5342         * @throws DataValidationException
5343         * @throws SpreadProcessingException
5344         * @throws SystemException
5345         */
5346        protected void validateQCTLegTradePrices(TradingProduct tradingProduct, StrategyLegTradePrice[] legPrices) throws DataValidationException, SpreadProcessingException, SystemException
5347        {
5348                boolean isSTSEnabled = ((TradingProductImpl)tradingProduct).isRolledoutSpreadClass();
5349                NBBOStruct[] nbbo = null;
5350                // If sts is disabled, get the NBBO from tradingProduct, else do a quoteQuery to 
5351        if(!isSTSEnabled)
5352        {
5353                nbbo = new NBBOStruct[legPrices.length];
5354                for(int i = 0;i<legPrices.length;i++)
5355                {
5356                        nbbo[i] = legPrices[i].getTradingProduct().getNBBO(
5357                            tradingProduct.getTradingClass().getSessionName());
5358                }
5359        }
5360        else
5361                {
5362                        int[] legProductKeys = new int[legPrices.length];
5363                        for(int i =0;i<legPrices.length;i++)
5364                        {
5365                                legProductKeys[i] = legPrices[i].getProductKey();//Gathering the legProduct keys to enable one time quotequery.
5366                        }
5367                        MarketDataService mds = StrategyTradeServiceHelper.getMarketDataServiceRoutingHome().find();
5368                        QuoteQueryV3Struct[] quoteQueryV3Struct = null;
5369                        String sessionName = legPrices[0].getTradingProduct().getTradingClass().getSessionName();
5370                        try
5371                        {
5372                                quoteQueryV3Struct = mds.getQuoteQueryDataForProductsV3(sessionName, legProductKeys);
5373                        }
5374                        catch(Exception e)
5375                        {
5376                                Log.exception("Failed to get NBBO markets for session=" + sessionName
5377                                                      + "; product key=" + legPrices[0].getProductKey(), e);
5378                                      throw ExceptionBuilder.systemException("Failed to get NBBO markets for session=" + sessionName
5379                                                      + "; product key=" + legPrices[0].getProductKey(), 0);
5380                        }
5381                          nbbo = new NBBOStruct[quoteQueryV3Struct.length];
5382                                      for (int i = 0; i < quoteQueryV3Struct.length; i++)
5383                              {
5384                                              nbbo[i] = quoteQueryV3Struct[i].quoteQueryV2Struct.nbboStruct;
5385                              }
5386        }
5387        
5388                                      for(int i =0;i<legPrices.length;i++)
5389                        {
5390                                for(Price legTradePrice : legPrices[i].getTradePrices())
5391                                {
5392                         // 1. validate leg trade prices against nbbo
5393                                        if(!isAtOrWithinNBBO(legTradePrice, nbbo[i]))
5394                                        {
5395                                    throw new SpreadProcessingException(
5396                            "TradServiceImpl.doTradeMatchForSpreadQCT : QCT Leg Trade price "
5397                                                    + legTradePrice + " is outside NBBO ( "
5398                                                    + PriceFactory.create(nbbo[i].bidPrice) + " , "
5399                                    + PriceFactory.create(nbbo[i].askPrice) + " )  " +legPrices[i].getProductKey()+">>>",
5400                                                         SpreadProcessingException.AtLeastOneCalculatedLegPriceTouchesBook);
5401                                        }
5402                            //2. validate leg trade prices against resting customer
5403                            if(!isQCTLegTradePricesBetterThanCustomer(legTradePrice,legPrices[i].getProductKey()))
5404                        {
5405                                throw new SpreadProcessingException(
5406                            "TradServiceImpl.doTradeMatchForSpreadQCT : QCT Leg Trade price "
5407                                    + legPrices[i].getTradePrice() + " is worse than or equal to resting customer order price for the leg "+legPrices[i].getProductKey()+">>>",
5408                                     SpreadProcessingException.AtLeastOneCalculatedLegPriceTouchesBook);
5409                        }
5410                //3. Check if leg trade prices are standard increment prices for that leg.
5411                if(!isLegTradePriceStandardIncrementPriceForTheLeg(legTradePrice,legPrices[i].getTradingProduct().getTradingClass().getProductClassKey()))
5412                {
5413                        throw new SpreadProcessingException(
5414                            "TradServiceImpl.doTradeMatchForSpreadQCT : QCT Leg Trade price "
5415                                    + legPrices[i].getTradePrice() + " is not a standard incremental price for this leg"+ ") "+legPrices[i].getProductKey()+" >>>",
5416                            SpreadProcessingException.LegPricesCanNotBeCalculated);
5417                }
5418                    }
5419            }
5420        }
5421        
5422        /**
5423         * Compare leg price with customer price on legs. 
5424         * 
5425         * @param leg
5426         * @return
5427         * @throws DataValidationException
5428         */
5429        protected boolean isQCTLegTradePricesBetterThanCustomer(Price legTradePrice, int productKey) throws DataValidationException
5430        {
5431                OrderBook book  = null;
5432                boolean result = true;
5433                Price bidSideCustomerPrice = PriceFactory.create(Price.NO_PRICE_STRING);;
5434                Price askSideCustomerPrice = PriceFactory.create(Price.NO_PRICE_STRING);;
5435                try
5436                {
5437                        book = getOrderBook(productKey);
5438                }
5439                catch( DataValidationException e)
5440                {
5441                 Log.information("TradeServiceImpl.legPricesBetterThanRestingCustomerOrderOnLegs>>>>>" +
5442                                 " OrderBook not found for product"+productKey);  
5443                 throw new DataValidationException("TradeServiceImpl.legPricesBetterThanRestingCustomerOrderOnLegs>>>>>" +
5444                                         " OrderBook not found for product",e.details);
5445                }
5446                
5447                if(book.getBestCustomerOrderQuantity(SideFactory.getBuySide()) > 0)
5448                {
5449                        bidSideCustomerPrice  = book.getBestPrice(SideFactory.getBuySide());
5450                }
5451                if(book.getBestCustomerOrderQuantity(SideFactory.getSellSide()) > 0)
5452                {
5453                        askSideCustomerPrice  = book.getBestPrice(SideFactory.getSellSide());
5454                }
5455                
5456                if((!bidSideCustomerPrice.isNoPrice() && legTradePrice.lessThanOrEqual(bidSideCustomerPrice)) ||
5457                                (!askSideCustomerPrice.isNoPrice()&& legTradePrice.greaterThanOrEqual(askSideCustomerPrice)))
5458                {
5459                        result = false;
5460                }
5461            return result;
5462        }

5614            {
5615                for (int j = 0; j < legPrices[i].getSplitRatios().length; j++)
5616                {
5617                    tempList.add(legPrices[i].getTradingProduct());
5618                }
5619            }
5620            else
5621            {
5622                                tempList.add(legPrices[i].getTradingProduct());
5623                        }
5624                }
5625                TradingProduct[] products = new TradingProduct[tempList.size()];
5626                tempList.toArray(products);
5627                return products;

5862    /**
5863     * getTradeReportCollection
5864     * 
5865     * @param broker
5866     * @param firm
5867     * @param sessionName
5868     * @param beginTime <code>DateTimeStruct</code>
5869     * @param endTime   <code>DateTimeStruct</code>
5870     * @param buySellInd -flag to indicates buy or sell side
5871     * @param activeOnly -flag to indicates active reports only or not
5872     * @return TradeReportStructV2[]
5873     * @exception NotFoundException AuthorizationException, SystemException, CommunicationException
5874     *
5875     * Mei Wu
5876     */
5877    private TradeReport[] getTradeReportCollection(ExchangeAcronymStruct broker,
5878            ExchangeFirmStruct firm, int productKey, String sessionName, DateTimeStruct beginTime,
5879            DateTimeStruct endTime, char buySellInd, boolean activeOnly)
5880            throws AuthorizationException, NotFoundException, DataValidationException,
5881            SystemException, CommunicationException
5882    {
5883        TradingSessionStruct tradingSessionStruct = TradingSessionNameHelper
5884                .getSession(sessionName);
5885        if (tradingSessionStruct == null)
5886        {
5887            Log.alarm(this,
5888                    "getTradeReportCollection => getTradeReports query for invalid session name: "
5889                            + sessionName);
5890            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException("Invalid session name: " + sessionName,
5891                    DataValidationCodes.INVALID_SESSION);
5892        }
5893        if ((beginTime.date.year == 0 && endTime.date.year != 0)
5894                || (beginTime.date.year != 0 && endTime.date.year == 0))
5895        {
5896            String msg  =  "Invalid begin/end dates: both begin and end time must be present or 0s";
5897            Log.alarm(this, "getTradeReportCollection => " + msg);
5898            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(msg, DataValidationCodes.INVALID_TIME);
5899        }
5900        else if (beginTime.date.year == 0 && endTime.date.year == 0)
5901        {
5902            // get the trade report from the start time of the current session to end time of the
5903            // session
5904            DateWrapper dateWrapper = new DateWrapper();
5905            dateWrapper.setTime(tradingSessionStruct.startTime);
5906            beginTime = dateWrapper.toDateTimeStruct();
5907            dateWrapper.setTime(tradingSessionStruct.endTime);
5908            endTime = dateWrapper.toDateTimeStruct();
5909        }
5910 
5911        // ensure that this trade service is configured to accept trades for this
5912        // session by getting the strategy for the session name
5913        // DataValidationException is thrown if an error occurs.
5914 
5915        // use default product type 0, to get a generic tradeValidationStrategy to validate the
5916        // trade report query
5917        // for real trade, we need to pass a meaning productType to get an appropriate trade
5918        // validation strategy
5919        getTradeValidationStrategy(sessionName, 0);
5920        validateFirm(firm);
5921        if (!broker.acronym.equals("") || !broker.exchange.equals(""))
5922        {
5923            validateUser(broker); // broker is optional in this call.
5924        }
5925        validateProduct(productKey);
5926        TradeReport[] reports = null;
5927        try
5928        {
5929            reports = getTradeReportHome().findTradeReports(broker, firm, productKey, sessionName,
5930                    beginTime, endTime, buySellInd, activeOnly);
5931        }
5932        finally
5933        {
5934            if (reports == null)
5935            {
5936                reports = new TradeReport[0];
5937            }
5938        }
5939        return reports;
5940    }
5941 
5942    private void validateFirm(ExchangeFirmStruct firm) throws DataValidationException,
5943            AuthorizationException, CommunicationException, SystemException
5944    {
5945        try
5946        {
5947            getFirmMaintenanceService().getFirmByNumber(firm);
5948        }
5949        catch (NotFoundException e)
5950        {

6047    /**
6048     * creat a pending trade for the quote trigger
6049     */
6050    public int createPendingTrade(OrderBook book, QuoteTriggerTradable aQuoteTrigger)
6051            throws SpreadProcessingException, DataValidationException, SystemException
6052    {
6053        int allocatedQuantity = 0;
6054        boolean success = false;
6055        boolean isStrategy = book.getTradingProduct().isStrategy();
6056 
6057        try
6058        {
6059            Transaction.startTransaction();
6060 
6061            Side otherSide = aQuoteTrigger.getSide().getOtherSide();
6062            int quantityToAllocate = aQuoteTrigger.getQuantityAllowed();
6063            Price triggerPrice = aQuoteTrigger.getNonQPrice();
6064            Price localTradePrice = triggerPrice;
6065            TradingProduct aProduct = book.getTradingProduct();
6066            ArrayList nonQParticipantLists = new ArrayList();
6067            ArrayList tradePrices = new ArrayList();
6068            ArrayList tradeQuantities = new ArrayList();
6069            int nonQAllocatedQuantity = createParticipantLists(nonQParticipantLists, tradePrices,
6070                    tradeQuantities, getPreferredFirmAcronym(aQuoteTrigger),
6071                    getPreferredFirmExchange(aQuoteTrigger), aProduct, book, otherSide,
6072                    triggerPrice, quantityToAllocate, true, false, false, null, false);
6073            if (nonQAllocatedQuantity > 0)
6074            {
6075                ArrayList triggerParticipantLists = new ArrayList();
6076                int triggerSideAllocatedQuantity = createParticipantLists(triggerParticipantLists,
6077                        tradePrices, tradeQuantities, aQuoteTrigger, null, nonQAllocatedQuantity,
6078                        aProduct.getTradingClass());
6079                if (triggerSideAllocatedQuantity != nonQAllocatedQuantity)
6080                {
6081                    allocatedQuantity = 0;
6082                }
6083                else
6084                {
6085                    allocatedQuantity = triggerSideAllocatedQuantity;
6086                    Tradable unBookedTradable = aQuoteTrigger;
6087                    QuoteTriggerTradeReport aTradeReport = aQuoteTrigger.getPendingTradeReport();
6088                    if (aTradeReport == null)
6089                    {
6090                        if (aQuoteTrigger.isAsDefinedSide())
6091                        {
6092                            double value = -1 * localTradePrice.toDouble();
6093                            localTradePrice = PriceFactory.create(value);
6094                        }
6095 
6096                        aTradeReport = getTradeReportHome().createQuoteTriggerTradeReport(aProduct,
6097                                localTradePrice, aQuoteTrigger.getSide(), myIdService);
6098                        aQuoteTrigger.setPendingTradeReport(aTradeReport);
6099                    }
6100                    // 12/11/04, need to publish ticker/last sale for spread legs at time of quote
6101                    // trigger creation
6102                    if (isStrategy)
6103                    {
6104                        saveLegPricesAtQTCreation(book, aTradeReport, aQuoteTrigger);
6105                    }
6106                    aTradeReport.addTrade(triggerParticipantLists, nonQParticipantLists,
6107                            tradePrices, tradeQuantities, unBookedTradable);
6108                }
6109            }
6110 
6111            if (allocatedQuantity > 0)
6112            {
6113                success = Transaction.commit();
6114            }
6115            else
6116            {
6117                Transaction.rollback();
6118                success = true;
6119            }
6120        }
6121        finally
6122        {
6123            if (!success)
6124            {
6125                Log.alarm(this, "createPendingTrade failed for " + aQuoteTrigger.toString() + ".");
6126                Transaction.rollback();
6127            }
6128        }
6129        return  allocatedQuantity;
6130    }
6131 
6132    /*
6133     * UD 12/15/04 calculate the leg prices at time of QT creation and save them in
6134     * QuoteTriggerTradable.
6135    */
6136    private void saveLegPricesAtQTCreation(OrderBook book, QuoteTriggerTradeReport aTradeReport,
6137            QuoteTriggerTradable aQuoteTrigger) throws DataValidationException,
6138            SpreadProcessingException, SystemException
6139    {
6140        StrategyLegTradePrice[] strategyLegTradePrices;
6141        aTradeReport.prepareForCompletion();
6142        Side derivedTradeSide = null;
6143        Price localTradePrice = aQuoteTrigger.getNonQPrice();
6144        if (aQuoteTrigger.isAsDefinedSide())
6145        {
6146            double value = -1 * localTradePrice.toDouble();
6147            localTradePrice = PriceFactory.create(value);
6148        }
6149        strategyLegTradePrices = getLegPrices(book.getTradingProduct(), localTradePrice,
6150                aTradeReport.getBidList(), aTradeReport.getAskList(), derivedTradeSide);
6151        Price[] tradePricesOfLegs = getTradePricesFrom(strategyLegTradePrices);
6152        // Following introduced when noticed that if a split occurs num(Prices) >
6153        // num(strategyLegTradePrices)
6154        // Currently, its commented out based on decision that tickValue(strategy) will not be less
6155        // than tickValue(legs)
6156//       TradingProduct[] tradingProducts = getTradingProductsFrom(strategyLegTradePrices);
6157//       aTradeReport.setTradingProductsFromLegTradePrices(tradingProducts);
6158        Side[] legSides = getLegSidesFrom(strategyLegTradePrices);
6159        aTradeReport.setStrategyLegTradePrices(strategyLegTradePrices);
6160        aTradeReport.setTradePricesOfLegs(tradePricesOfLegs);
6161        aTradeReport.setSidesOfLegs(legSides);
6162        aTradeReport.setDerivedTradeSide(derivedTradeSide);
6163    }

6165    /**
6166     * complete the pending trade for QuoteTrigger
6167     */
6168    public void completePendingTrade(OrderBook book, QuoteTriggerTradable aQuoteTrigger)
6169            throws DataValidationException, SystemException
6170    {
6171        try
6172        {
6173            internalCompletePendingTrade(book, aQuoteTrigger);
6174        }
6175        catch (RuntimeException ex)
6176        {
6177            // Since the interceptor is occasionally failing to log the stack trace, do it here.

6180            Log.alarm("Runtime exception " + ex + " in completePendingTrade(book.product="
6181                    + book.getProductKey() + ", trigger.side=" + aQuoteTrigger.getSide()

6184        }

6187    /**
6188     *  Refactored from completePendingTrade to add runtime exception logging.
6189     */
6190    private void internalCompletePendingTrade(OrderBook book, QuoteTriggerTradable aQuoteTrigger)
6191            throws DataValidationException, SystemException
6192    {
6193        QuoteTriggerTradeReport aTradeReport = aQuoteTrigger.getPendingTradeReport();
6194        if (aTradeReport == null)
6195        {
6196            Log.alarm("TradeServiceImpl >>> The QuoteTrigger has not TradeReport yet");
6197            return;
6198        }
6199        aTradeReport.prepareForCompletion();
6200        int quantity = aTradeReport.getQuantity();
6201        ParticipantList finalList = new ParticipantListImpl();
6202        int allocatedQuantity = createParticipantListForQuoteTrigger(finalList, book,
6203                aQuoteTrigger, quantity);
6204        if (quantity != allocatedQuantity)
6205        {
6206            Log.alarm("TradeServiceImpl >>> allocated quantity does not match traded quantity "
6207                    + quantity + ":" + allocatedQuantity);
6208            throw ExceptionBuilder.systemException(
6209                    "matched quantity does not match traded quantity " + quantity + ":"
6210                            + allocatedQuantity, 0);
6211        }
6212        aTradeReport.setQuoteTriggerParticipantList(finalList);
6213 
6214        // get final buyers and sellers
6215        ParticipantList buyers = aTradeReport.getBidList();
6216        ParticipantList sellers = aTradeReport.getAskList();
6217        ArrayList atomicTrades = new ArrayList();
6218        int matchQuantity = createAtomicTrades(buyers, sellers, atomicTrades, book
6219                .getTradingProduct());
6220        if (allocatedQuantity != matchQuantity)
6221        {
6222            Log.alarm("TradeServiceImpl >>> matched quantity does not match traded quantity "
6223                    + allocatedQuantity + ":" + matchQuantity);
6224            throw ExceptionBuilder.systemException(
6225                    "matched quantity does not match traded quantity " + allocatedQuantity + ":"
6226                            + matchQuantity, 0);
6227        }
6228 
6229        // UD 10/07/04...
6230        // create atomic trades for the strategy legs.
6231        HashMap buySideLegsMap = new HashMap();
6232        HashMap sellSideLegsMap = new HashMap();
6233        if (book.getTradingProduct().getProductKeys().productType == ProductTypes.STRATEGY)
6234        {
6235            try
6236            {
6237                createStrategyLegsAtomicTrades(book, aQuoteTrigger, buyers, sellers, aTradeReport,
6238                        buySideLegsMap, sellSideLegsMap);
6239            }
6240            catch (SpreadProcessingException spe)
6241            {
6242                Log
6243                        .exception(
6244                                this,
6245                                "createSpreadLegsTradeReports : Failed to create leg atomic trades for spread product in quote trigger",
6246                                spe);
6247                throw ExceptionBuilder.systemException("createSpreadLegsTradeReports " + spe, 0);
6248            }
6249        }
6250 
6251        aTradeReport.completePendingTrade(atomicTrades, myIdService, buySideLegsMap,
6252                sellSideLegsMap);
6253    }
6254 
6255    /*
6256     * UD 10/07/04 ...Create atomic trades for spread legs participants in quoteTrigger [spread to
6257     * spread]
6258    */
6259    public void createStrategyLegsAtomicTrades(OrderBook book, QuoteTriggerTradable aQuoteTrigger,
6260            ParticipantList buyers, ParticipantList sellers, QuoteTriggerTradeReport aTradeReport,
6261            HashMap buySideLegsMap, HashMap sellSideLegsMap) throws SpreadProcessingException,
6262            DataValidationException, SystemException
6263    {
6264        StrategyLegTradePrice[] legPrices = aTradeReport.getStrategyLegTradePrices();
6265        // Future use, if needed(see comment above in saveLegPricesAtQTCreation())
6266//        TradingProduct[] tradingProducts = aTradeReport.getTradingProductsFromLegTradePrices();
6267        ParticipantList[] bidLists = buyers.getListsForLegs(legPrices, aTradeReport
6268                .getDerivedTradeSide(), null);
6269        ParticipantList[] askLists = sellers.getListsForLegs(legPrices, aTradeReport
6270                .getDerivedTradeSide(), null);
6271        Price[] tradePrices = aTradeReport.getTradePricesOfLegs();
6272        Side[] legSides = aTradeReport.getSidesOfLegs();
6273        for (int i = 0; i < tradePrices.length; i++)
6274        {
6275            ArrayList atomicTrades = new ArrayList();
6276 
6277            if (legSides[i].isBuySide())
6278            {
6279                setContainersForLegSidesMap(buySideLegsMap, sellSideLegsMap, legPrices[i]
6280                        .getTradingProduct(), tradePrices[i], legSides[i], bidLists[i],
6281                        askLists[i], atomicTrades);
6282                // Future use, if needed(see comment above in saveLegPricesAtQTCreation())
6283                // tradingProducts[i], tradePrices[i], legSides[i], bidLists[i], askLists[i],
6284                // atomicTrades);
6285            }
6286            else
6287            {
6288                setContainersForLegSidesMap(buySideLegsMap, sellSideLegsMap, legPrices[i]
6289                        .getTradingProduct(), tradePrices[i], legSides[i], askLists[i],
6290                        bidLists[i], atomicTrades);
6291                // Future use, if needed(see comment above in saveLegPricesAtQTCreation())
6292                // tradingProducts[i], tradePrices[i], legSides[i], askLists[i], bidLists[i],
6293                // atomicTrades);
6294            }
6295        }
6296    }

6298    /*
6299     * UD 10/15/04 Create atomic trades for leg and save buyer/seller leg info in
6300     * buySideMap/sellSideMap.
6301    */
6302    private void setContainersForLegSidesMap(HashMap buySideLegsMap, HashMap sellSideLegsMap,
6303                                      TradingProduct tradingProduct, Price legTradePrice, Side legSide,
6304                                      ParticipantList bidList, ParticipantList askList, ArrayList atomicTrades)
6305        throws DataValidationException
6306    {
6307        StrategyLegQuoteTriggerContainer spreadQTBuySideContainter;
6308        StrategyLegQuoteTriggerContainer spreadQTSellSideContainter;
6309 
6310        int matchQuantity = createAtomicTrades(bidList, askList, atomicTrades, tradingProduct);
6311        // BUGBUG: If split occurs then matchQuantity can not be used instead, tradeQty should be
6312        // used while reporting
6313        spreadQTBuySideContainter = new StrategyLegQuoteTriggerContainer(tradingProduct, bidList,
6314                legTradePrice, legSide, matchQuantity, atomicTrades);
6315        buySideLegsMap.put(tradingProduct, spreadQTBuySideContainter);
6316        spreadQTSellSideContainter = new StrategyLegQuoteTriggerContainer(tradingProduct, askList,
6317                legTradePrice, legSide.getOtherSide(), matchQuantity, atomicTrades);
6318        sellSideLegsMap.put(tradingProduct, spreadQTSellSideContainter);
6319        // Following should be used
6320//        addStrategyLegQuoteTriggerContainerToMap(sellSideLegsMap, spreadQTSellSideContainter);
6321//        addStrategyLegQuoteTriggerContainerToMap(buySideLegsMap, spreadQTBuySideContainter);
6322    }
6323 
6324    /*
6325     * 10/07/04 ... Returns legPrices based on buyers and sellers
6326     */
6327    private StrategyLegTradePrice[] getLegPrices(TradingProduct tradingProduct, Price tradePrice,
6328            ParticipantList buyers, ParticipantList sellers, Side derivedTradeSide)
6329        throws SpreadProcessingException, DataValidationException, SystemException
6330    {
6331        StrategyLegTradePrice[] legPrices;
6332        if (buyers.isRegularList() && sellers.isRegularList())
6333        { // spread order trade with spread order
6334            derivedTradeSide = null;    /* value will not be used */
6335            legPrices = calculateTradePricesForLegs(buyers, sellers, tradePrice, tradingProduct, false);
6336        }
6337        else if (buyers.isDerivedList() && sellers.isRegularList())
6338        {
6339            derivedTradeSide = SideFactory.getAsDefinedSide();
6340            legPrices = buyers.getLegTradePrices();
6341        }
6342        else if (buyers.isRegularList() && sellers.isDerivedList())
6343        {
6344            derivedTradeSide = SideFactory.getOppositeSide();
6345            legPrices = sellers.getLegTradePrices();
6346        }
6347        else
6348        {
6349            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(
6350                    "Unexpected combination of participant list types for trade", 0);
6351        }
6352        return legPrices;
6353    }
6354 
6355    /**
6356     * create final participant list for a quote trigger when it expires
6357     */
6358    private int createParticipantListForQuoteTrigger(ParticipantList finalList, OrderBook book,
6359            QuoteTriggerTradable aQuoteTrigger, int quantityToAllocate)
6360    {
6361        int allocatedQuantity = 0;
6362        int size = 0;
6363        Price triggerPrice = aQuoteTrigger.getNonQPrice();
6364        AllocationTradeContext allocationContext = new AllocationTradeContextImpl(
6365                AllocationTradeTypes.QUOTE_TRIGGER);
6366        Iterator sets = book.getPrioritySets(aQuoteTrigger.getPriceDetails(), triggerPrice,
6367                quantityToAllocate, allocationContext);
6368        while (sets.hasNext() && allocatedQuantity < quantityToAllocate)
6369        {
6370            PriorityTradableSet nextSet = (PriorityTradableSet) sets.next();
6371            size = size + 1;
6372            int nextAllocatedQuantity = nextSet.allocate(finalList, quantityToAllocate
6373                    - allocatedQuantity);
6374            allocatedQuantity += nextAllocatedQuantity;
6375            if (Log.isDebugOn() && size > 1)
6376            {
6377                Log
6378                        .debug("TradeServiceImpl >>> OrderBook return more than 1 prioripty set "
6379                                + size);
6380            }
6381        }
6382        return allocatedQuantity;
6383    }
6384 
6385    /**
6386     * calculate leg prices for spread to spread trade.
6387     */
6388    protected StrategyLegTradePrice[] calculateTradePricesForLegs(ParticipantList aBiders,
6389            ParticipantList aAskers, Price aTradePrice, TradingProduct aTradingProduct, boolean isTBForCOB)
6390            throws DataValidationException, SpreadProcessingException, SystemException
6391    {

6500        }

6569    /**
6570     * Once a AcceptTradeUpdate is dequeued from the TradingClass, this method is invoked to

6572     * 
6573     * @param tradeId
6574     * @param tradesToUpdate
6575     **/
6576    public void processTradeUpdate(long tradeId, AtomicTradeStruct[] tradesToUpdate,
6577            TradeValidationStrategy strategy) throws SystemException, CommunicationException,
6578            AuthorizationException, DataValidationException, NotAcceptedException,
6579            TransactionFailedException
6580    {

6582        try
6583        {

6585        }
6586        catch (NotFoundException nfe)
6587        {

6589                    + nfe.details.message;

6591            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(msg, 0);
6592        }
6593

6595        validateUpdateTrade(tradeReport, tradesToUpdate, strategy);

6600 
6601    // validate the update trade request
6602    protected void validateUpdateTrade(TradeReport tradeReport,
6603            AtomicTradeStruct[] atomicTradeStructs, TradeValidationStrategy strategy)
6604            throws DataValidationException, AuthorizationException, CommunicationException,
6605            SystemException
6606{
6607    // verify that each atomic trade can be found and active
6608    for (int i = 0; i < atomicTradeStructs.length; ++i)
6609    {
6610        // Get affected entry and verify id - DataValidation will be thrown if entry not found
6611            TradeReportEntry affectedEntry = tradeReport.findTradeReportEntry(CboeId
6612                    .longValue(atomicTradeStructs[i].atomicTradeId));
6613 
6614            // Can only modify it if entry is active and entry type and last entry type are both ADD
6615            // entries
6616            if (!affectedEntry.isActive()
6617                    || (affectedEntry.getEntryType() != TradeReportEntryTypes.ADD)
6618                    || (affectedEntry.getLastEntryType() != TradeReportEntryTypes.ADD))
6619        {
6620            String message = "Cannot modify an inactive or deleted trade.";
6621            Log.alarm(this, message);
6622                throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(message,
6623                        DataValidationCodes.INVALID_UPDATE_ATTEMPT);
6624        }
6625 
6626        try
6627        {
6628            // validate the trade the update fields from update request
6629            strategy.validateUpdateTrade(affectedEntry, atomicTradeStructs[i]);
6630        }
6631        catch (DataValidationException e)
6632        {
6633            Log.exception(this, e.details.message, e);
6634            throw e;
6635        }
6636    }
6637}

6639    /**

6680                            oppositeParticipantLists, tradePrices, tradeQuantities, book,
6681                            updatedSide);
6682                }
6683            } // end else
6684        }
6685        return allocatedQuantity;

6735 
6736    public int createInternalizationTrade(InternalizationPair internalizationPair, OrderBook book,
6737            Price tradePrice) throws SystemException
6738    {
6739        Side otherSide = internalizationPair.getPrimaryOrder().getSide().getOtherSide();
6740        // try to trade @ best book price or 1-tick better than best book of the internalized order
6741        // side
6742        int incomingRemainingQty = 0; // since in this case, there will be no qty left and could
6743                                      // trade with customer qty of the book
6744        int allocatedQuantity = 0;
6745        if (tradePrice == null)
6746        {
6747            // if tradePrice is not given, use top BBO or 1 tick better than top BBO if there's cust
6748            // vol. on top BBO
6749            tradePrice = AuctionTradeHelper.getBestBookPriceOrOneTickBetter(otherSide
6750                    .getOtherSide(), book, AuctionTypes.AUCTION_INTERNALIZATION,
6751                    incomingRemainingQty);
6752            // for Cust-cust AIM, need to re-check the ajusted price against the opposite site NBBO
6753            if (canNotTradeInternally(internalizationPair, book, tradePrice, otherSide))
6754            {
6755                return allocatedQuantity; // no trade, both orders will be cancelled/rerouted
6756            }
6757        }
6758 
6759        if (!(internalizationPair.getSecondaryOrder().getSide().isFirstBetterOrEqual(
6760                internalizationPair.getSecondaryOrder().getPrice(), tradePrice) && internalizationPair
6761                .getPrimaryOrder().getSide().isFirstBetterOrEqual(
6762                        internalizationPair.getPrimaryOrder().getPrice(), tradePrice)))
6763        {
6764            Log.alarm(this, this.getClass().getName()
6765                    + ".createInternalizationTrade => the allocated quantity is 0");
6766            return allocatedQuantity; // couldn't trade at the given trade price
6767        }
6768        int quantityToAllocate = internalizationPair.getPrimaryOrder().getQuantityAllowed();
6769        ArrayList oppositeParticipantLists = new ArrayList();
6770        ArrayList tradePrices = new ArrayList();
6771        ArrayList tradeQuantities = new ArrayList();
6772        int oppositeAllocatedQuantity = AuctionTradeHelper.createInternalizationParticipantLists(
6773                internalizationPair, oppositeParticipantLists, tradePrices, tradeQuantities, book,
6774                tradePrice, quantityToAllocate);
6775        if (oppositeAllocatedQuantity > 0)
6776        {
6777            ArrayList incomingParticipantLists = new ArrayList();
6778 
6779            int sameSideAllocatedQuantity = createParticipantLists(incomingParticipantLists,
6780                    tradePrices, tradeQuantities, internalizationPair.getPrimaryOrder(), null,
6781                    oppositeAllocatedQuantity, book.getTradingProduct().getTradingClass());
6782 
6783            AuctionTradeHelper.prepareParticipantsForTrade(oppositeParticipantLists,
6784                    TradeContext.AUCTION_TRADE);
6785            AuctionTradeHelper.prepareParticipantsForTrade(incomingParticipantLists,
6786                    TradeContext.AUCTION_TRADE);
6787 
6788            if (sameSideAllocatedQuantity != oppositeAllocatedQuantity)
6789            {
6790                allocatedQuantity = 0;
6791                Log.alarm(this, this.getClass().getName()
6792                        + ".createInternalizationTrade => the allocated quantity("
6793                        + sameSideAllocatedQuantity + ") is different from the other side ( "
6794                        + oppositeAllocatedQuantity + ")");
6795            }
6796            else
6797            {
6798                allocatedQuantity = sameSideAllocatedQuantity;
6799                Side updatedSide = otherSide;
6800                try
6801                {
6802                    if (otherSide.isBuySide())
6803                    {
6804                        completeTrades(null, oppositeParticipantLists, incomingParticipantLists,
6805                                tradePrices, tradeQuantities, book, updatedSide);
6806                    }
6807                    else
6808                    {
6809                        completeTrades(null, incomingParticipantLists, oppositeParticipantLists,
6810                                tradePrices, tradeQuantities, book, updatedSide);
6811                    }
6812                }
6813                catch (SpreadProcessingException spe)
6814                {
6815                    Log.exception(this, spe);
6816                    throw ExceptionBuilder.systemException(spe.getMessage(),  0);
6817                }
6818                catch (DataValidationException de)
6819                {
6820                    Log.exception(this, de);
6821                    throw ExceptionBuilder.systemException(de.getMessage(),  0);
6822                }
6823            } // end else
6824        }
6825        return  allocatedQuantity;
6826    }
6827 
6828    /**
6829     * check whether it can trade internally or not.
6830     * 
6831     * @param internalizationPair
6832     * @param book
6833     * @param tradePrice
6834     * @param otherSide
6835     * @return true, if the trade price will not trade through the opposite NBBO/top customer price,
6836     *         otherwise, if the trade price is out of the range, then return true
6837     */
6838    private boolean canNotTradeInternally(InternalizationPair internalizationPair, OrderBook book,
6839            Price tradePrice, Side otherSide)
6840    {
6841        if (!AuctionProcessorBase.isCust2CustAIM(internalizationPair))
6842        {
6843            return false; // as this rule only applies to AIM Cust-cust
6844        }
6845        if(internalizationPair.isISO())
6846        {
6847            return false; // as AIM ISO ignores NBBO
6848        }   
6849        boolean notTrade = false;
6850        String message = "";
6851        Price auctionOppositeSideNBBO = internalizationPair.getNBBOPrice(true);
6852        if (otherSide.isFirstBetter(auctionOppositeSideNBBO, tradePrice))
6853        {
6854            notTrade = true;
6855            message = "Due to potential trade price=" + tradePrice + " worse than opposite NBBO="
6856                    + auctionOppositeSideNBBO;
6857        }
6858        else if (OrderBookImpl.isWorseThanBBOorEqualToCustomer(tradePrice, otherSide, book))
6859        {
6860            notTrade = true;
6861            message = "Due to potential trade price=" + tradePrice
6862                    + " worse than or equal to opposite BBO.";
6863        }
6864        if (notTrade)
6865        {
6866            message = "Cust-Cust AIM won't trade internally between primary Order( "
6867                + StructToString.toString(internalizationPair.getPrimaryOrder().getOrderId())
6868                + ") and match Order ( "
6869                + StructToString.toString(internalizationPair.getSecondaryOrder().getOrderId())
6870                + ")," + message;
6871            Log.information(this, message);
6872        }
6873        return notTrade;
6874    }
6875 
6876    /**
6877      * Gets next tradable starting from the current tradable passed in.
6878      */
6879    private Tradable getNextTradableFromCurrent(Tradable currentTradable,
6880            Enumeration theSideMarkets, Tradable firstTradable, int quantityRemaining,
6881            TradingClass tradingClass)
6882         {
6883        if (currentTradable == null)
6884        {
6885            if (firstTradable != null
6886                    && getMinQuantity(tradingClass, firstTradable) <= quantityRemaining)
6887             {
6888                 return firstTradable;
6889             }
6890         }
6891        while (theSideMarkets != null && theSideMarkets.hasMoreElements())
6892        {
6893             Tradable nextTradable = (Tradable) theSideMarkets.nextElement();
6894             if (getMinQuantity(tradingClass, nextTradable) <= quantityRemaining)
6895             {
6896                 return nextTradable;
6897             }
6898         }
6899         return null;
6900     }

7097    /**
7098     * Tells whether or not an entry that associates userAcronym and p_userId exists in a given look
7099     * up source. The look up is based on a key which is made up of a combination of the passed
7100     * parameters. The actual look up is performed by FirmPropertyService since it occurs on a table
7101     * created with user properties. The initial goal of this method is to provide with an
7102     * alternative look up method (user id - acronym) in additon to just looking at the acronym
7103     * field inside a UserStruct.
7104     * 
7105     * @param firm
7106     * @param classKey
7107     * @param userAcronym. the acronym.
7108     * @param p_userId: the user id.
7109     * @return true if a match is found, false otherwise.
7110     * 
7111     * @autor Francisco Ojeda
7112     */        
7113    private boolean associationFound(String sessionName, String firmNumber, String exchange,
7114            int classKey, String userAcronym, String userId)
7115    {
7116        boolean relationFound = false;
7117         
7118        BasePropertyKey key = buildSessionFirmClassAcronymKey(sessionName, firmNumber, exchange,
7119                userAcronym, classKey);
7120        
7121        String cmiUser = getFirmPropertyService().getMMTNCmiUser(key);
7122        if(cmiUser != null && userId.compareTo(cmiUser.trim()) == 0) 
7123        {
7124            relationFound = true;
7125        }
7126        return relationFound;
7127    }
7128    
7129    /**
7130     * Fills in certain fields (executing firm, account & subaccount) of p_TradeEntry using the 
7131     * information found in userInfo. The initial goal of this method is to use the values from user
7132     * info (overwriting the parameters passed in the original FloorTradeEntryStruct).
7133     * 
7134     * @param p_TradeEntry: floor trade which fields will be filled in.
7135     * @param userInfo: UserStruct from where the information to fill in the empty fiels will be
7136     * obtained.
7137     * @param classKey: the class key of the product being traded.
7138     * @return FloorTradeEntryStruct: this object is very similar to the p_TradeEntry argument, the
7139     * difference is in the firm, account and subaccount fields.
7140     * 
7141     * @autor Francisco Ojeda
7142     */    
7143    private FloorTradeEntryStruct fillWithUserInfo(FloorTradeEntryStruct p_TradeEntry,
7144            SessionProfileUserStruct sessionProfileUserStruct, int classKey)
7145    {
7146        boolean useUserProvidedAccount = false;
7147        boolean useUserProvidedSubaccount = false;
7148        String accMsg = "";
7149        String subaccMsg = "";
7150 
7151        // Overwrites the executing firm passed in the trade with the firm in user struct.  
7152        p_TradeEntry.firm = sessionProfileUserStruct.firm;
7153        
7154        if (p_TradeEntry.account != null && p_TradeEntry.account.length() > 0)
7155        {
7156            useUserProvidedAccount = true;
7157            accMsg = "Using user provided account value (" + p_TradeEntry.account + ").";
7158        }
7159 
7160        if (p_TradeEntry.subaccount != null && p_TradeEntry.subaccount.length() > 0)
7161        {
7162            useUserProvidedSubaccount = true;
7163            subaccMsg = "Using user provided subaccount value (" + p_TradeEntry.subaccount + ").";
7164        }
7165 
7166        // If account and subacount are provided by user in p_TradeEntry we keep these values.
7167        if (useUserProvidedAccount && useUserProvidedSubaccount)
7168        {
7169            String message = "In class " + this.getClass().getName()
7170                    + ".fillWithUserInfo() using user id: " + sessionProfileUserStruct.userId
7171                    + " found user provided information. " + accMsg + subaccMsg;
7172            Log.information(this, message);
7173            return p_TradeEntry;
7174        }
7175 
7176        // Look up the passed class in user struct's sessionProfilesByClass to obtain the account
7177        // and subaccount from class specific session profile.
7178        for ( int i = 0; i < sessionProfileUserStruct.sessionProfilesByClass.length; i++ )    
7179        {
7180            if (sessionProfileUserStruct.sessionProfilesByClass[i].sessionName
7181                    .equals(p_TradeEntry.sessionName)
7182                    && sessionProfileUserStruct.sessionProfilesByClass[i].classKey == classKey)
7183            {
7184                if (!useUserProvidedAccount)
7185            {
7186                p_TradeEntry.account = sessionProfileUserStruct.sessionProfilesByClass[i].account;
7187                    accMsg = "Using account value (" + p_TradeEntry.account + ") from profile. ";
7188                }
7189 
7190                if (!useUserProvidedSubaccount)
7191                {
7192                p_TradeEntry.subaccount = sessionProfileUserStruct.sessionProfilesByClass[i].subAccount;
7193                    subaccMsg = "Using subaccount value (" + p_TradeEntry.subaccount + ") from profile. ";
7194                }
7195 
7196                String message = "In class " + this.getClass().getName()
7197                        + ".fillWithUserInfo() using user id: " + sessionProfileUserStruct.userId
7198                        + " found class specific profile for session: " + p_TradeEntry.sessionName
7199                        + ", classKey: " + classKey + " in user's session profiles by class. "
7200                        + accMsg + subaccMsg;
7201                Log.information(this, message);
7202 
7203                return p_TradeEntry;
7204            }
7205        }
7206 
7207        // If no matches found in sessionProfilesByClass try to find a session default profile to
7208        // obtain account and subaccount from.
7209        for ( int i = 0; i < sessionProfileUserStruct.defaultSessionProfiles.length; i++)    
7210        {
7211            if (sessionProfileUserStruct.defaultSessionProfiles[i].sessionName
7212                    .equals(p_TradeEntry.sessionName))
7213            {
7214                if (!useUserProvidedAccount)
7215            {
7216                p_TradeEntry.account = sessionProfileUserStruct.defaultSessionProfiles[i].account;
7217                    accMsg = "Using account value (" + p_TradeEntry.account + ") from profile. ";
7218                }
7219 
7220                if (!useUserProvidedSubaccount)
7221                {
7222                p_TradeEntry.subaccount = sessionProfileUserStruct.defaultSessionProfiles[i].subAccount;
7223                    subaccMsg = "Using subaccount value (" + p_TradeEntry.subaccount + ") from profile. ";
7224                }
7225 
7226                String message = "In class " + this.getClass().getName()
7227                        + ".fillWithUserInfo() using user id: " + sessionProfileUserStruct.userId
7228                        + " found a default profile for session: " + p_TradeEntry.sessionName
7229                        + " in user's default session profiles. " + accMsg + subaccMsg;
7230                Log.information(this, message); 
7231                
7232                return p_TradeEntry;
7233            }            
7234        }        
7235        
7236        // If no session default profile then use the user default profile.
7237        if (!useUserProvidedAccount)
7238        {
7239        p_TradeEntry.account = sessionProfileUserStruct.defaultProfile.account;
7240            accMsg = "Using account value (" + p_TradeEntry.account + ") from profile. ";
7241        }
7242 
7243        if (!useUserProvidedSubaccount)
7244        {
7245        p_TradeEntry.subaccount = sessionProfileUserStruct.defaultProfile.subAccount;
7246            subaccMsg = "Using subaccount value (" + p_TradeEntry.subaccount + ") from profile. ";
7247        }
7248 
7249        String message = "In class " + this.getClass().getName()
7250                + ".fillWithUserInfo() using user id: " + sessionProfileUserStruct.userId
7251                + " could not find exact profile match for session: " + p_TradeEntry.sessionName
7252                + ", classKey: " + classKey + " in user's session profiles by class. "
7253                + "Could not find a default profile for session: " + p_TradeEntry.sessionName
7254                + " in user's default session profiles. Default user profile will be used. " + accMsg
7255                + subaccMsg;
7256        Log.information(this, message);
7257        
7258        return p_TradeEntry;
7259    }

7261    private String floorTradeStructToString(FloorTradeEntryStruct floorTradeEntry)
7262    {
7263        try
7264        {
7265            java.io.StringWriter resultWriter = new java.io.StringWriter();
7266            ReflectiveStructBuilder.printStruct(floorTradeEntry, "floorTrade.", resultWriter);
7267            return resultWriter.getBuffer().toString();
7268        }
7269        catch (java.io.IOException ex)
7270        {
7271            Log.exception(this,
7272                    "IOException writing FloorTradeEntryStruct struct to string.  Unexpected. "
7273                            + ex, ex);
7274            return "IOException writing struct to string.  Unexpected. " + ex;
7275        }
7276    }    
7277 
7278    /**
7279     * Interface method to accept floor trades. The goal of this method is to provide a common entry
7280     * point for handheld trade requests coming into the trade service.
7281     * 
7282     * @param p_tradeEntryStruct: floor trade.
7283     * @param userId: id of user sending the trade.
7284     * @param tradeType: type of floor trade. Currenlty only handheld trades are allowed.
7285     * @return CboeIdStruct corresponding to the accepted trade id.
7286     * @throws SystemException
7287     * @throws CommunicationException
7288     * @throws AuthorizationException
7289     * @throws DataValidationException
7290     * @throws NotAcceptedException
7291     * @throws TransactionFailedException
7292     * 
7293     * @autor Francisco Ojeda
7294     */
7295    
7296    public CboeIdStruct acceptFloorTrade(FloorTradeEntryStruct p_tradeEntryStruct, String p_userId,
7297            char p_tradeType) throws SystemException, CommunicationException,
7298            AuthorizationException, DataValidationException, NotAcceptedException,
7299           TransactionFailedException

7301        return processFloorTradeRequest(p_tradeEntryStruct, p_userId, p_tradeType);
7302    }
7303    
7304    /**
7305     * Working method to accept and process floor trades. The goal of this method is to support 
7306     * handheld trades processing inside the trade service. Handheld trades have their two sides 
7307     * with different amount of information. This is, one side always contains more information than
7308     * the other. They require a fair amount of validation and "filling-the-balnks" before the
7309     * actual trade could be executed. This method takes care of these two tasks: validation and
7310     * infromation completion. Currenlty Handheld trades are accepted in W_MAIN session only.
7311     * 
7312     * @param p_tradeEntryStruct: floor trade.
7313     * @param userId: id of user sending the trade.
7314     * @param tradeType: type of floor trade. Currenlty only handheld trades are allowed.
7315     * @return CboeIdStruct corresponding to the accepted trade id.
7316     * @throws SystemException
7317     * @throws CommunicationException
7318     * @throws AuthorizationException
7319     * @throws DataValidationException
7320     * @throws NotAcceptedException
7321     * @throws TransactionFailedException
7322     * 
7323     * @autor Francisco Ojeda
7324     */    
7325    
7326    private CboeIdStruct processFloorTradeRequest(FloorTradeEntryStruct p_tradeEntryStruct,
7327            String p_userId, char p_tradeType) throws SystemException, CommunicationException,
7328            AuthorizationException, DataValidationException, NotAcceptedException,
7329            TransactionFailedException
7330    {
7331        if(Log.isDebugOn())
7332        {
7333            String message0 = "In class " + this.getClass().getName() + ".acceptFloorTrade() "
7334                    + "Received: userId: " + p_userId + ", trade type: " + p_tradeType;
7335        Log.debug(this, message0 + ", " +  floorTradeStructToString(p_tradeEntryStruct));
7336        }
7337    
7338        //Get and validate product.
7339        TradingProduct product = getTradingProduct(p_tradeEntryStruct.productKey);        
7340        
7341        // Check input presence and format correctness
7342        validateFloorTradeInput(p_tradeEntryStruct, p_userId, p_tradeType,
7343                product.getProductKeys().productType);
7344    
7345        if(product.isStrategy()) 
7346        {
7347            String message = "Invalid product key: " + p_tradeEntryStruct.productKey
7348            + "The product key corresponds to a strategy. "
7349            + "In a HANDHELD_TRADE the trading product cannot be a strategy.";
7350 
7351            if(Log.isDebugOn())
7352            {
7353                Log.debug(this, message);
7354            }
7355            
7356            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(message,
7357                    DataValidationCodes.INVALID_PRODUCT);
7358        }
7359        int classKey = product.getTradingClass().getProductClassKey();  
7360        
7361        if (classKey <= 0) 
7362        {
7363            String message = "Invalid product class. Product with key: "
7364                    + p_tradeEntryStruct.productKey
7365                    + " corresponds to a class with an invalid class key: "
7366                    + classKey
7367                    + ". In a HANDHELD_TRADE the trading product's class must have a valid class key.";
7368            if(Log.isDebugOn())
7369            {
7370                Log.debug(this, message);
7371            }
7372            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(message,
7373                    DataValidationCodes.INVALID_PRODUCT_CLASS);
7374        }
7375 
7376        // The ultimate user profile to use. This is the actual executing user profile to use in the
7377        // trade report.
7378        SessionProfileUserStruct executingUser = null;
7379       
7380        SessionProfileUserStruct userFromPassedId = null;
7381        SessionProfileUserStruct userFromPassedAcronym = null;
7382 
7383        // FIRST LOOKUP: lookup user by userId and match the user's acronym with the passed acronym.
7384 
7385        // Get user from UserService using passed userId.
7386        try
7387        {
7388            userFromPassedId = getUserService().getSessionProfileUserInformation(p_userId);
7389        }
7390        catch (NotFoundException e)
7391        {
7392            String message = "Non-existant executig user id: " + p_userId
7393                    + " . Could not find a user that matches this id. ";
7394            Log.information(this, message);
7395        }
7396        
7397        // Match passed acronym and acronym of user returned from UserService.
7398        ExchangeAcronymContainer acronymFromPassedIdContainer = new ExchangeAcronymContainer(
7399                userFromPassedId.userAcronym);
7400        ExchangeAcronymContainer passedAcronymContainer = new ExchangeAcronymContainer(
7401                p_tradeEntryStruct.executingMarketMaker);
7402 
7403        if (!acronymFromPassedIdContainer.equalsIgnoringExchange(passedAcronymContainer))
7404        {
7405            String message = "Executing broker acronym mismatch: "
7406                    + p_tradeEntryStruct.executingMarketMaker.acronym
7407                    + ". UserService could not find an association between executing acronym and executing userId: "
7408                    + p_userId;
7409            Log.information(this, message);
7410 
7411            // SECOND LOOKUP: match userId and passed acronym. If match exist use passed acronym to
7412            // get user.
7413            
7414            // Get user and firm from UserService using passed acronym.
7415            try
7416            {
7417                userFromPassedAcronym = getUserService().getSessionProfileUserInformationByAcronym(
7418                        p_tradeEntryStruct.executingMarketMaker);
7419            }
7420            catch (NotFoundException e)
7421            {
7422                String message1 = "Invalid executig acronym: " + passedAcronymContainer
7423                        + " . UserService could not find a user that matches this acronym. ";
7424                throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(message1,
7425                        DataValidationCodes.INVALID_USER);
7426            }        
7427 
7428            // Match passed userId and acronym using property lookup.
7429            if (!associationFound(p_tradeEntryStruct.sessionName,
7430                    userFromPassedAcronym.firm.firmNumber, userFromPassedAcronym.firm.exchange,
7431                    classKey, p_tradeEntryStruct.executingMarketMaker.acronym, p_userId))
7432            {
7433                String message2 = "Executing broker acronym - userId mismatch. "
7434                        + "Could not find an association between executing acronym: "
7435                        + p_tradeEntryStruct.executingMarketMaker.acronym
7436                        + " and executing userId: " + p_userId;
7437                throw ExceptionBuilder.notAcceptedException(message2,
7438                        NotAcceptedCodes.INVALID_REQUEST);
7439            }   
7440            else
7441            {
7442                executingUser = userFromPassedAcronym;
7443                String message3 = "Found relation executing acronym - userId ( "
7444                        + p_tradeEntryStruct.executingMarketMaker.acronym + " - " + p_userId
7445                        + " ) in firm properties. ";
7446                Log.information(this, message3);
7447           }
7448        }
7449        else
7450        {
7451            executingUser = userFromPassedId;
7452            String message4 = "Found relation userId - executing acronym ( " + p_userId + " - "
7453                    + p_tradeEntryStruct.executingMarketMaker.acronym + " ) in user cache. ";
7454            Log.information(this, message4);
7455        }
7456 
7457        // Executing side must be a market maker.
7458        if (executingUser.role != UserRoles.MARKET_MAKER
7459                && executingUser.role != UserRoles.DPM_ROLE)
7460        {
7461            String message = "Invalid executing user role: "
7462                    + executingUser.role
7463                    + ". In a HANDHELD_TRADE the excecuting user must be on MARKET_MAKER (M) or DPM_ROLE (D) role. ";
7464 
7465            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(message,
7466                    DataValidationCodes.INVALID_USER);
7467        }
7468        
7469        // Fill in the passed trade entry with user info values.
7470        FloorTradeEntryStruct modifiedTradeEntryStruct = fillWithUserInfo(p_tradeEntryStruct,
7471                executingUser, classKey);
7472        if(Log.isDebugOn())
7473        {
7474            String message5 = "In class " + this.getClass().getName() + ".acceptFloorTrade() "
7475                    + "class key: " + classKey + "modifiedTradeEntryStruct: "
7476                    + floorTradeStructToString(modifiedTradeEntryStruct);
7477        Log.debug(this, message5);
7478        }
7479        
7480        // Transform FloorTradeEntryStruct into a TradeReportStructV2
7481        TradeReportStructV2 trade = TradeReportStructBuilder
7482                                    .convertToTradeReportStructV2(modifiedTradeEntryStruct);        
7483        
7484        return processFloorTrade(trade, product, TradeReportHandlingInstructions.REGULAR,
7485                modifiedTradeEntryStruct.side);
7486    }

7488    private void testARException(TradeReportStruct externalTrade, char tradedSide)
7489            throws SystemException, CommunicationException, DataValidationException,
7490    TransactionFailedException, AuthorizationException
7491    {
7492        String branch;
7493        if (tradedSide == Sides.BUY)
7494        {
7495            branch = externalTrade.parties[0].buyerFirmBranch;
7496        }
7497        else
7498        {
7499            branch = externalTrade.parties[0].sellerFirmBranch;
7500        }
7501 
7502        if (exceptionTypeAR != null && orderBranchAR != null && orderBranchAR.equals(branch))
7503        {
7504            if (exceptionTypeAR.equals("SE"))
7505            {
7506                throw ExceptionBuilder.systemException("testing AR command SystemException", 0);
7507            }
7508            else if (exceptionTypeAR.equals("CE"))
7509            {
7510                throw ExceptionBuilder.communicationException(
7511                        "testing AR command CommunicationException", 0);
7512            }
7513            else if (exceptionTypeAR.equals("TFE"))
7514            {
7515                throw ExceptionBuilder.transactionFailedException(
7516                        "testing AR command TransactionFailedException", 0);
7517            }
7518            else if (exceptionTypeAR.equals("DVE"))
7519            {
7520                throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(
7521                        "testing AR command DataValidationException", 0);
7522            }
7523            else if (exceptionTypeAR.equals("AE"))
7524            {
7525                throw ExceptionBuilder.authorizationException(
7526                        "testing AR command AuthorizationException", 0);
7527            }
7528            else if (exceptionTypeAR.equals("NP"))
7529            {
7530                throw new NullPointerException("testing AR command NullPointerException");
7531            }
7532            else
7533            {
7534                exceptionTypeAR = null;
7535    }
7536        }
7537    }
7538

7542        orderBranchAR = orderBranch;

7545    protected TradeServiceHome  getMyHome()
7546    {
7547        if (myHome == null)
7548        {
7549            myHome = (TradeServiceHome) getBOHome();
7550        }
7551        return myHome;
7552    }
7553 
7554    /**
7555     * Since getMyHome() may not return the TradeServiceHomeImpl (it may be
7556     * TradeMaintenanceServiceHomeImpl), and the contra anonymizing code is in
7557     * TradeServiceHomeImpl...
7558     */
7559    protected TradeServiceHomeImpl getTradeServiceHome()
7560    {
7561        if (tradeServiceHome == null)
7562        {
7563            try
7564            {
7565                BOHome home = HomeFactory.getInstance().findHome(TradeServiceHome.HOME_NAME);
7566                if (home instanceof TradeServiceHomeImpl)
7567                {
7568                    tradeServiceHome = (TradeServiceHomeImpl) home;
7569                }
7570                else
7571                {
7572                    Log.alarm(this, "Found home " + TradeServiceHome.HOME_NAME
7573                            + " is NOT instanceof TradeServiceHomeImpl: " + (home == null
7574                                    ? "null"
7575                                    : home.getClass().getName()));
7576                }
7577            }
7578            catch (CBOELoggableException e)
7579            {
7580                Log.alarm(this, "Failed to find home " + TradeServiceHome.HOME_NAME);
7581            }
7582        }
7583        return tradeServiceHome;
7584    }
