7603    
7604    public TradeReportStructV2 acceptCrossProductLegTrade(String originatingSessionName,
7605            TradeReportStructV2 trade, AtomicTradeBillingStruct[] billings) throws SystemException,
7606            CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException,
7607            NotAcceptedException, TransactionFailedException
7608    {
7609        // check the leg trade price against BBO market for AIM auction
7610        checkBBOForAIMCrossProductTrade(trade);        
7611        trade.settlementTradeReport.settlementDate = EquitySettlementDaysAheadCalculator
7612                .calculateSettlementTradeDate(trade.tradeReport.tradeType);
7613        // if settlement transaction time is 0, set to current date time
7614        if (trade.settlementTradeReport.transactionTime.date.year == 0)
7615        {
7616            trade.settlementTradeReport.transactionTime = (new DateWrapper(new Date()))
7617                    .toDateTimeStruct();
7618        }
7619        // if timeTraded is 0, set to current date time
7620        if (trade.tradeReport.timeTraded.date.year == 0)
7621        {
7622            trade.tradeReport.timeTraded = (new DateWrapper(new Date())).toDateTimeStruct();
7623        }
7624        return this.acceptTradeV2FromStruct(trade, originatingSessionName,
7625                TradeReportHandlingInstructions.REGULAR, billings);
7626    }
7627 
7628    /**
7629     * checkBBOForAIMCrossProductTrade Check the leg trade price against BBO market for AIM auction
7630     * 
7631     * @param trade
7632     * @throws DataValidationException
7633     */
7634    private void checkBBOForAIMCrossProductTrade(TradeReportStructV2 trade)
7635            throws DataValidationException
7636    {
7637              
7638        if (trade.tradeReport.tradeType == TradeTypes.CROSS_PRODUCT_AIM_CROSS_TRADE)
7639        {
7640           // check the leg trade price against BBO market for AIM auction
7641           Price tradePrice = PriceFactory.createValuedPrice(trade.tradeReport.price);
7642           int productKey = trade.tradeReport.productKey;           
7643           OrderBookImpl myOrderBook = (OrderBookImpl) getOrderBookHome().find(productKey);
7644           Side theSide = buySide;           
7645           if (OrderBookImpl.isWorseThanBBOorEqualToCustomer(tradePrice, theSide, myOrderBook))
7646           {                                
7647                handleBBOViolate(tradePrice, productKey, theSide);
7648           }
7649           else
7650           {
7651               theSide = theSide.getOtherSide();
7652               if (OrderBookImpl.isWorseThanBBOorEqualToCustomer(tradePrice, theSide, myOrderBook))
7653               {
7654                    handleBBOViolate(tradePrice, productKey, theSide);
7655               }              
7656           }            
7657        }
7658    }
7659 
7660    private void handleBBOViolate(Price tradePrice, int productKey, Side theSide)
7661            throws DataValidationException
7662    {
7663        ExceptionDetails detail = new ExceptionDetails();
7664        detail.message = "The trade price =" + tradePrice
7665                + "Worse than BBO or same as Customer price of product" + productKey + " on Side: "
7666                + theSide;
7667           Log.alarm(this, detail.message);
7668           throw new DataValidationException(detail);
7669    }
7670 
7671    public void completeTradeReport(TradeReport tradeReportToComplete, boolean heldOrderTrade,
7672            ParticipantList biders, ParticipantList askers, Price price)
7673            throws DataValidationException, SystemException
7674    {
7675        doTradeMatch((TradeReportImpl) tradeReportToComplete, tradeReportToComplete
7676                .getTradingProduct(), TradeTypes.CROSS_PRODUCT_LEG_TRADE,
7677                TradeTypes.CROSS_PRODUCT_LEG_TRADE, heldOrderTrade, biders, askers, price,
7678                (TradeReport) null);
7679 
7680    }
7681 
7682    public TradeReportStructV2 acceptCrossProductLegTradeV2(String p_originatingSessionName,
7683            TradeReportStructV2 p_crossProductLegTrade, AtomicTradeBillingStruct[] p_billings,
7684            OrderStruct[] p_buyers, OrderStruct[] p_sellers) throws SystemException,
7685            CommunicationException, AuthorizationException, DataValidationException,
7686            NotAcceptedException, TransactionFailedException
7687    {
7688        TradeReportStructV2 tradeReportResponse = null;
7689        try
7690        {
7691            //Setting the Sellers Order to Thread Local to be used 
7692            //to mark Short Sale indicator while creating Trade Report 
7693            //database entry.
7694            TradeHelper.setSellersOrderIntoContext(p_sellers);
7695            tradeReportResponse = acceptCrossProductLegTrade(
7696                p_originatingSessionName, p_crossProductLegTrade, p_billings);
7697        }
7698        finally
7699        {
7700            TradeHelper.setSellersOrderIntoContext(null);
7701        }
7702 
7703        // SEDL 5922 (PITS 9034) - cross product drop copies in stock
7704        // When a cross product spread-to-spread trade prints in CBSX, the firms really
7705        // want a drop copy available in CBSX.  This is an interim solution to the problem:
7706        // we will locally publish a fill report w/out contra information for each of the
7707        // spread orders that are traded.  We publish these fills only after the CBSX trade
7708        // is accepted.
7709        //
7710        // The proposed long-term solution is to generate orders in CBSX that represent the
7711        // stock legs of the spreads, and have them execute as a tied cross in CBSX.
7712        //
7713        // - Sinclair, 3/18/08
7714        if (generateCrossProductDropCopies)
7715        {
7716            try
7717            {
7718                generateFillsForCrossProductLegTrade(tradeReportResponse, p_buyers, p_sellers);
7719            }
7720            catch (Exception ex)
7721            {
7722                Log.exception(this, "Failed to publish cross product leg fill report "
7723                        + p_crossProductLegTrade.tradeReport.tradeId.highCboeId + ":"
7724                        + p_crossProductLegTrade.tradeReport.tradeId.lowCboeId, ex);
7725            }
7726        }
7727 
7728        return tradeReportResponse;
7729    }
7730 
7731    private void generateFillsForCrossProductLegTrade(TradeReportStructV2 p_legTrade,
7732            OrderStruct[] p_buyers, OrderStruct[] p_sellers)
7733    {
7734        OrderStatusConsumer orderStatus = EventHomes.getOrderStatusConsumerHome().find();
7735 
7736        Map<Long, List<AtomicTradeStruct>> buyers = new HashMap<Long, List<AtomicTradeStruct>>();
7737        Map<Long, List<AtomicTradeStruct>> sellers = new HashMap<Long, List<AtomicTradeStruct>>();
7738 
7739        for (int i = 0; i < p_legTrade.tradeReport.parties.length; i++)
7740        {
7741            AtomicTradeStruct atomic = p_legTrade.tradeReport.parties[i];
7742            addToMap(buyers, atomic, CboeId.longValue(atomic.buyerOrderOrQuoteKey));
7743            addToMap(sellers, atomic, CboeId.longValue(atomic.sellerOrderOrQuoteKey));
7744        }
7745 
7746        Log.information(this, "Publish cross product leg fills for drop copies for "
7747                + p_buyers.length + " buyers and " + p_sellers.length + " sellers.");
7748        publishFills(orderStatus, p_legTrade, Sides.BUY, buyers, p_buyers);
7749        publishFills(orderStatus, p_legTrade, Sides.SELL, sellers, p_sellers);
7750    }
7751 
7752    private void publishFills(OrderStatusConsumer p_orderStatus, TradeReportStructV2 p_legTrade,
7753            char p_side, Map<Long, List<AtomicTradeStruct>> p_orderToTradeMap,
7754            OrderStruct[] p_orders)
7755    {
7756        for (long orderId : p_orderToTradeMap.keySet())
7757        {
7758            OrderStruct order = null;
7759            for (OrderStruct anOrder : p_orders)
7760            {
7761                long anOrderId = CboeId.longValue(new CboeIdStruct(anOrder.orderId.highCboeId,
7762                        anOrder.orderId.lowCboeId));
7763                if (anOrderId == orderId)
7764                {
7765                    order = anOrder;
7766                    break;
7767                }
7768            }
7769            if (order == null)
7770            {
7771                Log.alarm(this, "Cross product leg fill publish: failed to find " + p_side
7772                        + "-side order in order list " + orderId + " in atomic trades for trade "
7773                        + CboeId.toString(p_legTrade.tradeReport.tradeId));
7774                continue;
7775            }
7776 
7777            FilledReportStruct fill = new FilledReportStruct();
7778 
7779            List<AtomicTradeStruct> atomicTrades = p_orderToTradeMap.get(orderId);
7780            ContraPartyStruct[] contras = new ContraPartyStruct[atomicTrades.size()];
7781            int totalTraded = 0;
7782            for (int i = 0; i < atomicTrades.size(); i++)
7783            {
7784                AtomicTradeStruct atomicTrade = atomicTrades.get(i);
7785                contras[i] = new ContraPartyStruct();
7786                contras[i].user = (p_side == Sides.BUY)
7787                        ? atomicTrade.sellerOriginator
7788                        : atomicTrade.buyerOriginator;
7789                contras[i].quantity = atomicTrade.quantity;
7790                contras[i].firm = (p_side == Sides.BUY)
7791                        ? atomicTrade.sellerFirm
7792                        : atomicTrade.buyerFirm;
7793 
7794                totalTraded += atomicTrade.quantity;
7795            }
7796 
7797            order.userId = "";
7798 
7799            fill.contraParties = getTradeServiceHome().prepareContrasForPublic(contras);
7800 
7801            fill.account = order.account;
7802            fill.cmta = order.cmta;
7803            fill.executingBroker = order.userAcronym.acronym;
7804            fill.executingOrGiveUpFirm = order.orderId.executingOrGiveUpFirm;
7805            for (LegOrderDetailStruct legEntry : order.legOrderDetails)
7806            {
7807                if (legEntry.productKey == p_legTrade.tradeReport.productKey)
7808                {
7809                    Log.information(
7810                                    this,
7811                                    "Using leg clearing firm "
7812                                            + legEntry.clearingFirm.exchange
7813                                            + ":"
7814                                            + legEntry.clearingFirm.firmNumber
7815                        + " for cross product drop copy stock fill, replacing (in the fill report only) the original "
7816                        + "orderId.executingOrGiveUpFirm "
7817                                            + order.orderId.executingOrGiveUpFirm.exchange + ":"
7818                                            + order.orderId.executingOrGiveUpFirm.firmNumber);
7819                    fill.executingOrGiveUpFirm = legEntry.clearingFirm;
7820                    order.orderId.executingOrGiveUpFirm = legEntry.clearingFirm;
7821                }
7822            }
7823            fill.extensions = "";
7824            fill.fillReportType = ReportTypes.STRATEGY_LEG_REPORT;
7825            fill.leavesQuantity = order.leavesQuantity;
7826            fill.optionalData = order.optionalData;
7827            fill.originator = order.originator;
7828            fill.orsId = order.orsId;
7829            fill.positionEffect = order.positionEffect;
7830            fill.price = p_legTrade.tradeReport.price;
7831            fill.productKey = p_legTrade.tradeReport.productKey;
7832            fill.sessionName = TradingSessionNameHelper.getConfiguredSessionNames()[0];
7833            fill.side = p_side;
7834            fill.subaccount = order.subaccount;
7835            fill.timeSent = DateWrapper.convertToDateTime(System.currentTimeMillis());
7836            fill.tradedQuantity = totalTraded;
7837            fill.tradeId = p_legTrade.tradeReport.tradeId;
7838            fill.transactionSequenceNumber = 1;
7839            fill.userAssignedId = order.userAssignedId;
7840            fill.userAcronym = order.userAcronym;
7841            fill.userId = order.userId;
7842 
7843            // Since the CAS requires all fills to have a minimal transaction sequence number of 2,
7844            // We'll artificially bump up the order seq number to 2 for the drop copy.
7845            // Note that if we can have a scenario where the order will fill multiple times in a
7846            // single
7847            // transaction, the sequence number 2 may get repeated. We don't currently have this
7848            // scenario
7849            // (as of CD7.1)
7850            // - sinclair, 10/24/2008
7851            //
7852            if (order.transactionSequenceNumber < MIN_ORDER_SEQ_NUM_FOR_FILL)
7853            {
7854                order.transactionSequenceNumber = MIN_ORDER_SEQ_NUM_FOR_FILL;
7855            }
7856 
7857            Log.information(this,
7858                    "Publishing fill for drop copy support of cross product trades.  Fill details follow:\n"
7859                            + "  userId='"
7860                            + fill.userId
7861                            + "'\n"
7862                            + "  executingBroker='"
7863                            + fill.executingBroker
7864                            + "'\n"
7865                            + "  executingOrGiveUpFirm='"
7866                            + fill.executingOrGiveUpFirm.firmNumber
7867                            + ":"
7868                            + fill.executingOrGiveUpFirm.exchange
7869                            + "'\n"
7870                            + "  side="
7871                            + fill.side
7872                            + "\n"
7873                            + "  quantity="
7874                            + fill.tradedQuantity
7875                            + "\n"
7876                            + "  price="
7877                            + PriceFactory.create(fill.price)
7878                            + "\n"
7879                            + "  productKey="
7880                            + PriceFactory.create(fill.productKey)
7881                            + "\n"
7882                            + "  tradeId="
7883                            + CboeId.toString(fill.tradeId)
7884                            + "\n"
7885                            + "  numContraParties="
7886                            + contras.length
7887                            + "\n"
7888                            + "  order.transactionSequenceNumber="
7889                            + order.transactionSequenceNumber + "\n");
7890 
7891            p_orderStatus.acceptOrderFillReport(ConfigurationGroupHelper
7892                    .getPublishingGroupsForProcess(), StatusUpdateReasons.NEW, order,
7893                    new FilledReportStruct[] { fill }, "");
7894        }
7895    }

7897    private void addToMap(Map<Long, List<AtomicTradeStruct>> p_orderToTradeMap,
7898            AtomicTradeStruct p_atomicTrade, long orderId)
7899    {
7900        List<AtomicTradeStruct> atomicTradeList = p_orderToTradeMap.get(orderId);
7901        if (atomicTradeList == null)
7902        {
7903            p_orderToTradeMap.put(orderId, atomicTradeList = new ArrayList<AtomicTradeStruct>());
7904        }
7905        atomicTradeList.add(p_atomicTrade);
7906    }

8000        public TradeBustResponseStruct[] acceptMultipleTradeBust(MultipleTradeBustStruct[] trades,
8001                        String requestingUserId, String transactionId, DateTimeStruct timeStamp, KeyValueStruct[] auditLogProperties)
8002                        throws SystemException, CommunicationException,
8003                        AuthorizationException, DataValidationException,
8004                        NotAcceptedException, TransactionFailedException 
8005        {
8006            TradeBustResponseStruct[] result = new TradeBustResponseStruct[0];
8007                Log.information(this, "acceptMultipleTradeBust invoked for user: " + requestingUserId);                
8008                synchronized(this)
8009                {
8010                    ArrayList<TradeBustResponseStruct> bustResults = new ArrayList<TradeBustResponseStruct>();
8011            BulkActionRequestHome bulkActionReqHome = getBulkActionRequestHome();
8012            BulkActionRequest requestDbId = null;
8013            try {
8014                requestDbId = FederatedServiceHelper.queryBulkActionRequest(bulkActionReqHome, requestingUserId, transactionId);
8015            }
8016            catch( Exception e) {
8017                Log.information("BulkActionRequestID not found : " + e.getMessage());
8018            }
8019                
8020            if (requestDbId == null) {
8021                requestDbId = FederatedServiceHelper.persistBulkActionRequest(bulkActionReqHome,
8022                        timeStamp, requestingUserId, BUST_OPERATION,
8023                        transactionId, RouteNameHelper.getRouteName(), auditLogProperties);
8024            }
8025            
8026            for (MultipleTradeBustStruct theTradeToBust: trades)
8027            {
8028                List<TradeBustResponseStruct> localResults;
8029                try
8030                {
8031                    TradeReport tradeReportToBust = validateTradeBustParameters(theTradeToBust);
8032                    localResults = bustLocalTrades(theTradeToBust.tradingSessionName, tradeReportToBust, 
8033                            theTradeToBust.tradeBustDetail, "", false, Sides.UNSPECIFIED);
8034                    bustResults.addAll(localResults);
8035                    persistBulkActionDtl(requestDbId, localResults, theTradeToBust.tradeBustDetail);
8036                    
8037                    // If this is a cross-product strategy trade report, submit the request
8038                    // to bust the remote leg trades.
8039                    if (isCrossProductStrategy(tradeReportToBust.getProduct()))
8040                    {                 
8041                        if ((tradeReportToBust.getTradeType() == TradeTypes.CROSS_PRODUCT_CROSS_TRADE) ||
8042                            (tradeReportToBust.getTradeType() == TradeTypes.CROSS_PRODUCT_LEG_TRADE) ||
8043                            (tradeReportToBust.getTradeType() == TradeTypes.CROSS_PRODUCT_AIM_CROSS_TRADE))            
8044                        {
8045                            List<TradeBustResponseStruct> remoteResults;
8046                            remoteResults = bustRemoteTrades(tradeReportToBust, theTradeToBust.tradeBustDetail,
8047                                requestingUserId, transactionId, timeStamp, auditLogProperties);
8048                            bustResults.addAll(remoteResults);
8049                        }
8050                    }
8051                }
8052                catch (NotAcceptedException nae)
8053                {
8054                    for (BustTradeStruct atomicTrade : theTradeToBust.tradeBustDetail)
8055                    {
8056                        TradeBustResponseStruct bustResponse = new TradeBustResponseStruct();
8057                        bustResponse.tradeId = atomicTrade.atomicTradeId;
8058                        bustResponse.serverId = RouteNameHelper.getRouteName();
8059                        bustResponse.errorCode = ServerResponseCodes.NOT_ACCEPTED_EXCEPTION;
8060                        bustResponse.description = "Unable to bust atomic trade report: " + nae.getMessage();
8061                        bustResults.add(bustResponse);
8062                    }                
8063                }
8064                catch (DataValidationException dve)
8065                {
8066                    for (BustTradeStruct atomicTrade : theTradeToBust.tradeBustDetail)
8067                    {
8068                        TradeBustResponseStruct bustResponse = new TradeBustResponseStruct();
8069                        bustResponse.tradeId = atomicTrade.atomicTradeId;
8070                        bustResponse.serverId = RouteNameHelper.getRouteName();
8071                        bustResponse.errorCode = ServerResponseCodes.DATA_VALIDATION_EXCEPTION;
8072                        bustResponse.description = "Unable to bust atomic trade report: " + dve.getMessage();
8073                        bustResults.add(bustResponse);
8074                    }                
8075                }
8076            }      
8077            result = new TradeBustResponseStruct[bustResults.size()];
8078            result = bustResults.toArray(result);
8079                }
8080        Log.information(this, "acceptMultipleTradeBust completed for user: " + requestingUserId);
8081        return result;
8082        }
8083 
8084    private boolean isCrossProductStrategy(int productKey)
8085    {
8086        boolean isCrossProductStrategy = false;
8087        ProductData prodData;
8088        try
8089        {
8090            prodData = getProductDataCacheHome().find().getProductData(productKey);
8091            if (prodData.isCrossProductStrategy())  
8092            {
8093                isCrossProductStrategy = true;
8094            }
8095        }
8096        catch (Exception e)
8097        {
8098            // This shouldn't really happen. So for now, let's just swallow the 
8099            // exception and move on.
8100            Log.alarm(this, "Encountered exception while attempting to confirm whether product is cross-product");
8101            Log.exception(this, "Encountered exception while attempting to confirm whether product is cross-product/", e);
8102        }
8103        return isCrossProductStrategy;
8104    }

8106    private boolean isEquityLeg(int productKey)
8107    {
8108        boolean isEquityLeg = false;
8109        ProductData prodData;
8110        try
8111        {
8112            prodData = getProductDataCacheHome().find().getProductData(productKey);
8113            if (prodData.getProductType() == ProductTypes.EQUITY)  
8114            {
8115                isEquityLeg = true;
8116            }
8117        }
8118        catch (Exception e)
8119        {
8120            // This shouldn't really happen. So for now, let's just swallow the 
8121            // exception and move on.
8122            Log.alarm(this, "Encountered exception while attempting to confirm whether the leg is equity");
8123            Log.exception(this, "Encountered exception while attempting to confirm whether whether the leg is equity/", e);
8124        }
8125        return isEquityLeg;
8126    }

8164    private Vector<String> getTradeIdList(TradeReportSummaryStruct[] p_tradeReportSummary)
8165    {
8166            Vector<String> tradeIds = null;
8167            if(p_tradeReportSummary != null && p_tradeReportSummary.length > 0 ) {
8168                tradeIds = new Vector<String>(p_tradeReportSummary.length);
8169                CboeIdStruct tis = null;
8170                TradeReportSummaryStruct trs = null;
8171                String tradeId = null;
8172                for(int i=0; i < p_tradeReportSummary.length; i++ ) {
8173                    trs = p_tradeReportSummary[i];
8174                    tradeId = String.valueOf(CboeId.longValue(trs.tradeId));
8175                    tradeIds.add(tradeId);
8176                }
8177            }
8178        return tradeIds;
8179        }

8373        public static class TradeReportQueryByTimeTest extends BaseTest
8374        {        
8375        private static final int TRADE_BY_TIME_QUERY_MILLIS = 30 * 1000; // 30 seconds
8376        private static final long BASE_TRADE_REPORT_DBID = 1001;
8377        private static final long BASE_TRADE_REPORT_ENTRY_DBID = 2001;
8378        private long endTradeTime;
8379            private long expectedProdKeys[] = {1234, 1235};
8380            private long nonConfigClassKey = 5678;
8381            private long tradeReportDbId = BASE_TRADE_REPORT_DBID;
8382            private long tradeReportEntryDbId = BASE_TRADE_REPORT_ENTRY_DBID;  
8383            private long expectedClassKeys[] = new long[2];
8384 
8385        public TradeReportQueryByTimeTest(String methodName)
8386        {
8387                super(methodName);                
8388        }
8389        
8390        /**
8391         * Prepare a set of test reports as follows. C1 and C2 are
8392         * real class keys configured for local trade server, while NC3 and NC4
8393         * are dummy class-keys not configured for local trade server. Product keys
8394         * P1 and P2 are irrelavant but we just want to keep some variety of 
8395         * product keys. The primary exchange walues E1 and E2 are also for the
8396         * purpose of having a variety of trade reports to ensure that this test of query
8397         * by time retrieves reports for variety of classkeys, productkeys, and
8398         * primary exchnages as long as the time criteria is met and the classkey
8399         * is configured for local trade server. For each combination of classkey
8400         * productkey and exchange, a copy of the report is added that is marked as
8401         * inactive. Note also that relative trade times are noted with base 
8402         * trade time marked as T. The increment in the trade times are in minutes.
8403         * The trade reports are created in order as follows. The tradeids are 
8404         * assigned sequentially.
8405         * 
8406         * TR1: C1, E1, P1, Active, T 
8407         * TR2: C1, E1, P1, Inactive, T+1
8408         * TR3: C1, E1, P2, Active, T+2 
8409         * TR4: C1, E1, P2, Inactive, T+3 
8410         * 
8411         * TR5: C2, E2, P1, Active, T+4
8412         * TR6: C2, E2, P1, Inactive, T+5
8413         * TR7: C2, E2, P2, Active, T+6
8414         * TR8: C2, E2, P2, Inactive, T+7
8415         * 
8416         * TR9: NC1, E1, P1, Active, T+8
8417         * TR10: NC1, E1, P2, Inctive, T+9
8418         * TR11: NC1, E1, P1, Active, T+10
8419         * TR12: NC1, E1, P2, Inactive, T+11
8420         * 
8421         * TR13: NC1, E2, P1, Active, T+12
8422         * TR14: NC1, E2, P2, Inctive, T+13
8423         * TR15: NC1, E2, P1, Active, T+14
8424         * TR16: NC1, E2, P2, Inactive, T+15
8425         * 
8426         * @throws Exception
8427         */
8428        private void prepareTestReportDetail() throws Exception
8429        {
8430                int classCount = 0;
8431                long tradeTime = startTradeTime;
8432                TradingClass[] allClasses = getConfiguredClasses();
8433                String exchList[] = {"NYSE", "NASD"};
8434                
8435                // First add test reports for trading classes configured
8436                // for local trade server.
8437                for (TradingClass tc : allClasses)
8438                {                        
8439                        if (tc.getProductType() != ProductTypes.STRATEGY)
8440                        {
8441                                expectedClassKeys[classCount] = tc.getProductClassKey();
8442                                for (int pk = 0; pk < 2; pk++)
8443                                {
8444                                        // Add one active and one inactive report for 
8445                                        // cobmination of (Class, Exchange)/Product.
8446                                        TestReportDetail aReport = new TestReportDetail();
8447                                        aReport.tradeReportDbId = tradeReportDbId++;
8448                                        aReport.tradeReportEntryDbId = tradeReportEntryDbId++;
8449                                        aReport.classKey = expectedClassKeys[classCount];
8450                                        aReport.primaryExchange = exchList[classCount];                                
8451                                         aReport.productKey = expectedProdKeys[pk];
8452                                         aReport.tradeTime = tradeTime;
8453                                         aReport.active = (byte) 1;
8454                                         testReportDetailList.add(aReport);
8455                                         tradeTime += TRADE_TIME_INTERVAL_MILLIS;
8456                                         
8457                                         TestReportDetail nextReport = aReport.getCopy();
8458                                         nextReport.tradeReportDbId = tradeReportDbId++; 
8459                                         nextReport.tradeReportEntryDbId = tradeReportEntryDbId++;
8460                                         nextReport.active = (byte) 0;
8461                                         nextReport.tradeTime = tradeTime;
8462                                         testReportDetailList.add(nextReport);
8463                                         tradeTime += TRADE_TIME_INTERVAL_MILLIS;
8464                                }
8465                                if (++classCount == 2)
8466                                {
8467                                        break;
8468                                }
8469                        }
8470                }
8471                // Now add the reports for a class not configured for the local trade server
8472                // This is done by adding a copy of the test reports created above 
8473                // except change the classkey to a value that is not
8474                // configured for local trade server.
8475                ArrayList<TestReportDetail> nonConfigCKReports = new ArrayList<TestReportDetail>(); 
8476                for (TestReportDetail aReport : testReportDetailList)
8477                {
8478                        TestReportDetail nextReport = aReport.getCopy();
8479                             nextReport.tradeReportDbId = tradeReportDbId++; 
8480                             nextReport.tradeReportEntryDbId = tradeReportEntryDbId++;
8481                        nextReport.classKey = nonConfigClassKey;
8482                        nonConfigCKReports.add(nextReport);
8483                        tradeTime += TRADE_TIME_INTERVAL_MILLIS;
8484                }
8485                testReportDetailList.addAll(nonConfigCKReports);
8486                endTradeTime = tradeTime;
8487        }
8488

8490        {
8491                prepareTestReportDetail();
8492                insertTestReportsToDatabase();
8493        }

8497                removeTestReportsFromDatabase();
8498        }

8500        public static junit.framework.TestSuite suite()
8501        {
8502           junit.framework.TestSuite suite = new junit.framework.TestSuite();
8503           suite.addTest(new TradeReportQueryByTimeTest("testGetAllActiveTradeReportsByTime"));
8504           return suite;

8507        public static void startTest()
8508        {
8509                junit.textui.TestRunner tr = new junit.textui.TestRunner(System.out);
8510                tr.doRun(suite(), false);
8511        }
8512        
8513        /**
8514         * This test is for the trader report query by time. The query criteria is
8515         * set to retrieve ONLY ACTIVE trade reports between time startTradeTime+1 and 
8516         * endTradeTime-1. From the above list of TRx (x = 1..16), only TR5 and TR9
8517         * are expected.
8518         */
8519        public void testGetAllActiveTradeReportsByTime() throws Exception
8520        {
8521                int expectedReportCount = 3;  
8522                long[] expectedTradeIds = {1003, 1005, 1007};
8523                DateTimeStruct beginTime = DateWrapper.convertToDateTime(startTradeTime + TRADE_BY_TIME_QUERY_MILLIS);
8524                DateTimeStruct endTime = DateWrapper.convertToDateTime(endTradeTime - TRADE_BY_TIME_QUERY_MILLIS);
8525                RelatedTradeReportSummaryStruct[] reports = null;
8526                try 
8527                {
8528                        reports = getTradeMaintenanceService().getTradeReportsByTime(beginTime, endTime, "W_MAIN", true);
8529                }
8530                catch (NotFoundException nfe)
8531                {
8532                        fail("Zero reports were found.");
8533                }
8534                catch (Exception e)
8535                {
8536                        fail("Unexpcted error while querying report. Caught exception: " 
8537                                        + e.getClass().getName() + ". Exception message: " + e.getMessage());
8538                }
8539                // We should have all trade reports except for the one at the begining and one at the end.
8540                assertNotNull("The query returned NULL.", reports);
8541                assertEquals("Actual report count " + reports.length + 
8542                                " does not match expected count " + expectedReportCount, 
8543                                reports.length, expectedReportCount);
8544                for (RelatedTradeReportSummaryStruct rtrss : reports)
8545                {
8546                          TradeReportSummaryStruct[] relatedReports = rtrss.relatedTradeReports;
8547                        // This test case only for simple trades, so there should only be one report
8548                        assertEquals("Expected a single related report. ", 1, relatedReports.length);
8549                        assertEquals("Expected parent report index to be 0", 0, rtrss.parentReportIndex);
8550                        long tradeTime = DateWrapper.convertToMillis(rtrss.relatedTradeReports[0].timeTraded);
8551                        assertTrue("Report from outside query time interval", (tradeTime > startTradeTime) && (tradeTime < endTradeTime));
8552                        long tradeId = CboeId.longValue(rtrss.relatedTradeReports[0].tradeId);
8553                        boolean unexpectedReportFound = false;
8554                        for (long expectTradeId : expectedTradeIds)  
8555                        {
8556                                if (tradeId != expectTradeId) {
8557                                        unexpectedReportFound = true;
8558                                        break;
8559                                }
8560                        }
8561                        assertTrue("Unexpected report with tradeid = " + tradeId + " received.", unexpectedReportFound);                         
8562                }
8563        }
8564        }
8565        
8566    private int getAdjustedMinTradedQty(int theLegProdKey, int reqBustQty, TradeReport tradeReport, int strategyProductKey)
8567    {
8568        int minPkgTradedQty = 0;
8569        Vector childReports = tradeReport.getChildReports();
8570        Map<Integer, Integer> tradedQtys = new HashMap<Integer, Integer>();
8571        if (childReports != null && childReports.size() > 0)
8572        {
8573            TradeReport[] tradeReports = new TradeReport[childReports.size()];
8574            childReports.toArray(tradeReports);
8575            for (TradeReport theTrade : tradeReports)
8576            {
8577                Integer theQty = tradedQtys.get(theTrade.getProduct());
8578                if (theQty == null)
8579                {
8580                    tradedQtys.put(theTrade.getProduct(), theTrade.getQuantity());
8581                }
8582                else
8583                {
8584                    int theProduct = theTrade.getProduct();
8585                    tradedQtys.put(theProduct, tradedQtys.get(theProduct) + theTrade.getQuantity());
8586                }
8587            }
8588        }
8589 
8590        boolean isCrossProduct = isCrossProductStrategy(tradeReport.getProduct());
8591        TradingStrategyLeg[] legs = getStrategyLegs(theLegProdKey, strategyProductKey);
8592        ArrayList<Integer> minPkgTradedQtyForLegs = new ArrayList<Integer>();
8593        for(TradingStrategyLeg leg : legs)
8594        {
8595            int legRatio = leg.getRatioQuantity();
8596            int productKey = leg.getProductKey();
8597            if ( isCrossProduct && isEquityLeg(productKey)) {
8598                continue;
8599            }
8600            if (productKey == theLegProdKey) {                
8601                minPkgTradedQtyForLegs.add((tradedQtys.get(theLegProdKey) - reqBustQty) / legRatio);
8602            }
8603            else {
8604                minPkgTradedQtyForLegs.add(tradedQtys.get(productKey) / legRatio);
8605            }            
8606        }
8607         
8608        minPkgTradedQty = Integer.MAX_VALUE;
8609        for (Integer minPkgTradedQtyForLeg : minPkgTradedQtyForLegs)   {
8610            if (minPkgTradedQtyForLeg < minPkgTradedQty)  {
8611                minPkgTradedQty = minPkgTradedQtyForLeg;
8612            }
8613        }
8614        return minPkgTradedQty;
8615    }

8618    {
8619        TradingProduct strategyProduct = null;
8620        try
8621        {
8622            strategyProduct = getTradingProductHome().findByKey(strategyProductKey);
8623        }
8624        catch(NotFoundException e)
8625        {
8626            Log.exception("TradeServiceImpl>>>Unable to find trading product",e);
8627        }
8628 
8629        return strategyProduct.getStrategyLegs();
8630    }

8641        }

8656    private BustTradeStruct[] getTradesToBustStructs(TradeReport tradeReport, TradeReportStruct theReport, int reqBustQty, boolean isLegQty) 
8657    throws DataValidationException
8658    {
8659        if (reqBustQty == 0) {
8660            Log.debug(this, "No package bust report");
8661            return new BustTradeStruct[0];
8662        }
8663 
8664        Map<Long, Integer> remainingQtyOnAtomicTrades = new HashMap<Long, Integer>();
8665        boolean isExit = false;
8666        try {
8667            AtomicTradeStruct[] parties = theReport.parties;
8668            Vector<BustTradeStruct> bustStructs = new Vector<BustTradeStruct>();
8669            if(parties.length == 1){ // A single atomic trade - no need for looping
8670                AtomicTradeStruct anParty = parties[0];
8671                BustTradeStruct bustStruct = new BustTradeStruct();
8672                bustStruct.atomicTradeId = new CboeIdStruct();
8673                bustStruct.atomicTradeId.highCboeId = anParty.atomicTradeId.highCboeId;
8674                bustStruct.atomicTradeId.lowCboeId = anParty.atomicTradeId.lowCboeId;
8675                bustStruct.bustedQuantity = reqBustQty; 
8676                bustStruct.buyerReinstateRequested = false; 
8677                bustStruct.sellerReinstateRequested = false;
8678                isExit = true;
8679                reqBustQty = 0;
8680                bustStructs.add(bustStruct);
8681            }
8682            if(!isExit){  // more than one atomic trade, will need to distribute the busted quantity
8683                int i = 0;                        
8684                for (AtomicTradeStruct anParty : parties)
8685                {
8686                    long lAtomicTradeId = CboeId.longValue(anParty.atomicTradeId);
8687                    remainingQtyOnAtomicTrades.put(lAtomicTradeId, anParty.quantity);
8688                    BustTradeStruct bustStruct = new BustTradeStruct();
8689                    bustStruct.atomicTradeId = new CboeIdStruct();
8690                    bustStruct.atomicTradeId.highCboeId = anParty.atomicTradeId.highCboeId;
8691                    bustStruct.atomicTradeId.lowCboeId = anParty.atomicTradeId.lowCboeId;
8692                    bustStruct.bustedQuantity = 1; 
8693                    bustStruct.buyerReinstateRequested = false; 
8694                    bustStruct.sellerReinstateRequested = false;
8695                    i++;
8696                    reqBustQty--;
8697                    bustStructs.add(bustStruct);
8698                    if (reqBustQty == 0) {
8699                        isExit = true;
8700                        break;
8701                    }
8702                }
8703            }
8704            if(!isExit){
8705                int maxIterations = reqBustQty;
8706                for(int k = 0; k <  maxIterations; k++)
8707                {
8708                    for (BustTradeStruct theStruct : bustStructs)
8709                    {
8710                        long lAtomicTradeId = CboeId.longValue(theStruct.atomicTradeId);
8711                        Integer remainingQty = remainingQtyOnAtomicTrades.get(lAtomicTradeId);
8712                        if (theStruct.bustedQuantity < remainingQty)
8713                        {
8714                            theStruct.bustedQuantity += 1;
8715                            reqBustQty--;
8716                            if (reqBustQty <= 0) {
8717                                isExit = true;
8718                                break;
8719 
8720                            }
8721                        }
8722                    }
8723                    if(isExit){
8724                        break;
8725                    }
8726                }
8727            }
8728            BustTradeStruct[] bustStructArray = new BustTradeStruct[bustStructs.size()];
8729            bustStructs.toArray(bustStructArray);
8730            return bustStructArray;
8731        }
8732        catch (Exception e)
8733        {
8734            Log.exception(this, "Unable to find child Trade Report for given tradeId = "
8735                    + theReport.tradeId, e);
8736            throw ExceptionBuilder.dataValidationException(
8737                    "Children Trade Report not found for given TradeId", DataValidationCodes.INVALID_ID);                            
8738        }
8739    }

8770    private void persistBulkActionDtl(BulkActionRequest requestDbId,List<TradeBustResponseStruct> tradeBustResponses,
8771            BustTradeStruct[] tradeBustDetail)
8772    {
8773        List<BulkActionDetailWrapper> actionDetailWrappters = new ArrayList<BulkActionDetailWrapper>();
8774        String resultCode = null;
8775        long theTradeId = 0;
8776        for (TradeBustResponseStruct theTradeBustResponse : tradeBustResponses)
8777        {
8778            theTradeId = CboeId.longValue(theTradeBustResponse.tradeId);
8779            for (BustTradeStruct theBustTrade : tradeBustDetail) {
8780                if (theTradeId == CboeId.longValue(theBustTrade.atomicTradeId)) {
8781                    resultCode = theBustTrade.buyerReinstateRequested ? "R" :
8782                        (theBustTrade.sellerReinstateRequested ? "S" : "B");
8783                }
8784            }
8785            actionDetailWrappters.add(new BulkActionDetailWrapper(requestDbId.getRequestDbId(),
8786                    theTradeId, resultCode));
8787        }
8788        FederatedServiceHelper.persistBulkActionDtl(actionDetailWrappters, getBulkActionDtlHome());
8789        
8790        }

8806    public int createNonQTrade(Tradable tradable, TradingProduct aProduct, OrderBook book,
8807            Price expectedEndingTradePrice, boolean isTradableInBook, boolean isTreatedLikeCustomer, boolean p_nonContingency)
8808            throws SpreadProcessingException, DataValidationException, SystemException
8809    {
8810        int allocatedQuantity = 0;
8811        boolean success = false;
8812        boolean tradeHappened = false;
8813 
8814        try
8815        {
8816            Side otherSide = tradable.getSide().getOtherSide();
8817            int quantityToAllocate = tradable.getQuantityAllowed();
8818            boolean nonQOnly = false;
8819 
8820            ArrayList oppositeParticipantLists = new ArrayList();
8821            ArrayList tradePrices = new ArrayList();
8822            ArrayList tradeQuantities = new ArrayList();
8823            // Mutually exclusive flags for nonQ and treatedLikeCustomer
8824            if (!isTreatedLikeCustomer)
8825            {
8826                nonQOnly = true;
8827            }
8828 
8829            int oppositeAllocatedQuantity = createParticipantLists(oppositeParticipantLists,
8830                    tradePrices, tradeQuantities, getPreferredFirmAcronym(tradable),
8831                    getPreferredFirmExchange(tradable), aProduct, book, otherSide,
8832                    expectedEndingTradePrice, quantityToAllocate, nonQOnly, false,
8833                    isTreatedLikeCustomer, tradable, p_nonContingency);
8834            if (oppositeAllocatedQuantity > 0)
8835            {
8836                ArrayList sameParticipantLists = new ArrayList();
8837                int sameSideAllocatedQuantity = createParticipantLists(sameParticipantLists,
8838                        tradePrices, tradeQuantities, tradable, null, oppositeAllocatedQuantity,
8839                        aProduct.getTradingClass());
8840                if (sameSideAllocatedQuantity != oppositeAllocatedQuantity)
8841                {
8842                    allocatedQuantity = 0;
8843                }
8844                else
8845                {
8846                    allocatedQuantity = sameSideAllocatedQuantity;
8847                    Side updatedSide = otherSide;
8848                    Tradable unBookedTradable = isTradableInBook
8849                            ? null
8850                            : tradable;
8851                    if (otherSide.isBuySide() || otherSide.isAsDefinedSide())
8852                    {
8853                        completeTrades(unBookedTradable, oppositeParticipantLists,
8854                                sameParticipantLists, tradePrices, tradeQuantities, book,
8855                                updatedSide);
8856                    }
8857                    else
8858                    {
8859                        completeTrades(unBookedTradable, sameParticipantLists,
8860                                oppositeParticipantLists, tradePrices, tradeQuantities, book,
8861                                updatedSide);
8862                    }
8863                    
8864                    tradeHappened = true;
8865                } // end else
8866            }
8867        }
8868        finally
8869        {
8870            if (tradeHappened)
8871            {
8872                OrderBookPriceDetailUndoLog.clear();
8873            }
8874            else
8875            {
8876                OrderBookPriceDetailUndoLog.undoChange();
8877            }
8878        }
8879        return  allocatedQuantity;
8880    }
